<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="46">三十、&nbsp;<strong>Ajax<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">同步和异步的区别，如何解决跨域问题</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同步的概念应该是来自于</span>OS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中关于同步的概念</span><span style="font-family: Arial">:</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不同进程为协同完成某项工作而在先后次序上调整</span><span style="font-family: Arial">(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过阻塞</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">唤醒等方式</span><span style="font-family: Arial">).</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同步强调的是顺序性</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">谁先谁后</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">异步则不存在这种顺序性</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同步：浏览器访问服务器请求，用户看得到页面刷新，重新发请求</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等请求完，页面刷新，新内容出现，用户看到新内容</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行下</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">步操作。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">异步：浏览器访问服务器请求，用户正常操作，浏览器后端进行请求。等请求完，页面不刷新，新内容也会出现，用户看到新内容。</span></p>
<p>jsonp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">iframe</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window.name</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window.postMessage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、服务器上设置代理页面</span></p>
<p class="46">三十一、&nbsp;<strong>列举几种后端通讯的方法及其使用的场景，关于跨域的理解。</strong></p>
<p>1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后端程序可以通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">session</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来进行通讯，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">session</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有过期时间，主要用于验证码的验证，登录过期等的应用。</span></p>
<p>2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据库，数据库支持多种语言的操作，那么通过数据库就可以通讯。</span></p>
<p>关于跨域：</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">跨域请求存在的原因：由于浏览器的同源策略，即属于不同域的页面之间不能相互访问各自的页面内容。</span></p>
<p><strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">跨域的场景</span></strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </p>
<p>1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">域名不同</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&nbsp;www.yangwei.com </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">www.wuyu.com </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即为不同的域名）</span></p>
<p>2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">二级域名相同，子域名不同（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">www.wuhan.yangwei.com www.shenzheng.yangwei.com </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为子域不同）</span></p>
<p>3.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">端口不同，协议不同</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（ </span><span style="font-family: Arial">http://www.yangwei.com </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">https://www.yangwei.com</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属于跨域</span><span style="font-family: Arial">www.yangwei.con:8888</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">www.yangwei.con:8080)</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">跨域的方式：</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（内容较多，需掌握</span>CORS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">jsonp</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，其他内容也要了解）</span></p>
<p><strong>1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">前端的方式</span></strong>: possMessage<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window.name,document.domain,image.src(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">得不到数据返回</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">jsonP(script.src</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后台不配合得不到数据返回</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">style.href</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（得不到数据返回</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p>一.image.src,script.src,style.href <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不受同源策略的影响可以加载其他域的资源，可以用这个特性，向服务器发送数据。最常用的就是使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">image.src </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">向服务器发送前端的错误信息。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">image.src </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">style.href </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是无法获取服务器的数据返回的，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">script.src </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器端配合可以得到数据返回。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">二</span>possMessage,window.name,document.domain <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是两个窗口直接相互传递数据。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">possMessage </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTML5</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中新增的，使用限制是 必须获得窗口的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">引用。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IE8+</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">firefox</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">chrome,safair,opera</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window.name </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个页面中打开另</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个页面时，</span>window.name <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是共享的，所以可以通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window.name </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来传递数据，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window.name</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的限制大小是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2M</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，这个所有浏览器都支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">且没有什么限制。</span></p>
<p>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">） </span><span style="font-family: Arial">document.domain </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将两个页面的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">document.domain </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置成相同，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">document.domain </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只能设置成父级域名，既可以访问，使用限制：这顶级域名必须相同</span></p>
<p>2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">纯后端方式</span><span style="font-family: Arial">: CORS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，服务器代理</span></p>
<p>CORS <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">w3c</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标准的方式，通过在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">web</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器端设置：响应头</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Access</span>一Cntrol一Alow一Origin <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来指定哪些域可以访问本域的数据，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ie8&amp;9(XDomainRequest),10+,chrom4 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">firefox3.5,safair4</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">opera12</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持这种方式。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器代理，同源策略只存在浏览器端，通过服务器转发请求可以达到跨域请求的目的，劣势：增加服务器的负担，且访问速度慢。</span></p>
<p>3.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">前后端结合</span><span style="font-family: Arial">:JsonP</span></p>
<p>script.src <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不受同源策略的限制，所以可以动态的创建</span><span style="font-family: Arial">script</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签，将要请求数据的域写在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">src </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中参数中附带回调的方法，服务器端返回回调函数的字符串，并带参数。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如</span> script.src="http://www.yangwei.com/?id=001&amp;callback=getInfoCallback",<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器端返回 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">getInfoCallBack("name:yangwei;age:18") </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这段代码会直接执行，在前面定义好</span><span style="font-family: Arial">getInfoCallBack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数，既可以获得数据并解析。 这种是最</span>常<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">见的方式。</span></p>
<p>4.webSocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（了解性拓展）</span></p>
<p><a title="Permanent Link to 服务端推送websocket和sse场景及应用" href="https://www.iflym.com/index.php/java-network/201607040001.html"><strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务端推送</span>websocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">场景及应用</span></strong></a></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用场景</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都可以进行服务端推送</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并且都是使用长连接来进行</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">但两者的实现又有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点不同</span>,sse<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">仍使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并且使用相同的链接发送正常的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议报文</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">websocket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议进行握手</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">然后再使用同</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个链接进行</span>websocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议的通信</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p><strong>websocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以进行双向的通信</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span></strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即服务端可以往客户端发信息</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">客户端也可以向服务端发信息</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是单向的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只能由服务端往客户端发</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p><strong>websocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">自带连接的保持</span></strong>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ping/pong</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议保证连接可以始终维持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">没有这个保证</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不过可以参考</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ping/pong</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">自己周期性地发送信息来同样地进行处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">比如</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,5</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">秒往客户端发</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个特别的信息</span>(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">type/name</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行区分</span><span style="font-family: Arial">).</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">其次</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为是基于浏览器的使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个特性</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是浏览器发现</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个连接断掉了</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就会自动地进行重联</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即重新发送请求</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这样</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务端也不用担心连接被断开</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不过需要处理新的请求必须和上</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次请求的内容相连续</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以及新的推送注册</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为都是使用</span>http<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议进行起始处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因此在签权上都可以使用到</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议本身的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些东西</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">比如</span><span style="font-family: Arial">header/cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">签权</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在相应的握手阶段</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过读取</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie(session)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来保证相应的请求必须是经过授权的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也可以用于定位使用人</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">甚至可以通过这些信息保证单个用户只能有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个请求</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">避免重复请求</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">由于都是基于浏览器使用</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因此建议的数据传输都是文本型</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">虽然</span><span style="font-family: Arial">websocket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持二进制</span><span style="font-family: Arial">frame</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">传输</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不过</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些都不建议使用</span>.sse<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只能传输文本</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不管是</span>websocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在用于通信时</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都建议只用于进行数据的推送</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而不是进行完整的应用处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这里可以理解为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">常规的业务处理仍然交给后端的服务来处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这样</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即可以使用之前的业务开发的优势</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">又可以使用推送的优势</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而不是走向另</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个级端</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即所有的信息都想通过推送来传递</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发方式</span></p>
<p>websocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发首选</span><span style="font-family: Arial">netty,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">netty</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对协议的封装已经做到了完全的支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">HttpServerCodec</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">作为握手协议</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,WebSocketServerProtocolHandler</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">作为协议处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">然后再加</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个自己的</span>handler,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就完成了相应的业务处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同时在性能上</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,netty</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>ws<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的请求建立起来之后</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会自动地去除</span><span style="font-family: Arial">httpServerCodec</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相关的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">handler,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这样保证后续的处理都是按照</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ws</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的协议来进行</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p>sse<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发首选</span><span style="font-family: Arial">jersey,jersey</span>一media一sse<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供了相应的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并且通过与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">rest</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相集成</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>sse<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就跟普通的业务开发相同</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p>ws<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在文本支持上都只支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">utf</span>一8<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">编码</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因此在处理上需要注册编码方式</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同时在使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">时</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果后端第</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次进行响应时</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相应的编码不对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.chrome</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会直接报错</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">包括</span><span style="font-family: Arial">utf8</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都会报错</span><span style="font-family: Arial">(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这是之前后端开发的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个问题</span>),<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以修正或者增加相应的拦截器</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">保证后端</span><span style="font-family: Arial">content</span>一type<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">响应中的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">charset=UTF</span>一8.</p>
<p>ws<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都可以通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">nginx</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行代理转发</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.ws</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的处理只需要设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">版本</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以及重新转发前端的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Upgrade</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Connection</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">头即可</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也可以通过禁用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">buffer</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">http://stackoverflow.com/questions/27898622/server</span>一sent一events一stopped一work一after一enabling一ssl一on一proxy</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">特定实现</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为保证在开发时推送类的和业务类的系统不会耦合在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">起</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者同</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个应用内有两种处理模式的功能存在</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">建议直接在系统层就开发</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个不同的系统</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个专门用于推送</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">另</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个用于相应的业务处理</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">然后业务处理后的数据</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要再交由推送处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">则可以在后端进行通过消息系统进行中转</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如</span><span style="font-family: Arial">kafka(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">持久保证</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或</span><span style="font-family: Arial">redis(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">内存订阅</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为二者在</span>ie<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上的支持都很有限</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因此不建议在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上进行尝试</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span>sse<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">websocket,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">取决于是否需要前台交互</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还取决于对后端的支持技术的了解程序</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">比如</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">了解</span><span style="font-family: Arial">jersey</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">多</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">netty</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">多</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">由于最近</span><span style="font-family: Arial">netty</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行微服务化底层通信支持越来越流行</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个人更倾向于使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">websocket.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">但如果仅仅是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个简单的推送功能</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">又不希望修改代码</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">那也可以使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">jersey(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">毕竟之前的系统就是在上面进行开发的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要后端有的时候需要进行定向发送或者是群发</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这种需求</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ws</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sse</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的实现中都有相应的处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ChannelGroup</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">SseBroadcaster,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这样在后端获取到</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个消息</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要进行路由时就可以从这里面拿相应的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">channel</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">信息</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">前提是对各个</span><span style="font-family: Arial">channel</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上进行了特定的消息绑定</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这样就好区分具体的路由信息</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">具体路由策略可以在建立时绑定</span><span style="font-family: Arial">session,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后续通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">session</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来路由</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p class="46">三十二、&nbsp;<strong>设计一个幻灯应用，需要列举选择的基础框架、项目的基础框架和代码管理、幻灯数据的存储和读取，部分特效的实现，可以只写思路，后续面聊。</strong></p>
<p>本题无标准答案，同学们可以自己研究考虑一下，。</p>
<p class="46">三十三、&nbsp;<strong>H</strong><strong>tml5<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中本地存储概念是什么，有什么优点，与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">有什么区别？</span></strong></p>
<p>html5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Web Storage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">包括了两种存储方式：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sessionStorage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">localStorage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>sessionStorage<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用于本地存储一个会话（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">session</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）中的数据，这些数据只有在同一个会话中的页面才能访问并且当会话结束后数据也随之销毁。因此</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sessionStorage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不是一种持久化的本地存储，仅仅是会话级别的存储。而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">localStorage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用于持久化的本地存储，除非主动删除数据，否则数据是永远不会过期的；</span></p>
<p>cookie<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是网站为了标示用户身份而储存在用户本地终端（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Client Side</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）上的数据（通常经过加密）。</span></p>
<p>区别：</p>
<p class="45">1、&nbsp;cookie<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据始终在同源的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求中携带（即使不需要），即</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在浏览器和服务器间来回传递。而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sessionStorage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">localStorage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不会自动把数据发给服务器，仅在本地保存。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据还有路径（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">path</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）的概念，可以限制</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只属于某个路径下。</span></p>
<p class="45">2、&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">存储大小限制也不同，</span>cookie<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据不能超过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">4k</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，同时因为每次</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求都会携带</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，所以</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只适合保存很小的数据，如会话标识。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">sessionStorage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">localStorage </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">虽然也有存储大小的限制，但比</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">大得多，可以达到</span><span style="font-family: Arial">5M</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或更大。</span></p>
<p class="45">3、&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据有效期不同，</span>sessionStorage<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：仅在当前浏览器窗口关闭前有效，自然也就不可能持久保持；</span><span style="font-family: Arial">localStorage</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：始终有效，窗口或浏览器关闭也一直保存，因此用作持久数据；</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只在设置的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">过期时间之前一直有效，即使窗口或浏览器关闭。</span></p>
<p class="45">4、&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">作用域不同，</span>sessionStorage<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不在不同的浏览器窗口中共享，即使是同一个页面；</span><span style="font-family: Arial">localStorage </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在所有同源窗口中都是共享的；</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也是在所有同源窗口中都是共享的。</span></p>
<p class="46">三十四、&nbsp;<strong>说说你对作用域链的理解</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">作用域链的作用是保证执行环境里有权访问的变量和函数是有序的，作用域链的变量只能向上访问，变量访问到</span>window<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象即被终止，作用域链向下访问变量是不被允许的。</span></p>
<p class="46">三十五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">什么是</span>ajax<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">json</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，它们的优缺点</span></strong></p>
<p>ajax<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的全称：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Asynchronous Javascript And XML</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">异步传输</span>+js+xml<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span>实现无刷新状态更新页面和异步提交</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所谓异步，在这里简单地解释就是：向服务器发送请求的时候，我们不必等待结果，而是可以同时做其他的事情，等到有了结果它自己会根据设定进行后续操作，与此同时，页面是不会发生整页刷新的，提高了用户体验。</span></p>
<p>Ajax<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实现过程：</span></p>
<p>(1)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">创建</span><span style="font-family: Arial">XMLHttpRequest</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也就是创建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个异步调用对象</span></p>
<p>(2)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">创建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个新的</span>HTTP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并指定该</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求的方法、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">及验证信息</span></p>
<p>(3)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置响应</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求状态变化的函数</span></p>
<p>(4)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">发送</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求</span></p>
<p>(5)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">获取异步调用返回的数据</span></p>
<p>(6)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JavaScript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">DOM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实现局部刷新</span></p>
<p>优点：</p>
<p>不需要插件支持</p>
<p>用户体验极佳</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提升</span>Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">程序性能</span></p>
<p>减轻服务器和宽带的负担</p>
<p>缺点：</p>
<p>前进后退按钮被破坏</p>
<p>搜索引擎的支持不够</p>
<p>开发调试工具缺乏</p>
<p>JSON<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>JavaScript Object Notation<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）和</span>XML<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一样也是一种简单文本格式。是一种比较流行的标准格式，是数据的载体，相对于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">XML</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JSON</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">更加易读、更便于肉眼检查。在语法的层面上，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JSON</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与其他格式的区别是在于分隔数据的字符，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JSON</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的分隔符限于单引号、小括号、中括号、大括号、冒号和逗号。</span></p>
<p>优点：</p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">作为一种数据传输格式，</span>JSON <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">XML </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">很相似，但是它更加灵巧。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;JSON<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不需要从服务器端发送含有特定内容类型的首部信息。</span></p>
<p>缺点：</p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">语法过于严谨</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码不易读</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;eval <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数存在风险</span></p>
<p class="46">三十六、&nbsp;<strong>H</strong><strong>tml5<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">有那些新增的表单元素</span></strong></p>
<p class="48"><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">表单控：</span>color<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">calendar</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">date</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">datetime</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>datetime一local，time<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">mouth</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">week</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">email</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">url</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">search</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>range<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>tel</p>
<p class="48">新的表单元素：datalist，keygen，output</p>
<p class="46">三十七、&nbsp;<strong>h1ttp<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">状态码有那些，分别代表什么意思</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">简单版</span>:</p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;100 &nbsp;Continue &nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">继续，一般在发送</span><span style="font-family: Arial">post</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求时，已发送了</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http header</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之后服务端将返回此信息，表示确认，之后发送具体参数信息</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;200 &nbsp;OK &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">正常返回信息</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;201 &nbsp;Created &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求成功并且服务器创建了新的资源</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;202 &nbsp;Accepted &nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器已接受请求，但尚未处理</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;301 &nbsp;Moved Permanently &nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求的网页已永久移动到新位置。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;302 Found &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">临时性重定向。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;303 See Other &nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">临时性重定向，且总是使用 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">GET </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求新的 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">URI</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;304 &nbsp;Not Modified <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">自从上次请求后，请求的网页未修改过。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;400 Bad Request &nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器无法理解请求的格式，客户端不应当尝试再次使用相同的内容发起请求。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;401 Unauthorized <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求未授权。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;403 Forbidden &nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">禁止访问。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;404 Not Found &nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">找不到如何与 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">URI </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相匹配的资源。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;500 Internal Server Error &nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">最常见的服务器端错误。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;503 Service Unavailable <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器端暂时无法处理请求（可能是过载或维护）。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">完整版</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;1**(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">信息类</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：表示接收到请求并且继续处理</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;100<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——客户必须继续发出请求</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;101<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——客户要求服务器根据请求转换</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议版本</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;2**(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">响应成功</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：表示动作被成功接收、理解和接受</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;200<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——表明该请求被成功地完成，所请求的资源发送回客户端</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;201<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——提示知道新文件的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;202<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——接受和处理、但处理未完成</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;203<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——返回信息不确定或不完整</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;204<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求收到，但返回信息为空</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;205<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——服务器完成了请求，用户代理必须复位当前已经浏览过的文件</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;206<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——服务器已经完成了部分用户的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">GET</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;3**(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">重定向类</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：为了完成指定的动作，必须接受进一步处理</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;300<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求的资源可在多处得到</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;301<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——本网页被永久性转移到另一个</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;302<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求的网页被转移到一个新的地址，但客户访问仍继续通过原始</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">地址，重定向，新的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">response</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Location</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中返回，浏览器将会使用新的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">发出新的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Request</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;303<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——建议客户访问其他</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或访问方式</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;304<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——自从上次请求后，请求的网页未修改过，服务器返回此响应时，不会返回网页内容，代表上次的文档已经被缓存了，还可以继续使用</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;305<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求的资源必须从服务器指定的地址得到</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;306<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——前一版本</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中使用的代码，现行版本中不再使用</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;307<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——申明请求的资源临时性删除</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;4**(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">客户端错误类</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：请求包含错误语法或不能正确执行</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;400<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——客户端请求有语法错误，不能被服务器所理解</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;401<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求未经授权，这个状态代码必须和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">WWW</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Authenticate</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">报头域一起使用</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;HTTP 401.1 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 未授权：登录失败</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 401.2 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 未授权：服务器配置问题导致登录失败</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 401.3 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">ACL </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">禁止访问资源</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 401.4 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 未授权：授权被筛选器拒绝</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;HTTP 401.5 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 未授权：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ISAPI </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">CGI </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">授权失败</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;402<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——保留有效</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ChargeTo</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">头响应</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;403<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——禁止访问，服务器收到请求，但是拒绝提供服务</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;HTTP 403.1 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">禁止访问：禁止可执行访问</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.2 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：禁止读访问</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.3 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：禁止写访问</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.4 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：要求 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">SSL</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.5 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：要求 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">SSL 128</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.6 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IP </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">地址被拒绝</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.7 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：要求客户证书</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.8 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：禁止站点访问</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.9 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：连接的用户过多</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.10 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：配置无效</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.11 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：密码更改</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.12 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：映射器拒绝访问</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.13 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：客户证书已被吊销</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.15 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：客户访问许可过多</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 403.16 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：客户证书不可信或者无效</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;HTTP 403.17 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 禁止访问：客户证书已经到期或者尚未生效</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;404<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——一个</span><span style="font-family: Arial">404</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">错误表明可连接服务器，但服务器无法取得所请求的网页，请求资源不存在。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">eg</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：输入了错误的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;405<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——用户在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Request</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Line</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">字段定义的方法不允许</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;406<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——根据用户发送的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Accept</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">拖，请求资源不可访问</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;407<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——类似</span><span style="font-family: Arial">401</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，用户必须首先在代理服务器上得到授权</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;408<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——客户端没有在用户指定的饿时间内完成请求</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;409<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——对当前资源状态，请求不能完成</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;410<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——服务器上不再有此资源且无进一步的参考地址</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;411<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——服务器拒绝用户定义的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Content</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Length</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性请求</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;412<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——一个或多个请求头字段在当前请求中错误</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;413<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求的资源大于服务器允许的大小</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;414<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求的资源</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">长于服务器允许的长度</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;415<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求资源不支持请求项目格式</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;416<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——请求中包含</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Range</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求头字段，在当前请求资源范围内没有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">range</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">指示值，请求也不包含</span><span style="font-family: Arial">If</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Range</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求头字段</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;417<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">——服务器不满足请求</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Expect</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">头字段指定的期望值，如果是代理服务器，可能是下一级服务器不能满足请求长。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;5**(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务端错误类</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：服务器不能正确执行一个正确的请求</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;HTTP 500 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 服务器遇到错误，无法完成请求</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 500.100 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 内部服务器错误 一 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">ASP </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">错误</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 500<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">11 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器关闭</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 500<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">12 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用程序重新启动</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 500<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">13 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 服务器太忙</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 500<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">14 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 应用程序无效</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>HTTP 500<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">15 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 不允许请求 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">global.asa</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　</span>Error 501 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 未实现</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;HTTP 502 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 网关错误</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;HTTP 503<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：由于超载或停机维护，服务器目前无法使用，一段时间后可能恢复正常</span></p>
<p class="46">三十八、&nbsp;<strong>HTTP<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的请求方法</span></strong></p>
<p>HTTP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Hypertext Transfer Protocol</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）的八种请求方法：</span></p>
<table>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center"><strong>方法</strong></p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p align="center"><strong>概述</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center"><strong>❤</strong><strong>GET</strong></p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p>请求页面的详细信息，并返回实体主体。</p>

</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center"><strong>❤</strong><strong>POST</strong></p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p>向指定资源提交数据进行数据请求（例如提交表单，或者上传文件）。数据被包含在请求体中。POST请求可能会导致新的资源的建立和/或已有资源的修改。</p>

</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center"><strong>PUT</strong></p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p>从客户端向服务器传送的数据取代指定的文档内容。</p>

</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center">DELETE</p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p>请服务器删除指定的页面。</p>

</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center">HEAD</p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p>类似与Get请求，只不过返回的响应中没有具体的内容，用于获取报头</p>

</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center">CONNECT</p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p>HTTP/1.1协议中预留给能够将连接改为管道方式的代理服务器。</p>

</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center">OPTIONS</p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p>允许客户端查看服务器的性能。</p>

</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="92">
<p align="center">TRACE</p>

</td>
<td valign="top" width="544">
<p>回显服务器收到的请求，主要用于测试或诊断。</p>

</td>

</tr>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="46">三十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">什么是闭包（</span>closure<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">）为什么要用它</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">闭包是指有权访问另一个函数作用域中变量的函数，创建闭包的最常见的方式就是在一个函数内创建另一个函数，通过另一个函数访问这个函数的局部变量</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">利用闭包可以突破作用链域，将函数内部的变量和方法传递到外部。</span></p>
<p>闭包的特性：</p>
<p>1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数内再嵌套函数</span></p>
<p>2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">内部函数可以引用外层的参数和变量</span></p>
<p>3.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参数和变量不会被垃圾回收机制回收</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">例如：</span>//li<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节点的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">onclick</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件都能正确的弹出当前被点击的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">li</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">索引</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="604">
<p><strong>&lt;ul id="testUL"&gt;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;li&gt; index = 0&lt;/li&gt;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;li&gt; index = 1&lt;/li&gt;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;li&gt; index = 2&lt;/li&gt;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;li&gt; index = 3&lt;/li&gt;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&lt;/ul&gt;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&lt;script type="text/javascript"&gt;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var nodes = document.getElementsByTagName("li");</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for(i = 0;i&lt;nodes.length;i+= 1){</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;nodes[i].onclick = (function(i){</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return function() {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;console.log(i);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不用闭包的话，值每次都是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">4</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;})(i);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&lt;/script&gt;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">执行</span>say667()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,say667()</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">闭包内部变量会存在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而闭包内部函数的内部变量不会存在</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使得</span>Javascript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的垃圾回收机制</span><span style="font-family: Arial">GC</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不会收回</span><span style="font-family: Arial">say667()</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所占用的资源</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为</span>say667()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的内部函数的执行需要依赖</span><span style="font-family: Arial">say667()</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的变量</span></p>
<p>这是对闭包作用的非常直白的描述</p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="633">
<p><strong>function say667() {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;// Local variable that ends up within closure</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var num = 666;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var sayAlert = function() {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;alert(num);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;num++;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return sayAlert;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;var sayAlert = say667();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;sayAlert()//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">执行结果应该弹出的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">667</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">你知道哪些针对</span>jQuery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的优化方法</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">基于</span>Class<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的选择性的性能相对于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Id</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">选择器开销很大，因为需遍历所有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">DOM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">元素。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">频繁操作的</span>DOM<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，先缓存起来再操作。用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Jquery</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的链式调用更好。</span></p>
<p>	&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">比如：</span>var str=$("a").attr("href");</p>
<p>for (var i = size; i &lt; arr.length; i++) {}</p>
<p>	&nbsp;for <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">循环每一次循环都查找了数组 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">(arr) </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.length </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性，在开始循环的时候设置一个变量来存储这个数字，可以让循环跑得更快：</span></p>
<p>	&nbsp;for (var i = size, length = arr.length; i &lt; length; i++) {}</p>
<p class="46">四十、&nbsp;<strong>用原型链继承的方式写一个类和子类</strong></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="633">

<p class="46">四十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">简单概括浏览器事件模型，如何获得资源</span>dom<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">节点</span></strong></p>
<p>在各种浏览器中存在三种事件模型:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原始事件模型</span><span style="font-family: Arial">( original event model),DOM2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件模型</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,IE</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件模型</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">其中原始的事件模型被所有浏览器所支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">DOM2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中所定义的事件模型目前被除了</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IE</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以外的所有主流浏览器支持。</span></p>
<p>浏览器事件模型分为三个阶段</p>
<p>	1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、捕获阶段</span></p>
<p>	2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、目标阶段</span></p>
<p>	3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、冒泡阶段</span></p>
<p>Dom<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节点获取方法：</span></p>
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>id<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性获取 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">document.getElementById()</span></p>
<p>2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>name<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性获取 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">document.getElementsByName()</span></p>
<p>3．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过标签名获取</span> document.getElementsByTagName()</p>
<p>4．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>class<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性获取 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">document.getElementsByClassName()</span></p>
<p>5．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原生</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">querySelector </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">querySelectorAll</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法也同样可以获取到相应的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">dom</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节点，相似于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">jquery</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，但比</span><span style="font-family: Arial">jq</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">更快</span></p>
<p class="46">四十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">写一段</span>ajax<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">提交的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">代码</span></strong></p>

<p class="46">四十六、&nbsp;<strong>css<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">引入的方式有哪些，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">link</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">@import</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的区别是什么</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有四种形式</span>:</p>
<p>1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">链入外部样式表</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是把样式表保存为一个样式表文件</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">然后在页面中用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" href="*.css"&gt;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">链接这个样式表文件</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p>2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">内部样式表</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是把样式表放到页面的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;head&gt;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">区里</span><span style="font-family: Arial">. &lt;style type="text/css"&gt;</span></p>
<p>div&nbsp;{height: 600px;}</p>
<p>&lt;/style&gt;</p>
<p>3.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">导入外部样式表</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">@import,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;head&gt;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;/head&gt;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之间，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;style type="text/css"&gt;</span></p>
<p>&lt;!一一</p>
<p>@import "*.css"</p>
<p>一一&gt;</p>
<p>&lt;/style&gt;</p>
<p>4.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">内嵌样式</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是在标签内写入</span><span style="font-family: Arial">style="",</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">比如</span><span style="font-family: Arial">:</span></p>
<p>&lt;div style="background:#cccccc"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">div</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">背景色为灰色</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p>区别：</p>
<p>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">. link</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">XHTML</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签，除了加载</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">外，还可以定义</span><span style="font-family: Arial">RSS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等其他事务；</span><span style="font-family: Arial">@import</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">范畴，只能加载</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">. link</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">引用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">时，在页面载入时同时加载；</span><span style="font-family: Arial">@import</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要页面网页完全载入以后加载。</span></p>
<p>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">. link</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">XHTML</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签，无兼容问题；</span><span style="font-family: Arial">@import</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS2.1</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提出的，低版本的浏览器不支持。</span></p>
<p>4<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">. link</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Javascript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">控制</span><span style="font-family: Arial">DOM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">去改变样式；而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">@import</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不支持。</span></p>
<p class="46">四十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">将字符串</span>helloChina<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">反转输出</span></strong></p>

<p class="46">四十八、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">为什么无法定义</span>1px<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">左右高度的容器</span></strong></p>
<p>IE6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下这个问题是因为默认的行高造成的，解决的方法也有很多，例如：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">overflow:hidden | zoom:0.08 | line</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">height:1px</span></p>

<p class="46">五十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">请写出</span>XHTML<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">css</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何注释</span></strong></p>
