<p class="46">五十一、&nbsp;<strong>现在想调节一下父元素的透明度，但是又不影响子元素的透明度，怎么破？</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法</span>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">RGBA</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：再加一层与父元素同级的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">div</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">装载子元素 定位到子元素原位置</span></p>
<p class="46">五十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">简述</span>ECMASCRIPT6<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的新特性</span></strong></p>
<p>1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增加块作用域</span></p>
<p>2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增加</span><span style="font-family: Arial">let const</span></p>
<p>3.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解构赋值</span></p>
<p>4.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数参数扩展 （函数参数可以使用默认值、不定参数以及拓展参数）</span></p>
<p>5.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增加</span><span style="font-family: Arial">class</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">类的支持</span></p>
<p>6.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增加箭头函数</span></p>
<p>7.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增加模块和模块加载（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ES6</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中开始支持原生模块化啦）</span></p>
<p>8.math, number, string, array, object<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增加新的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">API</span></p>
<p class="46">五十三、&nbsp;<strong>A</strong><strong>pply<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">call</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">方法的异同</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相同点</span>:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">两个方法产生的作用是完全一样的，第一个参数都是对象；</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不同点</span>:</p>
<p>call()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法参数将依次传递给借用的方法作参数，即</span><span style="font-family: Arial">fn.call(thisobj, arg1,arg2,arg3...argn)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">n</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个参数</span></p>
<p>apply()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法第一个参数是对象，第二个参数是数组</span><span style="font-family: Arial">fn.apply(thisobj,arg)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，此处的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">arg</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是一个数组</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只有两个参数</span></p>
<p class="46">五十四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">在</span>javascript<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中什么是伪数组，如何将伪数组转化为标准数组</span></strong></p>
<p>这里把符合以下条件的对象称为伪数组：</p>
<p>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，具有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">length</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性</span></p>
<p>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，按索引方式存储数据</span></p>
<p>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，不具有数组的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">push,pop</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等方法</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">伪数组（类数组）：无法直接调用数组方法或期望</span>length<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性有什么特殊的行为，不具有数组的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">push,pop</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等方法，但仍可以对真正数组遍历方法来遍历它们。典型的是函数的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">argument</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参数，还有像调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">document.getElementsByTagName, document.childNodes</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之类的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">它们返回的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">NodeList</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象都属于伪数组。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以使用以下函数将伪数组转化为真正的</span>Array<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象（兼容问题处理）。</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>
<p><strong>function &nbsp;makeArray(c) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;try{</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</strong><strong>return Array.prototype.slice.call(c);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}catch(e){</strong></p>
<p><strong>var ret = [],i, len = c.length;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for(i = 0; i &lt; len; i++) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;ret[i] = (c[i]);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return ret;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="46">五十五、&nbsp;<strong>J</strong><strong>s<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">native</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">交互的方法与问题</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实现</span>JS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Native</span>交互<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有两种方式</span>:</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">第</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种：</span>shouldOverrideUrlLoading(WebView view, String url<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过给</span>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个事件监听对象（</span>WebViewClient)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并重写</span><span style="font-family: Arial">shouldOverrideUrlLoading(WebView view, String url</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）方法。当按下某个连接时</span><span style="font-family: Arial">WebViewClient</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会调用这个方法，并传递参数</span><span style="font-family: Arial">view</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">url</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">第二种：</span>JS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Java</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">互调</span></p>
<p>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开启</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JavaScript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">脚本执行</span></p>
<p>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置供</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JavaScript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用的交互接口</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">客户端和网页端编写调用对方的代码</span></p>
<p>JS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JAVA</span>	</p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>JS : window.jsInterfaceName.methodName(parameterValues)</strong></p>
<p><strong>native: webView.addJavascriptInterface(new JsInteration(), “androidNative”);</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p>Java<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JS</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>webView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的基本格式为：</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>webView.loadUrl(“javascript:methodName(parameterValues)”)</strong></p>
<p><strong>调用<span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">无参无返回值函数： </span></strong></p>
<p><strong>String call =<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">“</span><span style="font-family: Arial">javascript:sayHello()</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">；</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webView.loadUrl(call);</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>调用<span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有参无返回值函数：</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>String call = “javascript:alertMessage(\”” + “content” + “\”)”; </strong></p>
<p><strong>webView.loadUrl(call);</strong></p>
<p><strong>调用<span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有参数有返回值的函数</span></strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p>Android<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">4.4</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之前并没有提供直接调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数并获取值的方法，所以在此之前，常用的思路是 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">java</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法执行完毕，再次调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">java</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码将值返回。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Android 4.4</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之后使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">evaluateJavascript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即可。</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>private void testEvaluateJavascript(WebView webView) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;webView.evaluateJavascript("getGreetings()", new ValueCallback&lt;String&gt;() {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;@Override</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;public void onReceiveValue(String value) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Log.i(LOGTAG, "onReceiveValue value=" + value);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;}});</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">注</span>:</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参数类型如果是简单的</span>int<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或</span><span style="font-family: Arial">String</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，可以直接传，对于复杂的数据类型，建议以字符串形式的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">json</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回。</span></p>
<p>evaluateJavascript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法必须在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">UI</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">线程（主线程）调用，因此</span><span style="font-family: Arial">onReceiveValue</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也执行在主线程。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当</span>native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">交互时存</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">看到很多人遇到过这样</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个问题</span>,cookie<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">存不进去</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">网上有很多解释方案</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">但是很多没说到重点上</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这里直接贴</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下代码</span>:</p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="633">
<p><strong>public static void synCookies(Context context, String url, String version) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CookieSyncManager.createInstance(context);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CookieManager cookieManager = CookieManager.getInstance();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cookieManager.setAcceptCookie(true);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cookieManager.removeAllCookie();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cookieManager.setCookie(url, "sessionKey="+UserInfoShareprefrence.getInstance(context).getLocalSessionKey())</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;cookieManager.setCookie(url, "productVersion=android<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">epocket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">v" + version);</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;CookieSyncManager.getInstance().sync();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">存不进去的很大</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">部分原因是你的</span>url<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不对 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这里的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">url</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是显示的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">url</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的域名</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这里顺便贴出取域名的方法</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">给出的是通过正则提取域名</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>&nbsp;/**</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">获得域名</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* @param url</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;* @return</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;*/</strong></p>
<p><strong>public static String getDomain(String url) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Pattern p = Pattern.compile("[^//]*?\\.(com|cn|net|org|biz|info|cc|tv)", Pattern.CASE_INSENSITIVE);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Matcher matcher = p.matcher(url);</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;matcher.find();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return matcher.group();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点就是</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果你想传递多个值给</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的话</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以多次使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">setCookie,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不要擅自的自己拼值</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为你拼的字符串中可能存在分号</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">内部多分号做了特殊处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">截取分号之前的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之后的直接放弃</span><span style="font-family: Arial">!</span></p>
<p class="46">五十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">用</span>sass<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">minix</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">定义一些代码片段，且可传参数</span></strong></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>/**</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;* @module <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">功能</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;* @description <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">生成全屏方法</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;* @method fullscreen</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;* @version 1.7.0</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;* @param {Integer} $z<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">指定层叠级别 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;1.7.0&gt;</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;* @param {Keywords} $position <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">指定定位方式，取除</span><span style="font-family: Arial">`static | relative`</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之外的值，默认值：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">absolute &lt;1.8.5&gt;</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;*/</strong></p>
<p><strong>@mixin fullscreen($z<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index: null, $position: absolute) {</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;position: $position;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;z<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index: $z</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index;</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;top: 0;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;right: 0;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;bottom: 0;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;left: 0;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="46">五十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">移动端经常出现的兼容问题，谈谈移动端应用或者</span>wap<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">站的一些优化技巧和心得</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">1、&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">安卓浏览器看背景图片，有些设备会模糊。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为手机分辨率太小，如果按照分辨率来显示网页，字会非常小，安卓手机</span>devicePixelRatio<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">比较乱，有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1.5</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的，有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的也有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">3</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的。想让图片在手机里显示更为清晰，必须使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2x</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的背景图来代替</span><span style="font-family: Arial">img</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签（</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般情况都是用</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">倍），或者指定 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">background</span>一size:contain;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都可以</span></p>
<p class="45">2、&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">防止手机中网页放大和缩小</span></p>
<p>	&lt;meta name="viewport" content="width=device一width,&nbsp;initial一scale=1.0,&nbsp;maximum一scale=1.0,user一scalable=0" /&gt;</p>
<p class="45">3、&nbsp;apple一mobile一web一app一capable<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Web</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用是否以全屏模式运行。</span></p>
<p>	&lt;meta name="apple一mobile一web一app一capable" content="yes"&gt;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果</span><span style="font-family: Arial">content</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">yes</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Web</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用会以全屏模式运行，反之，则不会。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">content</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的默认值是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">no</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，表示正常显示</span><span style="font-family: Arial">;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也可以通过只读属性</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window.navigator.standalone</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来确定网页是否以全屏模式显示。</span></p>
<ol>
<li>format一detection <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">启动或禁用自动识别页面中的电话号码。</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">语法：</span>&lt;meta name="format一detection" content="telephone=no"&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">默认情况下，设备会自动识别任何可能是电话号码的字符串。设置</span>telephone=no<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以禁用这项功能。</span></p>
<ol>
<li>html5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用安卓或者</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ios</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的拨号功能</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	html5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供了自动调用拨号的标签，只要在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">href</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中添加</span><span style="font-family: Arial">tel:</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就可以了。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如下：</span>&lt;a href="tel:4008106999,1034"&gt;400一810一6999 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">转 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">1034&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">拨打手机</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">号</span> &nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如下</span>&lt;a href="tel:15677776767"&gt;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点击拨打</span><span style="font-family: Arial">15677776767&lt;/a&gt;</span></p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上下拉动滚动条时卡顿、慢</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	body {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一overflow一scrolling: touch;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;overflow一scrolling: touch;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<p>	Android3+<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">iOS5+</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS3</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的新属性为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">overflow</span>一scrolling</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">禁止复制、选中文本</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	Element {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一user一select: none;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一moz一user一select: none;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一khtml一user一select: none;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;user一select: none;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决移动设备可选中页面文本</span>(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">视产品需要而定</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">长时间按住页面出现闪退</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	element {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一touch一callout: none;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<ol>
<li>iphone<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">及</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ipad</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下输入框默认内阴影</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	Element{</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一appearance: none; </p>
<p>	}</p>
<ol>
<li>ios<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">android</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下触摸元素时出现半透明灰色遮罩</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	Element {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一tap一highlight一color:rgba(255,255,255,0)</p>
<p>	}</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span>alpha<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">值为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">0</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就可以去除半透明灰色遮罩，备注：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">transparent</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的属性值在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">android</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下无效。详细介绍参照（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http://www.jb51.net/post/phone_web_ysk</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<ol>
<li>active<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">兼容处理 即 伪类 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">:active </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">失效</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span>body<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">添加</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ontouchstart</span></p>
<p>		&lt;body ontouchstart=""&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法二：</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">给 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">document </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">绑定 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">touchstart </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">touchend </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件</span></p>
<p>		&lt;style&gt;</p>
<p>		a {</p>
<p>		&nbsp;color: #000;</p>
<p>		}</p>
<p>		a:active {</p>
<p>		&nbsp;color: #fff;</p>
<p>		}</p>
<p>		&lt;/style&gt;</p>
<p>		&lt;a herf=foo &gt;bar&lt;/a&gt;</p>
<p>		&lt;script&gt;</p>
<p>		&nbsp;document.addEventListener('touchstart',function(){},false);</p>
<p>		&lt;/script&gt;</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">动画定义</span>3D<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">启用硬件加速</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	Element {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一transform:translate3d(0, 0, 0)</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);</p>
<p>	}</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">注意：</span>3D<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">变形会消耗更多的内存与功耗</span></p>
<ol>
<li>Retina<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">屏的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">边框</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	Element{</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;border一width: thin;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<ol>
<li>webkit mask <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">兼容处理</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">某些低端手机不支持</span>css3 mask<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，可以选择性的降级处理。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">比如可以使用</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">判断来引用不同</span><span style="font-family: Arial">class</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span></p>
<p>	if( 'WebkitMask' in document.documentElement.style){</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;alert('<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">mask');</span></p>
<p>	} else {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;alert('<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">mask');</span></p>
<p>	}</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">旋转屏幕时，字体大小调整的问题</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	html, body, form, fieldset, p, div, h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6 {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一text一size一adjust:100%;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<ol>
<li>transition<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">闪屏</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	/<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置内嵌的元素在 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">3D </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">空间如何呈现：保留</span><span style="font-family: Arial">3D /</span></p>
<p>	一webkit一transform一style: preserve一3d;</p>
<p>	/ <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置进行转换的元素的背面在面对用户时是否可见：隐藏 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">/</span></p>
<p>	一webkit一backface一visibility:hidden;</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">圆角</span>bug</li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">某些</span>Android<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">手机圆角失效 &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: Arial">background</span>一clip: padding一box;</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">顶部状态栏背景色</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	&lt;meta name="apple一mobile一web一app一status一bar一style" content="black" /&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">说明：</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">除非你先使用</span>apple一mobile一web一app一capable<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">指定全屏模式，否则这个</span><span style="font-family: Arial">meta</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签不会起任何作用。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果</span>content<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">default</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，则状态栏正常显示。如果设置为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">blank</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，则状态栏会有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个黑色的背景。如果设置为</span>blank一translucent<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，则状态栏显示为黑色半透明。如果设置为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">default</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或</span><span style="font-family: Arial">blank</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，则页面显示在状态栏的下方，即状态栏占据上方部分，页面占据下方部分，二者没有遮挡对方或被遮挡。如果设置为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">blank</span>一translucent<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，则页面会充满屏幕，其中页面顶部会被状态栏遮盖住（会覆盖页面</span><span style="font-family: Arial">20px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">高度，而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">iphone4</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">itouch4</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Retina</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">屏幕为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">40px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）。默认值是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">default</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置缓存</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	&lt;meta http一equiv="Cache一Control" content="no一cache" /&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">手机页面通常在第</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次加载后会进行缓存，然后每次刷新会使用缓存而不是去重新向服务器发送请求。如果不希望使用缓存可以设置</span>no一cache<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">桌面图标</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	&lt;link rel="apple一touch一icon" href="touch一icon一iphone.png" /&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link rel="apple一touch一icon" sizes="76x76" href="touch一icon一ipad.png" /&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link rel="apple一touch一icon" sizes="120x120" href="touch一icon一iphone一retina.png" /&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link rel="apple一touch一icon" sizes="152x152" href="touch一icon一ipad一retina.png" /&gt;</p>
<p>	iOS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下针对不同设备定义不同的桌面图标。</span></p>
<p>	&lt;link rel="apple一touch一icon一precomposed" href="touch一icon一iphone.png" /&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">图片尺寸可以设定为</span>5757<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）或者</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Retina</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以定为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">114114</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">），</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ipad</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">尺寸为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">72*72</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">px)</span></p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">启动画面</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	&lt;link rel="apple一touch一startup一image" href="start.png"/&gt;</p>
<p>	iOS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下页面启动加载时显示的画面图片，避免加载时的白屏。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以通过</span>madia<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来指定不同的大小：</span></p>
<p>	&lt;!一一iPhone一一&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link href="apple一touch一startup一image一320x460.png" media="(device一width: 320px)" rel="apple一touch一startup一image" /&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;!一一&nbsp;iPhone Retina 一一&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link href="apple一touch一startup一image一640x920.png" media="(device一width: 320px) and (一webkit一device一pixel一ratio: 2)" rel="apple一touch一startup一image" /&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;!一一&nbsp;iPhone 5 一一&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link rel="apple一touch一startup一image" media="(device一width: 320px) and (device一height: 568px) and (一webkit一device一pixel一ratio: 2)" href="apple一touch一startup一image一640x1096.png"&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;!一一&nbsp;iPad portrait 一一&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link href="apple一touch一startup一image一768x1004.png" media="(device一width: 768px) and (orientation: portrait)" rel="apple一touch一startup一image" /&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;!一一&nbsp;iPad landscape 一一&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link href="apple一touch一startup一image一748x1024.png" media="(device一width: 768px) and (orientation: landscape)" rel="apple一touch一startup一image" /&gt; </p>
<p>	&lt;!一一&nbsp;iPad Retina portrait 一一&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link href="apple一touch一startup一image一1536x2008.png" media="(device一width: 1536px) and (orientation: portrait) and (一webkit一device一pixel一ratio: 2)" rel="apple一touch一startup一image" /&gt; </p>
<p>	&lt;!一一&nbsp;iPad Retina landscape 一一&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;link href="apple一touch一startup一image一1496x2048.png"media="(device一width: 1536px) and (orientation: landscape) and (一webkit一device一pixel一ratio: 2)"rel="apple一touch一startup一image" /&gt;</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器私有及其它</span>meta</li>

</ol>
<p>	QQ<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器私有</span></p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">全屏模式</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="x5一fullscreen" content="true"&gt;</p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">强制竖屏</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="x5一orientation" content="portrait"&gt;</p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">强制横屏</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="x5一orientation" content="landscape"&gt;</p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用模式</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="x5一page一mode" content="app"&gt;</p>
<p>	UC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器私有</span></p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">全屏模式</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="full一screen" content="yes"&gt;</p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">强制竖屏</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="screen一orientation" content="portrait"&gt;</p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">强制横屏</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="screen一orientation" content="landscape"&gt;</p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用模式</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="browsermode" content="application"&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">其它</span>(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">针对手持设备优化，主要是针对</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些老的不识别</span>viewport<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的浏览器，比如黑莓</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="HandheldFriendly" content="true"&gt;</p>
<p>		<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">微软的老式浏览器</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="MobileOptimized" content="320"&gt;</p>
<p>		windows phone <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点击无高光</span></p>
<p>		&lt;meta name="msapplication一tap一highlight" content="no"&gt;</p>
<ol>
<li>IOS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中</span><span style="font-family: Arial">input</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">键盘事件</span><span style="font-family: Arial">keyup</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">keydown</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">keypress</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持不是很好</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用</span>input search<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">做模糊搜索的时候，在键盘里面输入关键词，会通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ajax</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后台查询，然后返回数据，然后再对返回的数据进行关键词标红。用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">input</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">监听键盘</span><span style="font-family: Arial">keyup</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件，在安卓手机浏览器中是可以的，但是在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ios</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">手机浏览器中变红很慢，用输入法输入之后，并未立刻响应</span><span style="font-family: Arial">keyup</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件，只有在通过删除之后才能响应！</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决办法：</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以用</span>html5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">oninput</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件去代替</span><span style="font-family: Arial">keyup</span></p>
<p>	&lt;input type="text" id="testInput"&gt;</p>
<p>	&lt;script type="text/javascript"&gt;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;document.getElementById('testInput').addEventListener('input', function(e){</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var value = e.target.value;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;});</p>
<p>	&lt;/script&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">然后就达到类似</span>keyup<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的效果！</span></p>
<ol>
<li>h5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">网站</span><span style="font-family: Arial">input </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">type=number</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的问题</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般会产生三个问题，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个问题是</span>maxlength<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性不好用了。另外</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个是</span>form<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提交的时候，默认给取整了。三是部分安卓手机出现样式问题。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">问题</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决，用</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如下</span></p>
<p>	&lt;input type="number" oninput="checkTextLength(this ,10)"&gt; </p>
<p>	function checkTextLength(obj, length) { &nbsp;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if(obj.value.length &gt; length) &nbsp;{ &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;obj.value = obj.value.substr(0, length); &nbsp;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} &nbsp;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">问题二，是因为</span>form<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提交默认做了表单验证，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">step</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">默认是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">要设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">step</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性，假如保留</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">位小数，写法如下：</span></p>
<p>	&lt;input type="number" step="0.01" /&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">关于</span>step<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">input </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中</span><span style="font-family: Arial">type=number</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般会自动生成</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个上下箭头，点击上箭头默认增加</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>step<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，点击下箭头默认会减少</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>step<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">number</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中默认</span><span style="font-family: Arial">step</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。也就是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">step=0.01,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以允许输入</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">位小数，并且点击上下箭头分别增加</span><span style="font-family: Arial">0.01</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和减少</span><span style="font-family: Arial">0.01</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">假如</span>step<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">min</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">起使用，那么数值必须在</span>min<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">max</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之间。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">问题三，去除</span>input<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">默认样式</span></p>
<p>	input[type=number] {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一moz一appearance:textfield;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<p>	input[type=number]::一webkit一inner一spin一button,</p>
<p>	input[type=number]::一webkit一outer一spin一button {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一appearance: none;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;margin: 0;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<ol>
<li>ios <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">input </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">按钮样式会被默认样式覆盖</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决方式如下：</span></p>
<p>	input,</p>
<p>	textarea {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;border: 0; </p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;一webkit一appearance: none; </p>
<p>	}</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置默认样式为</span>none</p>
<ol>
<li>IOS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">键盘字母输入，默认首字母大写</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决方案，设置如下属性</span></p>
<p>	&lt;input type="text" autocapitalize="off" /&gt;</p>
<ol>
<li>select <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下拉选择设置右对齐</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置如下：</span></p>
<p>	select option {</p>
<p>	direction: rtl;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>transform<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行</span><span style="font-family: Arial">skew</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">变形，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">rotate</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">旋转会造成出现锯齿现象</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以设置如下：</span></p>
<p>	一webkit一transform: rotate(一4deg) skew(10deg) translateZ(0);</p>
<p>	&nbsp;transform: rotate(一4deg) skew(10deg) translateZ(0);</p>
<p>	&nbsp;outline: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0)</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">移动端点击</span>300ms<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">延迟</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	300ms<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">导致用户体验不是很好，解决这个问题，我们</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般在移动端用</span>tap<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件来取代</span><span style="font-family: Arial">click</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件。推荐两个</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个是</span>fastclick<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个是</span>tap.js</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">关于</span>300ms<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">延迟，具体请看：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http://thx.github.io/mobile/300ms</span>一click一delay/</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">移动端点透问题</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">案例如下：</span></p>
<p>	&lt;div id="haorooms"&gt;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点头事件测试</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;/div&gt;</span></p>
<p>	&lt;a href="www.jb51.net"&gt;www.jb51.net&lt;/a&gt;</p>
<p>	div<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是绝对定位的蒙层</span><span style="font-family: Arial">,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并且</span><span style="font-family: Arial">z</span>一index<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">高于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签是页面中的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个链接，我们给</span>div<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">绑定</span><span style="font-family: Arial">tap</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件：</span></p>
<p>	$('#haorooms').on('tap',function(){</p>
<p>		$('#haorooms').hide();</p>
<p>	});</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">我们点击蒙层时</span> div<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">正常消失，但是当我们在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签上点击蒙层时，发现</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">链接被触发，这就是所谓的点透事件。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原因：</span></p>
<p>	touchstart <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">早于 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">touchend </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">早于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">click</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。即</span><span style="font-family: Arial">click</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的触发是有延迟的，这个时间大概在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">300ms</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">左右，也就是说我们</span><span style="font-family: Arial">tap</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">触发之后蒙层隐藏， 此时</span><span style="font-family: Arial">click</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还没有触发，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">300ms</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之后由于蒙层隐藏，我们的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">click</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">触发到了下面的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">链接上。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决：</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）尽量都使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">touch</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件来替换</span><span style="font-family: Arial">click</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件。例如用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">touchend</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件</span><span style="font-family: Arial">(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">推荐</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">fastclick</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，参考：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">https://github.com/ftlabs/fastclick</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">preventDefault</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">阻止</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">click</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>4<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）延迟</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定的时间</span>(300ms+)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来处理事件 （不推荐）</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）以上</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般都能解决，实在不行就换成</span>click<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下面介绍</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下</span>touchend<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件，如下：</span></p>
<p>	$("#haorooms").on("touchend", function (event) {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;event.preventDefault();</p>
<p>	&nbsp;});</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">关于</span> iOS <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">OS X </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">端字体的优化</span><span style="font-family: Arial">(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">横竖屏会出现字体加粗不</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">致等</span>)</li>

</ol>
<p>	iOS <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器横屏时会重置字体大小，设置 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">text</span>一size一adjust <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">none </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以解决 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">iOS </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上的问题，但桌面版 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">Safari </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的字体缩放功能会失效，因此最佳方案是将 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">text</span>一size一adjust <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">100% </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>	一webkit一text一size一adjust: 100%;</p>
<p>	一ms一text一size一adjust: 100%;</p>
<p>	text一size一adjust: 100%;</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">关于</span> iOS <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">系统中，中文输入法输入英文时，字母之间可能会出现</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个六分之</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">空格可以通过正则去掉</span>this.value = this.value.replace(/\u2006/g, '');</li>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">移动端</span> HTML5 audio autoplay <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">失效问题</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这个不是</span> BUG<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，由于自动播放网页中的音频或视频，会给用户带来</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些困扰或者不必要的流量消耗，所以苹果系统和安卓系统通常都会禁止自动播放和使用</span>JS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的触发播放，必须由用户来触发才可以播放。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决方法思路：先通过用户</span>touchstart<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">触碰，触发播放并暂停（音频开始加载，后面用 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">JS </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">再操作就没问题了）。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决代码：</span></p>
<p>	document.addEventListener('touchstart', function () {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;document.getElementsByTagName('audio')[0].play();</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;document.getElementsByTagName('audio')[0].pause();</p>
<p>	});</p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">移动端</span> HTML5 input date <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不支持 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">placeholder </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">问题</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">复制代码</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码如下</span>:</p>
<p>	&lt;input placeholder="Date" class="textbox一n" type="text" onfocus="(this.type='date')" &nbsp;id="date"&gt;</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有的浏览器可能要点击两遍！</span></p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">部分机型存在</span>type<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">search</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">input</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，自带</span><span style="font-family: Arial">close</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">按钮样式修改方法</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有些机型的搜索</span>input<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">控件会自带</span><span style="font-family: Arial">close</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">按钮（</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个伪元素），而通常为了兼容所有浏览器，我们会自己实现</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个，此时去掉原生</span>close<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">按钮的方法为</span></p>
<p>	#Search::一webkit一search一cancel一button{</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;display: none; &nbsp;</p>
<p>	}</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果想使用原生</span>close<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">按钮，又想使其符合设计风格，可以对这个伪元素的样式进行修改。</span></p>
<ol>
<li><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">唤起</span>select<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">option</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">展开</span></li>

</ol>
<p>	zepto<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方式</span><span style="font-family: Arial">:</span></p>
<p>	$(sltElement).trrgger("mousedown");</p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原生</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方式</span><span style="font-family: Arial">:</span></p>
<p>	function showDropdown(sltElement) {</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;var event;</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;event = document.createEvent('MouseEvents');</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;event.initMouseEvent('mousedown', true, true, window);</p>
<p>	&nbsp;&nbsp;sltElement.dispatchEvent(event);</p>
<p>	};</p>
<p class="46">五十八、&nbsp;<strong>H</strong><strong>5<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中新增的单位</span><span style="font-family: Arial">rem</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">是什么意思，和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">em</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的关系，以及</span><span style="font-family: Arial">rem</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">在自适应布局中的应用方法</span></strong></p>
<p>Rem<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为单位：</span></p>
<p>rem<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是相对于根元素</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;html&gt;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的“</span><span style="font-family: Arial">font</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">size</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">”为基准。比如说我们给</span><span style="font-family: Arial">html</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">font</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">size</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">100px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">那么我们要给</span>html<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">p</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">16px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的字体，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">font</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">size</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.16rem</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就可以，在这里</span><span style="font-family: Arial">16px=.16rem</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>Em<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为单位：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这种技术需要一个参考点，一般都是以</span>&lt;body&gt;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的“</span><span style="font-family: Arial">font</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">size</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">”为基准。比如说我们使用“</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1em</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">”等于“</span><span style="font-family: Arial">10px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">”来改变默认值“</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1em=16px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">”，这样一来，我们设置字体大小相当于“</span><span style="font-family: Arial">14px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">”时，只需要将其值设置为“</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1.4em</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">”。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这个单位与</span>em<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有什么区别呢？</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">区别在于使用</span>rem<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为元素设定字体大小时，仍然是相对大小，但相对的只是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTML</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">根元素。这个单位可谓集相对大小和绝对大小的优点于一身，通过它既可以做到只修改根元素就成比例地调整所有字体大小，又可以避免字体大小逐层复合的连锁反应。目前，除了</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IE8</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">及更早版本外，所有浏览器均已支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">rem</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。对于不支持它的浏览器，应对方法也很简单，就是多写一个绝对单位的声明。这些浏览器会忽略用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">rem</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设定的字体大小。</span></p>
<p class="46">五十九、&nbsp;<strong>如何实现浏览器内多个标签页之间的通信？</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>WebSocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或</span><span style="font-family: Arial">SharedWorker</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把客户端和服务器端建立</span><span style="font-family: Arial">socket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">连接，从而实现通信；也可以调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">localstorge</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookies</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等本地存储方法。</span></p>
<p class="46">六十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">假设现在页面里有一个</span>id<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">con</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">div</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，现在需要编写</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">代码，在页面加载完成后 将</span><span style="font-family: Arial">div</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的高度设置成</span><span style="font-family: Arial">100px</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，宽度设置成</span><span style="font-family: Arial">60px</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，并设置成灰色的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1px</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的边框，背景设置成浅黄色。</span></strong></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>window.onload=function(){</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;var oDiv=document.getElementById("con");</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;oDiv.style.height="100px";</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;oDiv.style.width="60px";</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;oDiv.style.width="1px solid gray";</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;oDiv.style.backgroundColor="yellow";</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="46">六十一、&nbsp;<strong>对新技术有那些了解，常去的网站有那些</strong></p>
<p>node.js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">angular.js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">vue.js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">reactjs</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">react-native</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，微信小程序</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">掘金、简书、</span>github<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">csdn</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，知乎等</span></p>
<p class="46">六十二、&nbsp;<strong>用程序找出数组中出现次数超过一半的数字</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">思路：</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、 </span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个数字在数组中出现次数超过了</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">半，则排序后，位于数组中间的数字</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定就是该出现次数超过了长度</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">半的数字（可以用反证法证明），也即是说，这个数字就是统计学上的中位数。最容易想到的办法是用快速排序对数组排序号后，直接取出中间的那个数字，这样的时间复杂度为</span>O(nlogn)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，空间复杂度为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">O(1)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、事实上可以不用对数组进行排序，或者说仅部分排序，受快速排序的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">partition</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数的启发，我们可以利用反复调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">partition</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数来求的该数字。我们现在数组中随机选取</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个数字，而后通过</span>Partition<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数返回该数字在数组中的索引</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，如果</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">刚好等于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">n/2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，则这个数字便是数组的中位数，也即是要求的数，如果</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">大于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">n/2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，则中位数肯定在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的左边，在左边继续寻找即可，反之在右边寻找。这样可以只在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">边寻找，而不用两边都排序，减少了</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">半排序时间。这种情况的平均时间复杂度大致为：</span>T(n) = n+n/2+n/4+n/8+....+1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，很明显当</span><span style="font-family: Arial">n</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">很大时，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">T(n)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">趋近于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2n</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，也就是说平均情况下时间复杂度为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">O(n),</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">但是这种情况下，最坏的时间复杂度依然为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">O(n*n)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，最坏情况下，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">index</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">总是位于数组的最左或最右边，这样时间复杂度为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">T(n) = n+n</span>一1+n一2+n一3+....+1 = n(n一1)/2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，显然，时间复杂度为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">O(n*n)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，空间复杂度为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">O(1)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p class="46">六十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">请设计一套方案，用于确保页面中</span>js<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">加载完全，对于优化某网页的加载速度，有什么独到见解</span></strong></p>
<p>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法：</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>&lt;script type="text/javascript"&gt; </strong></p>
<p><strong>window.onload=function(){ </strong></p>
<p><strong>var userName="xiaoming"; </strong></p>
<p><strong>alert(userName); </strong></p>
<p><strong>} </strong></p>
<p><strong>&lt;/script&gt;</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p>jquery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法：</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>&lt;script type="text/javascript"&gt; </strong></p>
<p><strong>$(document).ready(function(){ </strong></p>
<p><strong>var userName="xiaoming"; </strong></p>
<p><strong>alert(userName); </strong></p>
<p><strong>}); </strong></p>
<p><strong>&lt;/script&gt; </strong></p>
<p><strong>或者简写：</strong></p>
<p><strong>$(function(){ </strong></p>
<p><strong>var userName="xiaoming"; </strong></p>
<p><strong>alert(userName); </strong></p>
<p><strong>});</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如何确定</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是否加载完全或者页面中的所有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加载完全，具体办法如下：</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>
<p><strong>function loadScript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（ </span><span style="font-family: Arial">url, callback</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">） </span><span style="font-family: Arial">{</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var script = document.createElement("script");</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;script.type = "text/javascript";</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if (script.readyState) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;script.onreadystatechange = function() {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if (script.readyState == "loaded" || script.readyState == "complete") {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;script.onreadystatechange = null;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;callback();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;} else {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;script.onload = function() {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;callback();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;script.src = url;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;document.getElementsByName("head")[0].appendChild(script);</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如何让脚本的执行顺序按照你设定的顺序执行，使用嵌套的方式：</span></p>
