<p class="46">七十四、&nbsp;<strong>对前端界面工程师这个职位是怎么理解的？它的前景怎样？</strong></p>
<p>前端工程师属于一个比较新兴的技术，各种技术层出不穷，随着客户体验的重要性前端需要掌握的技能也越来越多，对前端的要求也越来越多，而且我们前端是最贴近用户的程序员，主要负责<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实现界面交互</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提升用户体验</span>，而且<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有了</span>Node.js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，前端可以实现服务端的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些事情</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">针对服务器的优化、拥抱最新前端技术</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，除了掌握必要的技能还要掌握用户的心理，善于沟通。</span> </p>
<p>前景：前景无疑是值得肯定的，也需要我们时刻关注最新的技术，这会是一个时刻都在学习的道路</p>
<p class="46">七十五、&nbsp;<strong>E</strong><strong>val<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">函数的作用</span></strong></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;eval<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以将字符串生成语句执行，一般执行动态的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">语句。 </span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;eval<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的使用场合：有时候我们预先不知道要执行什么语句，只有当条件和参数给时才知道执行什么语句，这时候</span><span style="font-family: Arial">eval</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就派上用场了。</span></p>
<p class="46">七十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">标签上</span>title<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">alt</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">属性的区别是什么</span></strong></p>
<p>title <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是鼠标放上去的额外信息 </span></p>
<p>alt <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是图片不能正常显示的时候，用文字代替</span></p>
<p class="46">七十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">对</span>WEB<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">标准以及</span><span style="font-family: Arial">w3c</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的理解与认识？</span></strong></p>
<p>Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标准就是将页面的解构、表现和行为各自独立实现，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">w3c</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对标注提出了规范化的要求</span></p>
<p>1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对结构的要求：（标签规范可以提高搜索引擎对页面的抓取效率，对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">SEO</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">很有帮助）</span></p>
<p>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）标签字母要小写；</span></p>
<p>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）标签要闭合；</span></p>
<p>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）标签不允许随意嵌套。</span></p>
<p>2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">css</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的要求：</span></p>
<p>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）尽量使用外联</span><span style="font-family: Arial">css</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">样式表和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">脚本，使结构、表现和行为分成三块，符合规范，同时提高页面渲染速度，提高用户体验；</span></p>
<p>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）样式尽量少用行间样式表，使结构与表现分离，标签的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">id</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">class</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">命名要做到见文知义，标签越少，加载越快，用户体验更高，代码维护更简单，便于改版；</span></p>
<p>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）不需要变动页面内容，便可提供打印版本而不需要复制内容，提高网站易用性</span></p>
<p class="46">七十八、&nbsp;<strong>C</strong><strong>ss<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">选择符有哪些？哪些属性可以继承？优先级算法如何计算？</span></strong></p>
<p>	1.id<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">选择器（ </span><span style="font-family: Arial"># myid</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>	2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">类选择器（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.myclassname</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>	3.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签选择器（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">div, h1, p</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>	4.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相邻选择器（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">h1 + p</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>	5.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">子选择器（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ul &lt; li</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>	6.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后代选择器（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">li a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>	7.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通配符选择器（ </span><span style="font-family: Arial">* </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>	8.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性选择器（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a[rel = "external"]</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>	9.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">伪类选择器（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">a: hover, li: nth </span>一&nbsp;child<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>可继承：&nbsp;font一size font一family color,;</p>
<p>不可继承&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span>border padding margin width height</p>
<p>优先级就近原则，样式定义最近者为准；<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">载入样式以最后载入的定位为准</span>;</p>
<p>优先级为:&nbsp;&nbsp;!important &gt; &nbsp;id &gt; class &gt; tag &nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;important <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">比 内联优先级高</span></p>
<p class="46">七十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">请戳出</span>ie6/7<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">下特有的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cssbug</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一：</span>li<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">边距“无故</span>”&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增加</span> </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span>ul<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的显示形式为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">*display:inline</span>一block;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即可，前面加</span><span style="font-family: Arial">*</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是只 针对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IE6/IE7</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有效</span></p>
<p>二：IE6 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">min</span>一height<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性，但它却认为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">height</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是最小高度</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span>ie6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不支持但其余浏览器支持的属性</span><span style="font-family: Arial">!important</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">三</span>:Overflow:</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>IE6/7<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">overflow</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">无法正确的隐藏有相对定位</span><span style="font-family: Arial">position:relative;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的子元素。解决方法就是给外包容器</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.wrap</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加上</span><span style="font-family: Arial">position:relative;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">四：</span>border<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">none </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IE6</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不起作用： 写成</span><span style="font-family: Arial">border</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">0 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就可以了</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">五</span>:100%<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">高度</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>IE6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下，如果要给元素定义</span><span style="font-family: Arial">100%</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">高度，必须要明确定义它的父级元素的高度，如果你需要给元素定义满屏的高度，就得先给</span><span style="font-family: Arial">html</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">body</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定义 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">height:100%;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">六</span>:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">双边距 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">Bug</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当元素浮动时，</span>IE6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会错误的的把浮动方式的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">margin</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">值双倍计算，给</span><span style="font-family: Arial">float</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的元素添加一个</span><span style="font-family: Arial">display</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">inline</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">七：躲猫猫</span>bug</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定义了</span>:hover<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的链接，当鼠标移到那些链接上时，在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IE6</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下就会触发躲猫猫。</span><br>	1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在（那个未浮动的）内容之后添加</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>&lt;span style=”clear: both;”&gt;&lt;/span&gt;<br>	2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">触发包含了这些链接的容器的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">hasLayout</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个简单的方法就是给其定义</span>height:1%;</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">八</span>:IE6 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">绝对定位的元素</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1px </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">间距</span><span style="font-family: Arial">bug</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当绝对定位的父元素或宽度为奇数时，</span>bottom<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">right</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会多出现</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1px</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决方案，针对</span>IE6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行</span><span style="font-family: Arial">hack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">处理</span>			</p>
<p class="46">八十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何将一个元素</span>600<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">毫秒的速度缓慢向上滑动显示？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果需要在父元素底部向上，可以利用</span>margin<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">top </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把子元素，挤下去，同事父元素设置隐藏，然后改变</span><span style="font-family: Arial">margintop</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的值也可以利用定来做，把子元素定位最下边</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>(function(){</strong></p>
<p><strong>var oDiv = document.createElement('div');</strong></p>
<p><strong>oDiv.style.width = '100px';</strong></p>
<p><strong>oDiv.style.height = '100px';</strong></p>
<p><strong>oDiv.style.backgroundColor = 'red';</strong></p>
<p><strong>oDiv.style.position = 'absolute';</strong></p>
<p><strong>oDiv.style.marginTop = 100 + 'px';</strong></p>
<p><strong>document.body.appendChild(oDiv);</strong></p>
<p><strong>var timer = setInterval(function(){</strong></p>
<p><strong>var m = parseInt(oDiv.style.marginTop);</strong></p>
<p><strong>if (m == 0 ) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>clearInterval(timer);</strong></p>
<p><strong>return;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>oDiv.style.marginTop = parseInt(oDiv.style.marginTop) <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">1 + 'px';</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>},600);</strong></p>
<p><strong>})();</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="46">八十一、&nbsp;<strong>写一个获取非行间样式的函数</strong></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>Function getStyle(obj, attr){</strong></p>
<p><strong>If(obj.currentStyle){</strong></p>
<p><strong>return obj.currentStyle[attr];</strong></p>
<p><strong>}else{</strong></p>
<p><strong>return getComputedStyle(obj,false)[attr];</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="46">八十二、&nbsp;<strong>请用正则表达式验证数字</strong></p>
<p><strong>/</strong><strong>[0</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span></strong><strong>9]*$</strong><strong>/</strong></p>
<p class="46">八十三、&nbsp;<strong>为什么利用多个域名来提供网站资源会更有效？</strong></p>
<p>1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">突破浏览器的并发限制（浏览器同一域名最大的并发请求数量为</span>6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ie6</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个）</span></p>
<p>2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节约</span>cookie带宽</p>
<p>3)&nbsp;CDN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">缓存更方便</span></p>
<p>4)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">防止不必要的安全问题（尤其是</span>cookie<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的隔离尤为重要）</span></p>
<p>5)&nbsp;节约主机域名连接数，优化页面响应速度</p>
<p class="46">八十四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你如何从浏览器的</span>URL<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中获取参数信息</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器宿主环境中，有一个</span>location<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象，同时这个对象也是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">window</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">document</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象的属性。</span></p>
<p>location<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象中提供了与当前窗口加载的文档有关的的信息，即</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">信息。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如</span> &nbsp;https://www.baidu.com/api/sousu?search=baidu&amp;id=123#2</p>
<p>		location.href: <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">完整</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span></p>
<p>		location.protocol: <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回协议（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">https:</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>		location.host: <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回服务器名称和端口号（</span><a href="http://www.baidu.com/"><span style="text-decoration: underline">www.baidu.com</span></a>）</p>
<p>&nbsp;location.hostname: <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回服务器名称（</span><a href="http://www.baidu.com/"><span style="text-decoration: underline">www.baidu.com</span></a>）</p>
<p>&nbsp;location.port:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回服务器端口号（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">默认</span><span style="font-family: Arial">80</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">https</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">默认</span><span style="font-family: Arial">443</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;location.pathname:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回</span><span style="font-family: Arial">URL</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的目录和文件名（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">api/sousu</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;location.search:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回查询字符串（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">?search=baidu&amp;id=123#2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;location.hash:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回</span><span style="font-family: Arial">hash</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">值（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">#2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p class="46">八十五、&nbsp;<strong>手机端文字大小用什么单位</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对于只需要适配少部分手机设备，且分辨率对页面影响不大的，使用</span>px<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即可</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对于需要适配各种移动设备，使用</span>rem<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，例如只需要适配</span><span style="font-family: Arial">iPhone</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">iPad</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等分辨率差别比较挺大的设备</span></p>
<p class="46">八十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">是否做过有上百图层的</span>psd<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">切图？</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ps</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">隐藏其他图层，只显示其中一个图层的快捷键</span></strong></p>
<p>Alt&nbsp;+ <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当前图层前眼睛</span></p>
<p class="46">八十七、&nbsp;<strong>浏览器标准模式和怪异模式之间的区别是什么？</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这是个历史遗留问题</span>，W3C<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标准推出前，旧的页面都是根据旧的渲染方式对页面进行渲染的，因此在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">W3C</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标准推出后为了保证旧页面的正常显示，保持浏览器的兼容性，这样浏览器上就产生了能够兼容</span><span style="font-family: Arial">W3C</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标准渲染的严格模式和保证旧页面显示的怪异模式的标准兼容模式。</span></p>
<p>	具体表现：</p>
<p>1.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在严格模式中 ：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">width</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是内容宽度</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，元素真正的宽度 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">= margin</span>一left + border一left一width + padding一left + width + padding一right + border一right一&nbsp;width + &nbsp;margin一right;</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>怪异<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模式中</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span>width<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">则是元素的实际宽度</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，内容宽度 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">= width </span>一&nbsp;( padding一left + padding一right + border一left一width + border一right一width)</p>
<p>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）可以设置行内元素的高宽</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在标准模式下，给</span><span style="font-family: Arial">span</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等行内元素设置</span><span style="font-family: Arial">wdith</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">height</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都不会生效，而在</span>怪异<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模式下，则会生效。</span></p>
<p>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）可设置百分比的高度</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在标准模式下，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个元素的高度是由其包含的内容来决定的，如果父元素没有设置高度，子元素设置</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个百分比的高度是无效的。</span></p>
<p>4<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">margin:0 auto</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置水平居中在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IE</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下会失效</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">margin:0 auto</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在标准模式下可以使元素水平居中，但在</span>怪异<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模式下却会失效</span>,&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">怪异</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模式下的解决办法，用</span>text一align<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性</span><span style="font-family: Arial">:</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;body{text一align:center};#content{text一align:left}</p>
<p>5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span>怪异<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模式下设置图片的</span>padding<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会失效</span></p>
<p>6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span>怪异<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模式下</span>Table<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的字体属性不能继承上层的设置</span></p>
<p>7<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span>怪异<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模式下</span>white一space:pre<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会失效</span></p>
<p class="46">八十八、&nbsp;<strong>J</strong><strong>avascript<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">同源策略</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同源策略是</span>Javascript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">重要的安全度量标准。它最早出自</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Netscape Navigator2.0</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，其目的是防止某个文档或脚本从多个不同源装载。所谓的同源就是同协议</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同主机名</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同端口号</span>。</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">它的精髓很简单：它认为自任何站点装载的信赖内容是不安全的。当被浏览器半信半疑的脚本运行在沙箱时，它们应该只被允许访问来自同</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">站点的资源，而不是那些来自其它站点可能怀有恶意的资源。</span></p>
<p class="46">八十九、&nbsp;<strong>为什么要有同源限制？</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">我们举例说明：比如一个黑客程序，他利用</span>Iframe<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把真正的银行登录页面嵌到他的页面上，当你使用真实的用户名，密码登录时，他的页面就可以通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Javascript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">读取到你的表单中</span><span style="font-family: Arial">input</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的内容，这样用户名，密码就轻松到手了。</span></p>
<p>缺点：</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">现在网站的</span>JS <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都会进行压缩，一些文件用了严格模式，而另一些没有。这时这些本来是严格模式的文件，被 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">merge </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后，这个串就到了文件的中间，不仅没有指示严格模式，反而在压缩后浪费了字节。</span></p>
<p class="46">九十、&nbsp;<strong>了解响应式布局吗？请大体说一说</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">响应式布局概念</span>：Responsive design<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，意在实现不同屏幕分辨率的终端上浏览网页的不同展示方式。通过响应式设计能使网站在手机和平板电脑上有更好的浏览阅读体验。</span></p>
<p>	设计步骤：</p>
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span>meta<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签</span></p>
<p>2．根据媒体查询设置样式</p>
<p>3．设置多种视图宽度</p>
<p>4．注意点：</p>
<p>5．宽度使用百分比</p>
<p>6．处理图片缩放问题</p>
<p class="46">九十一、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">身为以为</span>web<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">前端工程师，你肯定知道现在最流行的前端技术吧，有那些？</span></strong></p>
<p>Vuejs2.0/Angular2.0/React Native /es6//Nodejs</p>
<p>http2</p>
<p>gulp/webpack</p>
<p class="46">九十二、&nbsp;<strong>请简述为什么要使用数据库的事务</strong></p>
<p class="48"><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据库事务</span>(Database Transaction) <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，是指作为单个逻辑工作单元执行的一系列操作，要么完全地执行，要么完全地不执行。</span></p>
<p class="48"><strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原子性（</span>Atomic<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Atomicity)</span></strong><br>　　事务必须是原子工作单元；对于其数据修改，要么全都执行，要么全都不执行。通常，与某个事务关联的操作具有共同的目标，并且是相互依赖的。如果系统只执行这些操作的一个子集，则可能会破坏事务的总体目标。原子性消除了系统处理操作子集的可能性。<br>　　<strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一致性（</span>Consistent<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">(Consistency)</span></strong><br><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　事务在完成时，必须使所有的数据都保持一致状态。在相关数据库中，所有规则都必须应用于事务的修改，以保持所有数据的完整性。事务结束时，所有的内部数据结构（如</span> B <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">树索引或双向链表）都必须是正确的。某些维护一致性的责任由应用程序开发人员承担，他们必须确保应用程序已强制所有已知的完整性约束。例如，当开发用于转帐的应用程序时，应避免在转帐过程中任意移动小数点。</span><br>　　<strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">隔离性（</span>Insulation<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">(Isolation)</span></strong><br>　　由并发事务所作的修改必须与任何其它并发事务所作的修改隔离。事务查看数据时数据所处的状态，要么是另一并发事务修改它之前的状态，要么是另一事务修改它之后的状态，事务不会查看中间状态的数据。这称为隔离性，因为它能够重新装载起始数据，并且重播一系列事务，以使数据结束时的状态与原始事务执行的状态相同。当事务可序列化时将获得最高的隔离级别。在此级别上，从一组可并行执行的事务获得的结果与通过连续运行每个事务所获得的结果相同。由于高度隔离会限制可并行执行的事务数，所以一些应用程序降低隔离级别以换取更大的吞吐量。<br>　<strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　持久性（</span>Duration<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">(Durability</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></strong><br>　　事务完成之后，它对于系统的影响是永久性的。该修改即使出现致命的系统故障也将一直保持。</p>
<p class="46">九十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">聊</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">聊前端存储。</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">老朋友</span>cookie</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">短暂的</span> sessionStorage</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">简易强大的</span>localStorage</p>
<p>websql<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">indexeddb</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000005927232"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https://segmentfault.com/aZ1190000005927232</span></a></p>
<p class="46">九十四、&nbsp;<strong>BFC</strong></p>
<p>w3c<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">规范中的</span>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定义：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浮动元素和绝对定位元素，非块级盒子的块级容器（例如</span>inline一blocks, table一cells,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span> table一captions),<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以及</span>overflow<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">值不为</span>“visiable”<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的块级盒子，都会为他们的内容创建新的</span> BFC&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">块级格式上下文）。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中，盒子从顶端开始垂直地</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个接</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个地排列，两个盒子之间的垂直的间隙是由他们</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>margin<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">值所决定的。在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中，两个相邻的块级盒子的垂直外边距会产生折叠。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中，每</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个盒子的左外边缘</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>margin一left)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会触碰到容器的左边缘</span>(border一left)(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对于 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">从右到左的格式来说，则触碰到右边缘）。</span></p>
<p>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的通俗理解：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">首先</span>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个名词，是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个独立的布局环境，我们可以理解为</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个箱子（实际上是看不见</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">摸不着的），箱子里面物品的摆放是不受外界的影响的。转换为</span>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的理解则是：</span>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">元素的布局是不受外界的影响（我们往往利用这个特性来消除浮动元素对其非浮动的兄弟元</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">素和其子元素带来的影响。</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并且在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>BFC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中，块盒与行盒</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">行盒由</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">行中所有的内联元</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">素所组成）都会垂直的沿着其父元素的边框排列。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span></p>
<p><a href="http://www.w3cplus.com/css/understanding-bfc-and-margin-collapse.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">w</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">3</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cplus</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">css</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">understanding</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">bfc</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">and</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">margin</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">collapse.html</span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.zhihu.com/question/28433480"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhihu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">question</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/28433480</span></a></p>
<p><strong><em>一一一一一一一一</em></strong><strong><em><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">前端工程化</span></em></strong><strong><em>一一一一一</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">九十五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">场景：你是第</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">天来公司上班的，项目代码托管在</span></strong><strong>&nbsp;GitLab</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">项目地址：</span></strong><strong>git@lab.com:org/project.git<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，现</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">在有</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">处代码需要你修改。请完成此项任务中，与</span> git/gitlab</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">相关的操作步骤。</span></strong></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>第一步：<span style="font-family: Arial">$&gt; ssh</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">keygen </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">t rss </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">C zhangsan@abc.com </span></strong></p>
<p><strong>第二步：拷贝公钥到<span style="font-family: Arial">gitlab </span></strong></p>
<p><strong>第三步：</strong></p>
<p><strong>$&gt; git config —global user.name zhangsan</strong></p>
<p><strong>$&gt; git config —global user.email zhangsan@abc.com</strong></p>
<p><strong>第四步：<span style="font-family: Arial">$&gt; git clone git@lab.com:org/project.git</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>第五步：<span style="font-family: Arial">$&gt; git checkout </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">b project</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">20170227</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">zhangsan</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">bugfix</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>第六步：修改代码</strong></p>
<p><strong>第七步：<span style="font-family: Arial">git status</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>第八步：<span style="font-family: Arial">git add .</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>第九步：<span style="font-family: Arial">git commit </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">am </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">‘</span><span style="font-family: Arial">bugfix</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">’</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>第十步：</strong></p>
<p><strong>git push <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">set</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">upstream origin project</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">20170227</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">zhangsan</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">bugfix</span></strong></p>

<p class="46">九十六、&nbsp;CSS<span style="font-family: &quot;Malgun Gothic&quot;">，</span>JS<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">代码压缩，以及代码</span></strong>CDN<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">托管，图片整</span></strong><strong>合</strong></p>
<p>CSSJS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码压缩：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以应用</span>gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">gulp</span>一uglify, gulp一minify一css<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模块完成；可以应用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webpack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">UglifyJsPlugin </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">压缩插件完成。</span></p>
<p>CDN:</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">内容分发网络</span>(CDN)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个经策略性部署的整体系统，包括分布式存储、负载均衡、网络请</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">求的重定向和内容管理</span>4<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个要件。主要特点有：本地</span>Cache<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加速，镜像服务，远程加速，带</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">宽优化。关键技术有：内容发布，内容路由，内容交换，性能管理。</span>CDN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">网站加速适合以</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">咨询为主的网站。</span>CDN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是对域名加速不是对网站服务器加速。</span>CDN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和镜像站比较不需要访</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">客手动选择要访问的镜像站。</span>CDN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用后网站无需任何修改即可使用</span>CDN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">获得加速效果。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果通过</span>CDN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后看到的网页还是旧网页，可以通过</span>URL<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">推送服务解决，新增的网页和图片</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不需要</span>URL<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">推送。使用动态网页可以不缓存即时性要求很高的网页和图片。</span>CDN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以通过</span> gi<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">域</span>SVN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来管理。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">图片整合</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">减少网站加载时间的最有效的方式之</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是减少网站的</span>HTTP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求数。实现这</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目标的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有效的方法就是通过</span>CSS&nbsp;Sprites&nbsp;——<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将多个图片整合到</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个图片中，然后再用</span>CSS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来定</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">位。缺点是可维护性差。可以使用百度的</span>fis/webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来自动化管理</span>sprite<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p class="46">九十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何利用</span></strong>webpack<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">把代码上传服务器以及转码测试</span>?</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码上传：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以使用</span>sftp一webpack一plugin,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">但是会把子文件夹给提取出来，不优雅。可以使用</span>gulp +webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来实现。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">转码测试</span></p>
<p>webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">babel</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ES</span>6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">转码，开启</span>devtool: “source一map"<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来进行浏览器测试。应用</span> karma<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或</span><span style="font-family: Arial">mocha</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来做单元测试。</span></p>
<p class="46">九十八、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">项目上线流程是怎样的？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">流程建议</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模拟线上的开发环境</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">本地反向代理线上真实环境开发即可。</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>apache, nginx, nodejs<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">均可实现）</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模拟线上的测试环境</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模拟线上的测试环境，其实是需要</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">台有真实数据的测试机，建议没条件搭</span>daily<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的，就直接</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用线上数据测好了，只不过程序部分走你们的测试环境而已，有条件搭</span>daily<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">最好。</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可连调的测试环境</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可连调的测试环境，分为</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种。</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种是开发测试都在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个局域网段，直接绑</span>hosts<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">即可，不在</span> 一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个网段，就每人分配</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">台虚拟的测试机，放在大家都可以访问到的公司内网，代码直接往</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上布即可。</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">自动化的上线系统</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">自动化的上线系统，可以采用</span>Jenkins<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果没有，可以自行搭建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个简易的上线系统，原</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">理是每次上线时都抽取最新的</span>trunk<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或</span>master<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">做</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>tag<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">再打</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个时间戳的标记，然后分</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">发到</span>cdn<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就行了。界面里就</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个功能，打</span>tag,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">回滚到某</span><span style="font-family: Arial">tag,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">部署。</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">适合前后端的开发流程</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发流程依据公司所用到的工具，构建，框架。原则就是分散独立开发，互相不干扰，连调</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">时有</span>hosts<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可绑即可。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">简单的可操作流程</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码通过</span>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">管理，新需求创建新分支，分支开发，主干发布</span> 一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上线走简易上线系统，参见上</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>gulp+webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">连到发布系统，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">键集成，本地只关心原码开发</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">本地环境通过</span>webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">反向代理的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">server</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">搭建基于</span>linux<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的本地测试机，自动完成</span>build+push<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">功能</span></p>
<p class="46">九十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">工程化怎么管理的？</span></strong></p>
<p>前端工程化可以自动化处理一些繁复的工作，提高开发效率，减少低级错误。</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目前前端构建工具很多，综合比较来看，</span>gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相对来说更灵活，可以做更多的定制化任务，而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webpack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在模块化方面更完美一些</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">打造前端工程化方案，同时引入</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webpack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来管理模块化代码，大致分工如下：</span></p>
<p>gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">html</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">压缩</span><span style="font-family: Arial">/</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">预处理</span><span style="font-family: Arial">/</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">条件编译，图片压缩，精灵图自动合并等任务</span></p>
<p>webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：管理模块化，构建</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js/css</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">具体流程可参考：</span> <a href="http://blog.csdn.net/java_goodstudy/article/details/52797322"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://blog.csdn.net/java_goodstudy/article/details/52797322</span></a></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="46">一百、&nbsp;git<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">常用命令</span></strong></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td width="35" height="0">&nbsp;</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>&nbsp;</td>
<td>&nbsp;</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p>Workspace:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">工作区</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;Index/Stage:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">暂存区</span> </p>
<p>Repository:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">仓库区（或本地仓库</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;Remote:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">远程仓库</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;git &nbsp;init; (# <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在当前目录新建一个</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Git</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码库</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;git &nbsp;add <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（添加当前目录的所有文件到暂存区）</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;git &nbsp;rm –cached [file] (# <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">停止追踪指定文件，但该文件会保留在工作区</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;git &nbsp;commit&nbsp;&nbsp;[file1] [file2] &nbsp;-m&nbsp;&nbsp;[message]&nbsp;(# <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提交暂存区的指定文件到仓库区 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;git&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;branch &nbsp;-a&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">列出所有本地分支和远程分支</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;git &nbsp;checkout&nbsp;&nbsp;[branch-name]&nbsp;(# <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">切换到指定分支，并更新工作区</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p>git &nbsp;status( # <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">显示有变更的文件</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></p>
<p>git &nbsp;push &nbsp;[remote] -tags (# <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提交所有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">tag) </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="http://www.ruanyifeng.com/blog/2015/12/git-cheat-sheet.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ruanyifeng</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/2015/12/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">git</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cheat</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">sheet.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百〇一、&nbsp;<strong>git<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">svn</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的区别</span></strong></p>
<p>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是分布式的，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">svn</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不是。</span></p>
<p>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">跟</span><span style="font-family: Arial">svn</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一样有自己的集中式版本库或服务器。但</span><span style="font-family: Arial">git</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">更倾向于被使用于分布式模式，克隆版本库后即使没有网络也能够</span><span style="font-family: Arial">commit</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件，查看历史版本记录，创建项目分支等，等网络再次连接上</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Push</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">到服务器端。</span></p>
<p>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把内容按元数据方式存储，而</span><span style="font-family: Arial">svn</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是按文件。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所有的资源控制系统都是把文件的元信息隐藏在一个类似</span>.svn,.cvs<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等的文件夹里。</span></p>
<p>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目录是处于你的机器上的一个克隆版的版本库，它拥有中心版本库上所有的东西，例如标签，分支，版本记录等。</span></p>
<p>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">没有一个全局的版本号，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">svn</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有。</span></p>
<p>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的内容完整性优于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">svn</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。因为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">git</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的内容存储使用的是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">SHA-1</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">哈希算法。</span></p>
<p>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以有无限个版本库，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">svn</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只能有一个指定中央版本库。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当</span>svn<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中央版本库有问题时，所有工作成员都一起瘫痪直到版本库维修完毕或者新的版本库设立完成。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">每一个</span>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都是一个版本库，区别是它们是否拥有活跃目录（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Git Working Tree</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）。如果主要版本库（例如：置於</span><span style="font-family: Arial">GitHub</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的版本库）有问题，工作成员仍然可以在自己的本地版本库（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">local repository</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）提交，等待主要版本库恢复即可。工作成员也可以提交到其他的版本库！</span></p>
<p class="46">一百〇二、&nbsp;<strong>webpack</strong>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: MingLiU">和</span> <strong>gulp</strong>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: MingLiU">对比</span></p>
<p>Gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是为了规范前端开发流程，实现前后端分离、模块化开发、版本控制、文件合并与</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">压缩、</span>mock<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据等功能的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个前端自动化构建工具。说的形象点，</span>“Gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就像是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个产品的</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">流水线，整个产品从无到有，都要受流水线的控制，在流水线上我们可以对产品进行管</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">理。</span>”<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">另外，</span>Gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是通过</span>task<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对整个开发过程进行构建。</span></p>
<p>Webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是当下最热门的前端资源模块化管理和打包工具。它可以将许多松散的模块按照</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">依赖和规则打包成符合生产环境部署的前端资源。还可以将按需加载的模块进行代码分隔，</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等到实际需要的时候再异步加载。通过</span>loader<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的转换，任何形式的资源都可以视作模块，比</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如</span> CommonJs&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模块</span>、AMD&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模块、</span>ES6 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模块、</span>CSS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">图片、</span>JSON<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span>Coffeescript、LESS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等。</span></p>
<p>Gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>Webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">功能实现对比：从基本概念、启动本地</span>Server<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span>sass/less<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">预编译、模块化</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发、文件合并与压缩、</span>mock<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据、版本控制、组件控制八个方面对</span>Gulp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>Webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行对比。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="http://www.tuicool.com/articles/e632EbA"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">tuicool</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">articles</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">e</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">632</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">EbA</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百〇三、&nbsp;webpack<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">打包文件太大怎么办？</span></strong></p>
<p>webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把我们所有的文件都打包成</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>JS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件，这样即使你是小项目，打包后的文件也</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会非常大。可以从去除不必要的插件，提取第三方库，代码压缩，代码分割，设置缓存几个</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方面着手优化。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span>http://www.jianshu.com/p/a64735eb0e2b</p>
<p class="46">一百〇四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">谈谈你对</span>webpack<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的看法</span></strong></p>
<p>WebPack <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是一个模块打包工具，你可以使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">WebPack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">管理你的模块依赖，并编绎输出模块们所需的静态文件。它能够很好地管理、打包</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Web</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发中所用到的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTML</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JavaScript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以及各种静态文件（图片、字体等），让开发过程更加高效。对于不同类型的资源，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webpack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有对应的模块加载器。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webpack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模块打包器会分析模块间的依赖关系，最后 生成了优化且合并后的静态资源。</span></p>
<p>webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的两大特色：</span></p>
<p>1.code splitting<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（可以自动完成）</span></p>
<p>2.loader <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以处理各种类型的静态文件，并且支持串联操作</span></p>
<p>webpack <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是以</span><span style="font-family: Arial">commonJS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的形式来书写脚本滴，但对 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">AMD/CMD </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的支持也很全面，方便旧项目进行代码迁移。</span></p>
<p>webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">具有</span><span style="font-family: Arial">requireJs</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">browserify</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的功能，但仍有很多自己的新特性：</span></p>
<p>1. <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">CommonJS </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">AMD </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ES6</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的语法做了兼容</span></p>
<p>2. <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">css</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、图片等资源文件都支持打包</span></p>
<p>3. <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">串联式模块加载器以及插件机制，让其具有更好的灵活性和扩展性，例如提供对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CoffeeScript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ES6</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的支持</span></p>
<p>4. <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有独立的配置文件</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webpack.config.js</span></p>
<p>5. <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以将代码切割成不同的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">chunk</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，实现按需加载，降低了初始化时间</span></p>
<p>6. <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">SourceUrls </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">SourceMaps</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，易于调试</span></p>
<p>7. <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">具有强大的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Plugin</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">接口，大多是内部插件，使用起来比较灵活</span></p>
<p>8.webpack <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用异步 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">IO </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并具有多级缓存。这使得 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">webpack </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">很快且在增量编译上更加快</span></p>
<p class="46">一百〇五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">说说你对</span>AMD<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Commonjs</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的理解</span></strong></p>
<p>CommonJS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是服务器端模块的规范，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Node.js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">采用了这个规范。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CommonJS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">规范加载模块是同步的，也就是说，只有加载完成，才能执行后面的操作。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">AMD</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">规范则是非同步加载模块，允许指定回调函数。</span></p>
<p>AMD<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">推荐的风格通过返回一个对象做为模块对象，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CommonJS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的风格通过对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">module.exports</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或</span><span style="font-family: Arial">exports</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的属性赋值来达到暴露模块对象的目的。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百〇六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">不想让别人盗用你的图片，访问你的服务器资源该怎么处理？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目前常用的防盗链方法主要有两种：</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">Referer</span>:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">适合不想写代码的用户，也适合喜欢开发的用户</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>Referer<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议中的请求头，在跨页面访问的时候会带上。需要看看浏览器请求的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Referer</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http://</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">https://</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，一般是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http://</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">签名</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">URL</span>:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">适合喜欢开发的用户</span></p>
<p>详细参见：<span style="text-decoration: underline">https://yq.aliyun.com/articles/57931</span></p>
<p class="46">一百〇七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">精灵图和</span></strong>base<strong>64</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何选择？</span></strong></p>
<p>css<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">精灵，用于</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些小的图标不是特别多，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个的体积也稍大，比如大于</span>10K&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这个没有严 格的界定）。</span></p>
<p>base64,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用于小图标体积较小</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相对于</span>css<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">精灵），多少都无所谓。字体图标，用于</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些别</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">人做好的图标库（也有少数自己去做的）用起来比较方便，他的图标只能用于单色，图标用</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只能于</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种颜色。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百〇八、&nbsp;webpack<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">怎么引入第三方的库？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">拿</span>jQuery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为例： </span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>entry: {</strong></p>
<p><strong>page: 'path/to/page.js',</strong></p>
<p><strong>jquery: 'node—modules/jquery/dist/jquery.min.js'</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>new HtmlWebpaekPlugin({</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;filename: 'index.html',</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;template: 'index.html',</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;inject: true,</strong></p>
<p><strong>chunks: ['jquery','page'] // <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">按照先后顺序插入 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">script </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>})</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="46">一百〇九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如果线上出现</span></strong>bug<strong>&nbsp;</strong>git<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">怎么操作？</span></strong></p>
<p>方法<strong>1</strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：在当前主分支修改</span>bug，暂存当前的改动的代码，目的是让工作空间和远程代码一致：</p>
<p>Git stash</p>
<p>修改完bug<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">后提交修改：</span></p>
<p>git add .</p>
<p>git commit 一m "fix bug 1"</p>
<p>git push</p>
<p>从暂存区把之前的修改恢复，这样就和之前改动一样了</p>
<p>git stash pop</p>
<p>这时可能会出现冲突，因为你之前修改的文件，可能和bug<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是同</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个文件，如果有冲突会提示：</span></p>
<p>Auto一merging xxx.Java</p>
<p>CONFLICT (content): Merge conflict in xxx.java</p>
<p>前往xxx.java<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决冲突</span></p>
<p>注意stash pop<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">意思是从暂存区恢复到工作空间，同时删除此条暂存记录。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>方式<strong>2</strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：拉</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个新分支，老司机都推荐这样做，充分利用了</span>git<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">特性</span>，先暂存一下工作空间改动：</p>
<p>git stash</p>
<p>新建一个分支，并且换到这个新分支</p>
<p>git branch fix_bug //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">新建分支</span></p>
<p>git checkout fix_bug //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">切换分支</span></p>
<p>这时候就可以安心的在这个fix_bug<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">分支改</span><span style="font-family: Arial">bug</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">了，改完之后：</span></p>
<p>git add .</p>
<p>git commit 一m "fix a bug"</p>
<p>切换到master<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">主分支</span></p>
<p>git checkout master</p>
<p>从fix_bug<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">合并到</span><span style="font-family: Arial">master</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">分支</span></p>
<p>git merge fix_bug</p>
<p>提交代码</p>
<p>git push</p>
<p>然后从暂存区恢复代码</p>
<p>git stash pop</p>
<p>此时如有冲突，需要解决冲突</p>
<p class="46">一百一十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">用过</span></strong>Nginx<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">吗？都用过哪些？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="text-decoration: underline">nginx</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个高性能的</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和反向代理服务器</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section1">
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">常使用场景：</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">反向代理</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">网站负载均衡</span></p>
<p>详细参见：<a href="http://www.cnblogs.com/hobinly/p/6023883.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cnblogs</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">c</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">om</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">hobinly</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">p</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/6023883</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.html</span></a></p>
<h1><strong><em><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">移动端布局与适配</span></em></strong></h1>
<p class="46">一百一十一、&nbsp;iscroll<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">安卓低版本卡顿，如何解决？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方案</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span>iScroll&nbsp;v5.1.3 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置</span>momentum: true </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方案二：配置</span>probeType</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方案三：开启硬价加速：给</span>scroll<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">元素增加</span><span style="font-family: Arial">css</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">样式：</span>一webkit一transform:translate3d(0,0,0); </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方案四：判断手机版系统版本，应用原生</span>CSS: overflow:scroll一y</p>
<p class="46">一百一十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">移动布局自适应不同屏幕的几种方式</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">响应式布局</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;100%布局（弹性布局）</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;等比缩放布局（<span style="text-decoration: underline">rem</span>)</p>
<p class="46">一百一十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">请说下移动端常见的适配不同屏幕大小的方法？</span></strong></p>
<p>响应式布局</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">简而言之，就是页面元素的位置随着屏幕尺寸的变化而变化，通常会用百分比来定位，而在设计上需要预留一些可被</span>“压缩”的空间。</p>
<p>Cover<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">布局</span></p>
<p>就跟background一size<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cover</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">样，保持页面的宽高比，取宽或高之中的较小者占满屏幕，超出的内容会被隐藏。此布局适用于主要内容集中在中部，边沿无重要内容的设计。</span></p>
<p>Contain<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">布局</span></p>
<p>同样，也跟background一size<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">contain</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性那样，保持页面的宽高比，取宽或高之中的较大者占满屏幕，不足的部分会用背景填充。个人比较推荐用这种方式，但在设计上需要背景为单色，或者是可平铺的背景。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百一十四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你们做移动端平时在什么浏览器上测试？</span></strong></p>
<p>Chrome<span style="font-family: &quot;Malgun Gothic&quot;">，</span>Safari<span style="font-family: &quot;Malgun Gothic&quot;">，</span>微信X5, UC<span style="font-family: &quot;Malgun Gothic&quot;">，</span>其他手机自带浏览器</p>
<p class="46">一百一十五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">说说移动端是如何调试的？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">移动端调试：</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模拟手机调试</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;真机调试之android手机+Chrome</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">真机调试之</span> <span style="text-decoration: underline">iphone</span>&nbsp;+ <span style="text-decoration: underline">safari </span>⑷<span style="text-decoration: underline">UC</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">微信内置浏览器调试</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;debuggap</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">抓包</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参考：</span><a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000005964730"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">segmentfault</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">eom</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">190000005964730</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百一十六、&nbsp;<strong>ICONFONT</strong><strong>使用及其利与弊</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把一些零散的</span>icon<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">做成字体。我们调用文字的时候，渲染出来的就是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">icon</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">图像，这样的显示就是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">iconfont</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（字体图标）</span></p>
<p>好处：</p>
<ol>
<li>iconfont<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">图像放大后，不会失真。</span></li>
<li>iconfont<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节省流量</span></li>
<li>iconfont<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在颜色变幻方面很简单</span></li>

</ol>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">缺点：</span></p>
<ol>
<li>iconfont<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不能支持一个图像里面混入多重颜色</span></li>
<li>iconfont<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的使用没有使用图片那么直接，简单。</span></li>

</ol>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000005904616?_ea=953657"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">segmentfault</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">190000005904616? </span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ea</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">=953657</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百一十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">说说移动端</span></strong>Web<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">分辨率</span></strong></p>
<p>从以下几个方面做答：</p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">pc</span>到移动，渲染的变迁</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;可以更改的布局宽度</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;再次变迁的像素</p>
<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;又一次变迁</p>
<p class="45">(5)&nbsp;是时候说说安卓了</p>
<p>详细参见：<a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000005884985"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">segmentfault</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">190000005884985</span></a></p>
<p class="43"><strong><em>性能和效率</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百一十八、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你平时如何评测你写的前端代码的性能和效率。</span></strong></p>
<p>Chrome&nbsp;DevTools<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Timeline</span>:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是用来排查应用性能瓶颈的最佳工具。</span></p>
<p>Chrome&nbsp;DevTools<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>Audits:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对页面性能进行检测，根据测试的结果进行优化。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">第三方工具</span>Yslow<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span></p>
<p><a href="http://www.cnblogs.com/-simon/p/5883336.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cnblogs</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">simon</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">p</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/5883336</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.html</span></a></p>
<p><a href="http://blog.csdn.net/ivan0609/article/details/45508365"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">csdn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">net</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ivan</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">0609/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">artide</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">details</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/45508365</span></a></p>
<p><a href="http://www.wtoutiao.com/p/1305TZW.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">wtoutiao</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">p</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1305</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">TZW.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百一十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何优化页面，加快页面的加载速度</span>(<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">至少</span><span style="font-family: Arial">5</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">条</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;优化图片资源的格式和大小</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;开启网络压缩</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;使用浏览器缓存</p>
<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;减少重定向请求</p>
<p class="45">(5)&nbsp;使用<span style="text-decoration: underline">CDN</span>存储静态资源</p>
<p class="45">(6)&nbsp;减少<span style="text-decoration: underline">DNS</span>查询次数</p>
<p class="45">(7)&nbsp;压缩<span style="text-decoration: underline">css</span>和<span style="text-decoration: underline">js</span>内容</p>
<p>详细参见：<a href="http://www.mahaixiang.cn/wyzz/1589.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">mahaixiang</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">wyzz</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1589</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百二十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">怎么保证多人开发进行内存泄漏的检查（内存分析</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">工具）</span></strong></p>
<p>1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span>xcode<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里面的</span>Analyze<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行静态分析</span></p>
<p>build setting ----<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">》 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">automa ----</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">》 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">mrc</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">环境</span></p>
<p>product ----<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">》 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">analyze ----</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">》</span><span style="font-family: Arial">command + R</span></p>
<p>2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为避免不必要的麻烦，多人开发的时候尽量使用</span> ARC</p>
<p>内存泄露：</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考：</span>http://blog.csdn.net/panda_bear/article/details/8009421</p>
<p class="46">一百二十一、&nbsp;<strong>前后端</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">性能如何调优？</span></strong></p>
<p>1.	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">减少</span>http<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求数</span></p>
<p>2.	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用内容分布式网络</span></p>
<p>3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">给头部添加</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个失效期或者</span>Cache一Control</p>
<p>4.	Gzip<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">压缩组件</span></p>
<p>5.	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把样式表放在前面</span></p>
<p>6.	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把脚本放在最后</span></p>
<p>7.	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不使用</span>CSS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">表达式</span></p>
<p>8.	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用外部的</span>JavaScript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS</span></p>
<p>9.	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">减少</span>DNS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的查询</span></p>
<p>10. <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">缩小</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JavaScript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CSS</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参</span>考：http://blog.csdn.net/sonta/article/details/44454787</p>
<p class="46">一百二十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">浏览器</span></strong>http<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">请求过多怎么解决？</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;合并<span style="text-decoration: underline">JS、CSS</span>文件</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;合并图片css&nbsp;sprite</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 微软雅黑">使用</span> Image&nbsp;maps</p>
<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">data</span>嵌入图片：如<span style="text-decoration: underline">base</span>64</p>
<p class="45">(5)&nbsp;使用<span style="text-decoration: underline">CDN</span>，减少<span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span>请求头</p>
<p class="42"><strong><em>Web</em></strong><strong><em><span style="font-family: 微软雅黑">安全</span></em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百二十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你所了解到的</span></strong>Web<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">攻击技术</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">XSS</span>攻击</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">CSRF</span>攻击</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;网络劫持攻击</p>
<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;控制台注入代码</p>
<p class="45">(5)&nbsp;钓鱼</p>

<div class="Section2">
<p class="46">一百二十四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何防止</span></strong>XSS<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">攻击？</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;将前端输出数据都进行转义</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将输出的字符串中的</span>\<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">反斜杠进行转义</span></p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;从<span style="text-decoration: underline">url</span>中获取的信息，防止方法是由后端获取，在前端转义后再行输出</p>
<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;使用<span style="text-decoration: underline">cookie</span>的<span style="text-decoration: underline">HttpOnly</span>属性，保护好<span style="text-decoration: underline">cookie</span></p>
<p>详细参见：<a href="http://blog.csdn.net/fengyinchao/article/details/52303118"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">csdn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">net</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">fengyinchao</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">article</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">details</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/52303118</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百二十五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">项目中有没有用过加密，哪种加密算法？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">项目中没有用过，但我了解几个加密算法：</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">RSA</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加密</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">MD</span>5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加密</span></p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">SHA</span>256<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加密</span></p>
<p class="46">一百二十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">聊</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">聊网页的分段传输与渲染</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">从下面几个方面说：</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;CHUNKED编码</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;BIGPIPE</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">分段传输与</span>bigpipe<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">适用场景</span></p>

<p class="46">一百二十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">百度移动端首页秒开是如何做到的？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">从几个方面优化：</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">静态文件放置</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">缓存</span></p>

<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">缓存</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">DOM</span></p>
<p class="45">(5)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: MingLiU">使用</span> iconfont</p>
<p class="45">(6)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">卡片的异步加载与缓存</span></p>
<p class="45">(7)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不在首屏的就要异步化</span></p>
<p class="45">(8)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">少量静态文件的域名</span></p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section3">
<p class="46">一百二十八、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">前端速度统计（性能统计）如何做？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">回答下面的两个问题：</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">网站都有哪些指标？</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如何统计自己网站的这些指标？</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="https://segmentfault.eom/a/1190000005869953"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">segmentfault</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">eom</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1190000005869953</span></a></p>
<p class="51"><strong><em>架构</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百二十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如果让你来制作</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个访问量很高的大型网站，你会如何来管理所有</span></strong>css<span style="font-family: MingLiU">、</span>js<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">文件、图片？</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">遵循自定的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">套</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">CSS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">JS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和图片文件和文件夹命名规范</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">依托采用的前端工程化工具，依照工具脚手架规范</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">gulp</span>, <span style="text-decoration: underline">webpack</span>, <span style="text-decoration: underline">grunt</span>, <span style="text-decoration: underline">yeoman</span>)</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">依据采用的框架规范</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">Vue</span>, <span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span>, <span style="text-decoration: underline">jQuery</span>)</p>
<p class="46">一百三十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如果没有框架、怎么搭建你的项目</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用原生</span>JS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">自己尝试搭建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>MVC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">架构：</span></p>
<p>(1)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">基本模块</span></p>
<p>common:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">公共的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件，下面的各模块都会用到</span></p>
<p>config:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">配置模块，解决框架的配置问题</span></p>
<p>startup:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">启动模块，解决框架和</span>Servlet<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如何进行整合的问题</span></p>
<p>plugin:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">插件模块，插件机制的实现，提供</span>IPlugin<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的抽象实现</span></p>
<p>routing:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">路由模块，解决请求路径的解析问题，提供了</span> IRoute<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的抽象实现和基本实现</span></p>
<p>controller:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">控制器模块，解决的是如何产生控制器</span></p>
<p>model:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">视图模型模块，解决的是如何绑定方法的参数</span></p>
<p>action: action<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模块，解决的是如何调用方法以及方法返回的结果，提供了</span>IActionResult<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">抽象实现和基本实现</span></p>
<p>view:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">视图模块，解决的是各种视图引擎和框架的适配</span></p>
<p>filter:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">过滤器模块，解决是执行</span>Action,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回</span>IActionResult<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">前后的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">AOP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">功能，提供了 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">IFilter </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的抽象实现以及基本实现 </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">扩展模块</span>filters：一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些</span>IFilter&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的实现</span> </p>
<p>results&nbsp;:―<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IActionResult</span>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的实现</span> </p>
<p>routes&nbsp;:―<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些</span><span style="font-family: Arial">IRoute</span>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的实现</span> </p>
<p>plugins:—<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些</span> IPlugin&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的实现</span></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section4">&nbsp;</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section5">
<p class="46">一百三十一、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">在选择框架的时候要从哪方面入手</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">影响团队技术选型有很多因素，如技术组成，新技术，新框架，语言及发布等。为了更好的</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">考量不同的因素，需要列出重要的象限，如开发效率、团队喜好，依次来决定哪个框架更适</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">合当前的团队和项目。上线时间影响框架选择，不要盲目替换现有框架。</span></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;jQuery</p>
<p>项目功能比较简单。并不需要做成一个单页面应用，就不需要<span style="text-decoration: underline">MV</span>*框架。项目是一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个遗留</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">系统。与其使用其他框架来替换，不如留着以后重写项目。</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;AngularJS</p>
