<p>当我们在制作一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个应用，它对性能要求不是很高的时候，那么我们应该选择开发速度更快的</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术栈</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">AngularJS</span>，她拥有混合开发能力的<span style="text-decoration: underline">ionic</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">框架。对于复杂的前端应用来说，基于</span> <span style="text-decoration: underline">Angular</span>.<span style="text-decoration: underline">js</span>应用的运行效率，仍然有大量地改进空间。<span style="text-decoration: underline">Angular</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要学习新的语言，需慎重</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">选择。</span></p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;React</p>
<p>选择<span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span>有两个原因，一是通过<span style="text-decoration: underline">Virtual</span>&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">DOM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提高运行效率，二是通过组件化提高开发效</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">率。大型项目首选。选择</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还有</span>_<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个原因是</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">：</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span>&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Native、React</span>&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">VR</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等等，可以让</span> <span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span>运行在不同的平台之上。我们还能通过<span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span>轻松编写出原生应用，还有<span style="text-decoration: underline">VR</span>应用。</p>
<p>令人遗憾的是<span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span>只是一个<span style="text-decoration: underline">View</span>层，它是为了优化<span style="text-decoration: underline">DOM</span>的操作而诞生的。为了完成一&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个完整的应用，我们还需要路由库、执行单向流库</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">、</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">web</span>&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">AP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">丨调用库、测试库、依赖管理库</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等等，为了完整搭建出</span>一个完整的<span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span>项目，我们还需要做大量的额外工作。</p>
<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;Vue.js</p>
<p>对于使用Vue.js的开发者来说，我们仍然可以使用熟悉的HTML和CSS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来编写代码。并</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">且，</span>Vue.js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也使用了</span> Virtual&nbsp;D〇M、Reactive<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">及组件化的思想，可以让我们集中精力于编写</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用，而不是应用的性能。</span></p>
<p>对于没有<span style="text-decoration: underline">Angular</span>和<span style="text-decoration: underline">React</span>经验的团队，并且规模不大的前端项目来说，<span style="text-decoration: underline">Vue</span>.<span style="text-decoration: underline">js</span>是一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个非常</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">好的选择。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/25194137"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhuanlan</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhihu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">p</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/25194137</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百三十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">聊</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">聊前端模板与渲染</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;页面级的渲染，后端模板</p>
<p>如<span style="text-decoration: underline">smarty</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这种方式的特点是展示数据快，直接后端拼装好数据与模板，展现到用户面前，</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">SEO</span>友好。</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;异步的请求与新增模板，前端模板</p>
<p>如<span style="text-decoration: underline">Mustache</span>, <span style="text-decoration: underline">ArtTemplate</span>,前端解析模板的引擎的语法，与后端解析模板引擎语法一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">致。</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这样就达到了</span>一份<span style="text-decoration: underline">HTML</span>前后端一起使用的效果。</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000005916423"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">segmentfault</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1190000005916423</span></a></p>
<p><span style="text-decoration: underline">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><strong><em>混合开发</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百三十三、&nbsp;<strong>UIWebView<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JavaScript</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">之间是怎么交互的？</span></strong></p>
<p>UlWebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><a href="http://lib.csdn.net/base/ios"><span style="text-decoration: underline">i</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">〇</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">S</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">&nbsp;</span></a>SDK<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中渲染网面的控件，在显示网页的时候，我们可以</span><span style="font-family: Arial">hack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">网页 然后显示想显示的内容。其中就要用至</span><a href="http://lib.csdn.net/base/javascript"><span style="text-decoration: underline">JavaScript</span></a><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的知识，而</span>UlWebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">javascript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">交互的 方法就是 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">stringByEvaluatingJavaScriptFromString</span>:</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有了这个方法我们可以通过</span>objc<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">javascript</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以注入</span>javascript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>UIWebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span><a href="http://lib.csdn.net/base/ios"><span style="text-decoration: underline">iOS</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">&nbsp;</span></a>SDK<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中渲染网面的控件，在显示网页的时候，我们可以</span><span style="font-family: Arial">hack</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">网页 然后显示想显示的内容。其中就要用至</span><a href="http://lib.csdn.net/base/javascript"><span style="text-decoration: underline">JavaScript</span></a><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的知识，而</span>UIWebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">javascript</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">交互的 方法就是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">stringByEvaluatingJavaScriptFromString</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有了这个方法我们可以通过</span>objc<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">javascript</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以注入</span> javascript</p>
<p>Js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〇</span>C<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法原理就是利用</span>UIWebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">重定向请求，传</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些命令到我们的</span> UIWebView,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>UIWebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>delegate<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的方法中接收这些命令，并根据命令执行相应的</span>objc <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法。这样就相当于在</span>javascript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中调用</span>objc<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的方法。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>android<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中，我们有固有组件</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webview</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">经过设置可以让它支持我们的</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的渲染，然 后在代码中设置</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>WebViewClient/WebChromeClient)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">让应用跳转页面时在本</span>webview<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中跳 转，通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webview.loadurl</span>&nbsp;(String&nbsp;str)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法可以在需要的地方加载我们前端的页面或者调用</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">前端所定义的方法</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>wv.loadUrl("javascript:sendDataToAndroid('<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">我是来自</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的呦，你看到了 吗</span><span style="font-family: Arial">')");</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">），我们再通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JavascriptInterface</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">接口设置我们前端和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">android</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通讯的标识，</span></p>
<p>wv.addJavascriptInterface(new&nbsp;MJavascriptInterface(getApplicationContext()), "WebViewFunc");</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这样前端就可以在页面上调用我们的方法了，</span>funl<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法是在</span>android<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中定义的</span> Window.WebViewFunc.fun1 ();</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">总之，前端和</span>android<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者</span>ios<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行结合开发，我们称之为混合开发，原理就是在原生</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的开发语言中，我们提供了</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个组件</span>webview<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这个组件就是我们的原生语言的浏览器，但</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是我们得自行设置让其能够完美支持我们的应用，需要设置对应的标识，然后连接起来，我</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">们称之为</span> JavascriptInterfac<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百三十四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">混合开发桥接</span></strong>api<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">是怎么调用的，需要引入类库嘛？</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">调用的对象是什么？</span></strong></p>
<p>Hybrid<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">框架结构</span></p>
<p>HyBrid&nbsp;App&nbsp;= H5 App&nbsp;+ Native&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">框架</span></p>
<p>H5App<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用来实现功能逻辑和页面渲染</span> Native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">框架提供</span><span style="font-family: Arial">WebView</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和设备接口供</span>H5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方案</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">重混合应用，在开发原生应用的基础上，嵌入</span>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">但是整体的架构使用</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原生应用提供，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般这样的开发由</span>Native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发人员和</span>Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">前端开发人员组成。</span>Native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发人</span></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section6">
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">员会写好基本的架构以及</span>API<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">让</span>Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发人员开发界面以及大部分的渲染。保证到交互设</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">计，以及开发都有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个比较折中的效果出来，优化得好也会有很棒的效果。</span></p>
<p>Hybrid&nbsp;App<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术发展的早期，</span>Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的运行性能成为主要瓶颈！</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为解决性能问题</span>Hybrid&nbsp;App<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">走向</span><span style="font-family: Arial">‘‘</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">重混</span><span style="font-family: Arial">”</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过多</span>WebView:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实现流畅的多页加载和专场动画。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span>Navtive&nbsp;UI<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件：框架、菜单、日期等。</span></p>
<p>‘‘<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">重混</span><span style="font-family: Arial">”</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的优缺点 优点：</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提升了运行性能</span> 一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增强了交互体验</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">缺点</span>一</p>
<p>一Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>Native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术交叉混杂</span> 一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要同时掌握</span>Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>Native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术，学习难度增加</span> 一一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个页面有</span>Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件也有</span>Native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件，编程调试困难</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要引入各自需要的各种依赖工具</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方案二：轻混合应用，使用</span>PhoneGap、AppCan<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之类的中间件，以</span>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">作为用</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">户界面层，以</span>Javascript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">作为基本逻辑，以及和中间件通讯，再由中间件访问底层</span>API<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的方</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">式，进行应用开发。这种架构</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般会非常依赖</span>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">层的性能。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">随着时代的发展，手机硬件、浏览器技术、无线网络技术都得到了大幅的提升，</span>H5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">已经可</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以支持复杂应用，并拥有良好的运行性能。使用轻混方案的</span>App<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也越来越多。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目前我们要学习的</span>Hybrid&nbsp;App<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发就是方案二，使用</span>H5+Js+Native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">框架开发当前轻</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">混合应用。</span></p>
<p>Phonegap&nbsp;引入phonegap.js&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者</span> cordova.js,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象为</span> navigator Dcloud<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">引入引入</span><span style="font-family: Arial">mui.js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者其他的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件，对象为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">plus apiloud</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">引入各种第三方插件，对象为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">api</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">顺变提</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下，</span>2012<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">年</span><span style="font-family: Arial">8</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">月，微信公众平台的上线，重新定义了移动应用：移动应用 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">=</span>Iphone&nbsp;App&nbsp;+ Android&nbsp;App&nbsp;+ <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">微信 </span>App</p>
<p class="46">一百三十五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">说</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">下你对支付，推送（远程，本地</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">）</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的理解</span></strong></p>
<p>消息的推送主要有两种：</p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种是本地推送，主要应用在系统的工具中，例如：闹钟，生日提醒等；实现本地推</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">送需要以下三个步骤，</span></p>
<ol>
<li>实例化一个本地推送对象</li>
<li>设置通知对象的各个属性</li>
<li>添加本地推送对象</li>

</ol>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种是远程消息推送，主要应用联网设备的信息推送，例如：邮件，各种软件的广告</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或优惠信息的推送。远程推送比较复杂，需要使用开发者账号进行申请证书，获得实</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">现推送功能的配置文件，所以想要实现远程推送功能，必须要有开发者账号并且生成</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">配置文件</span></p>
<ol>
<li>完成证书的申请和<span style="text-decoration: underline">Xcode</span>的配置</li>
<li>在<span style="text-decoration: underline">Demo</span>中注册远程服务对象，并设置其代理</li>
<li>找一个简单的<span style="text-decoration: underline">App</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器进行消息推送（推荐使用</span>:<span style="text-decoration: underline">PushMeBaby</span>, <span style="text-decoration: underline">gitup</span>网站上就有）</li>
<li><span style="font-family: 微软雅黑">运行</span> PushMeBaby</li>

</ol>
<p class="47">参考网址：<a href="http://blog.csdn.net/u014642572/article/details/26857717"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://blog.csdn.net/u014642572/article/details/26857717</span></a></p>
<p class="49">远程推送流程图如下</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="46">一百三十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">什么是代理和通知，写</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">下他们基本的实现方式</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>代理</strong>：“一对一”，对同一个协议，一个对象只能设置一个代理delegate</p>
<p>六个步骤：</p>
<p class="45">1．声明一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个协议</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定义代理方法</span></p>
<p class="45">2．遵循协议</p>
<p class="45">3．设置一个代理对象</p>
<p class="45">4．调用代理方法</p>
<p class="45">5．给代理赋值</p>
<p class="45">6．实现代理方法</p>
<p>注意事项：</p>
<p class="45">1．单例对象不能用代理；</p>
<p class="45">2．代理执行协议方法时要使用<span style="text-decoration: underline">respondsToSelector</span>检查其代理是否符合</p>
<p>3．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议</span>(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">检查对象能否响应指定的消息</span>),以避免代理在回调时因为没有实现方法而造成程序崩溃</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用场景：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">公共接口，方法较多也选择用</span>delegate<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行解耦 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">iOS</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">最常用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">tableViewDelegate</span>, textViewDelegate iOS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有很多例子比如常用的网络库</span><span style="font-family: Arial">AFNetwork</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>ASIHTTP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">库， </span><span style="font-family: Arial">UlAlertView</span>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">类。</span></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>
<p><strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通知</span></strong><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对</span>一&nbsp;一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对多</span>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">传值</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">四个步骤：</span></p>
<p class="45">1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">发送通知</span></p>
<p class="45">2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">创建监听者</span></p>
<p class="45">3．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">接收通知</span></p>
<p class="45">4．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">移除监听者</span></p>
<p>使用场景：</p>
<p>1一很多控制器都需要知道一个事件，应该用通知；</p>
<p>2 一相隔多层的两个控制器之间跳转</p>
<p>注意事项：</p>
<p class="45">1．一旦接收消息的对象多了，就难以控制了，可能有你不希望的对象接收了消息并做了处理</p>
<p class="45">2．创建了观察者，在<span style="text-decoration: underline">dealloc</span>里面一定要移除；</p>
<p class="45">&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>Block</strong><strong>&nbsp;</strong>:&nbsp;&nbsp;Block<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span>i<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〇</span>S4.0+<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>Mac&nbsp;OS&nbsp;X 10.6+引<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进的对</span>C<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">语言的扩展，用来实现匿名函数的特性。</span>Blocks<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">语法块代码以闭包得形式将各种内容进行传递，可以是代码，可以是数组</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">无所不能。闭包就是能够读取其它函数内部变量的函数。就是在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">段请求连续代码中可以看</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">到调用参数（如发送请求</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和响应结果。所以采用</span>Block<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术能够抽象出很多共用函数，提</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">高了代码的可读性，可维护性，封装性。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用场景：</span></p>
<p>—:&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">动</span>画</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">二：数据请求回调</span> </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">三：枚举回调</span> </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">四：多线程</span>gcd</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">注意事项：</span>Iblock<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要注意防止循环引用</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考网址：</span><a href="http://www.cnblogs.com/wenboliu/articles/5422033.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cnblogs</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">wenboliu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">articles</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/5422033</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百三十七、&nbsp;<strong>UIViewController <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的生命周期</span></strong></p>
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>alloc init<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">分配内存，初始化</span><span style="font-family: Arial">controller.</span></p>
<p>2．loadView （loadView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法默认实现</span><span style="font-family: Arial">[super</span>&nbsp;loadView]</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果在初始化</span>controller<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">吋指定了</span><span style="font-family: Arial">xib</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件名，就会根据传入的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">xib</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件名加载对应的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">xib</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件，如果 没传</span><span style="font-family: Arial">xib</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件名，默认会加载跟</span><span style="font-family: Arial">controller</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同名的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">xib</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件，如果没找到相关联的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">xib</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件，就会创建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个空白的</span>UIView,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">然后赋給</span><span style="font-family: Arial">controller</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">view</span>）</p>
<p>3．viewDidLoad&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当</span><span style="font-family: Arial">loadView</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">创建完</span><span style="font-family: Arial">view</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之后，此吋</span><span style="font-family: Arial">view</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">已经完成加载了，会调用 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">viewDidLoad</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法；</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般我会在这里做界面上的初始化操作，比如添加按钮，子视图，等等</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>4．viewWillAppear&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当</span><span style="font-family: Arial">view</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">load</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">完之后，将要显示在屏幕之前会调用这个方法，在重写这些方法吋候最好先调用</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下系统的方法之后在做操作。）</span></p>
<p>5．viewDidAppear&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当</span><span style="font-family: Arial">view</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">已经在屏幕上显示出来之后，会调用这个方法，当</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个视图被移除屏幕并且销毁的吋候）</span></p>
<p>6．viewWillDisappear&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当视图将要从屏幕上移除吋候调用</span>&nbsp;)</p>
<p>7．viewDidDisappear&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当视图已经从屏幕上移除吋候调用</span>&nbsp;)</p>
<p>8．Dealloc (view<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">被销毁吋候调用，如果是手动管理内存的话，需要释放掉之前在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">init</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">viewDidLoad</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中分配的内存（类似</span><span style="font-family: Arial">alloc,new,copy) ; dealloc</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法不能甶我们主动调用，必须等引用计数为</span>0<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">吋候甶系统调用</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>9．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考网址：</span><a href="http://www.cnblogs.com/wujy/p/5822329.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">&nbsp;http://www.cnblogs.eom/wujy/p/5822329.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百三十八、&nbsp;rem<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">布局字体太大怎么处理？</span></strong></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般情况下我们设置了</span>html<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">根节点的字体大小作为</span>rem<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">单位的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个基本标准，那么我</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">们可以紧接着在</span>body<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签内设置</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个字体大小为该应用的基本字体大小</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">针对于</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些机型如果</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开始就显示的字体不正常，我们可以通过判断机型然后加载不同的样式</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〈</span>script&nbsp;language="javascript"&gt;</p>
<p>window.onload&nbsp;= function() { </p>
<p>alert(“1”);</p>
<p>var&nbsp;u&nbsp;= navigator.userAgent;</p>
<p>if(u.index<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〇</span>f('Android') &gt; <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span>1 || &nbsp;u.indexOf('Linux') &gt; <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span>1) { //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">安卓手机</span></p>
<p>alert("<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">安卓手机</span>")<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">；</span></p>
<p>} else&nbsp;if(u.index<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〇</span>f('iPhone') &gt; 一1) { //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">苹果手机</span> </p>
<p>alert("<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">苹果手机</span>")<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">；</span></p>
<p>} else&nbsp;if(u.index<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〇</span>f('Windows&nbsp;Phone') &gt; 一1) { //winphone<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">手机 </span>		&nbsp;&nbsp;		&nbsp;&nbsp;alert("winphone&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">手机</span>")<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">；</span></p>
<p>}</p>
<p>}</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〈</span>/script&gt;</p>
<p class="46">一百三十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何调用原生的接口？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">首先你得选择</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个合适的框架作为自己的基础，以</span>Dcloud<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为例，页面中</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定要存在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个事件，</span>plusready, plusready<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实际上是原生将桥接</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">注入到页面中的容器，进行任何方法</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用的时候都在</span>plusready<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之后。所有</span>api<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法全部都托管在了</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>plus<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象中。使用语法</span> plus.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模块名称</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">具体方法</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参数，</span>callback)</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当我们需要打开系统相册的时候，可以这样做：</span></p>
<p>Gallery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模块管理系统相册，支持从相册中选择图片或视频文件、保存图片或视频文</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">件到相册等功能。通过</span>plus.gallery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">获取相册管理对象。打开相册</span>plus.gallery.pick<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行打开，选取多个图片</span>{multiple:true,maximum:9,system:false}</p>
<p class="46">一百四十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">微信支付怎么做？说说流程</span></strong></p>
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">申请微信公众号及支付功能申请：根据公众号申请流程申请即可。</span></p>
<p>2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">获取商户支付配置信息及支付</span><a href="http://lib.csdn.net/base/softwaretest"><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">测试</span></span></a><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">配置：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支付授权目录最多可以配置三个域名，测试授权目录只可以</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个，这里需要</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">注意的是域名大小写必须要网站</span>URL—<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">致，否则会无法通过授权，提示支付请求的 </span>URL<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不合法。另外，测试支付的微信号必须加到测试白名单，否则无法进行支付测</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">试。</span></p>
<p>3．H5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">页面发起支付请求，请求生成支付订单</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">获取用户授权（获取用户的</span>openid)</p>
<p>4．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用统</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下单</span>API<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">生成预付单</span></p>
<p>5．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">生成</span>JSAPI<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">页面调用的支付参数并签名，注意时间戳</span>timeStamp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span>32<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">位字符串</span></p>
<p>6．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回支付参数</span>prepay—id,paySign<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参数的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">html</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文本给前端。</span></p>
<p>7．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">微信浏览器自动调起支付</span>JSAPI<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">接口支付，提示用户输入密码。</span></p>
<p>8．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">确认支付，输入密码，提交支付。</span></p>
<p>9．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">步通知商户支付结果，商户收到通知返回确认信息。</span></p>
<p>10．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回支付结果，并发微信消息提示。</span></p>
<p>11．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">展示支付信息给用户，跳转到支付结果页面。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百四十一、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">混合开发的注意点</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增强</span>WebView&nbsp;:&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原生</span>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">基本是</span>PC<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">平台浏览器内核的移植，但对于移动场景并不完全适合，各种硬件</span>API<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">得不到</span>HTML5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原生支持。因此对于</span>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的种种</span>Hack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">增强应运而生，甚至出现了基于增强</span>WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供第三方服务的。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">路由：应用内跳转由于加入了</span> WebView<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而变得复杂起来，同时由于组件化、模块化带来的问</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">题，路由也成为人们讨论的重点。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">缓存：移动网络条件差，为了用户体验，必须要做资源缓存和预加载。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通信：即</span>HTML5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>Native<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之间的通信。利用系统提供的桥接</span>API<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以实现，不过在应用上还</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有着</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些坑点和安全问题。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百四十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">说说你对手机平台的安装包后缀的理解</span></strong></p>
<p>Android：**apk </p>
<p>Ios：**ipa</p>
<p>Windows：	wp7 wp8<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的是</span>xap&nbsp;&nbsp;wp8.1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以后用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">8.1</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开发的是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">appx</span></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section7">
<p class="42"><strong><em>NodeJS</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百四十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">谈谈你对</span></strong>Socket<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">编程的理解及实现原理</span></strong><span style="font-family: 宋体">，</span>Socket <strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">之间是怎么通讯的</span></strong></p>
<p>A<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Socket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定义</span></p>
<p>Socket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是进程通讯的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种方式，即调用这个网络库的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些</span>API<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数实现分布在不同主机的相</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">关进程之间的数据交换。几个定义：</span>IP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">地址：即依照</span>TCP/IP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">协议分配给本地主机的网络地</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">址，两个进程要通讯，任</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进程首先要知道通讯对方的位置，即对方的</span>IP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">端口号：用来辨</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">别本地通讯进程，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个本地的进程在通讯时均会占用</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个端口号，不同的进程端口号不同，</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因此在通讯前必须要分配</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个没有被访问的端口号。连接：指两个进程间的通讯链路。</span></p>
<p>B<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实现原理</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>TCP/IP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">网络应用中，通信的两个进程间相互作用的主要模式是客户</span>/<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>Client/ Server, C/S)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模式，即客户向服务器发出服务请求，服务器接收到请求后，提供相应的服务。客户</span>/<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器模式的建立基于以下两点：首先，建立网络的起因是网络中软硬件资源、运算能力和信息不均等，需要共享，从而造就拥有众多资源的主机提供服务，资源较少的客 户请求服务这</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">非对等作用。其次，网间进程通信完全是异步的，相互通信的进程间既不存</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在父子关系，又不共享内存缓冲区，因此需要</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种机制为希望通信的进程间建立联系，为二</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">者的数据交换提供同步，这就是基于客户</span>/<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器模式的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">TCP/IP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>C<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通讯过程</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器端：其过程是首先服务器方要先启动，并根据请求提供相应服务：（</span>1)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">打开</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通信</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通道并告知本地主机，它愿意在某</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">公认地址上的某端</span>□(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如</span>FTP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的端口可能为</span>21)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">接收客</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">户请求；</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>2)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等待客户请求到达该端口；</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>3)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">接收到客户端的服务请求时，处理该请求并</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">发送应答信号。接收到并发服务请求，要激活</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">新进程来处理这个客户请求（如</span>UNIX<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">系统</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中用</span>fork<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span>exec)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">新进程处理此客户请求，并不需要对其它请求作出应答。服务完成后，</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">关闭此新进程与客户的通信链路，并终止。</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>4)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回第</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>2)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">步，等待另</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">客户请求。</span>（5）<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">关闭服务器客户端：（</span>1)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">打开</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通信通道，并连接到服务器所在主机的特定端口；</span>(2)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">向服务器发服务请求报文，等待并接收应答；继续提出请求</span>......<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">3)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求结束后关闭通信通道并终止。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">从上面所描述过程可知：</span>（1）<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">客户与服务器进程的作用是非对称的，因</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">此代码不同。</span>（2）<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务器进程</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般是先启动的。只要系统运行，该服务进程</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">直存在，直到正常或强迫终止。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.zhihu.com/question/29637351"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhihu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">question</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/29637351</span></a></p>
<p><a href="http://blog.csdn.net/panker2008/article/details/46502783?ref=myread"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">csdn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">net</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">panker</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">2008/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">article</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">details</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/46502783?</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ref=myread</span></a></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section8">
<p class="46">一百四十四、&nbsp;<strong>WEB</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">应用从服务器主动推送</span></strong><strong>Data</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">到客户端有哪些方</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">式？</span></strong></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般的服务器</span>Push<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术包括：</span></p>
<p>1)&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">基于</span>AJAX<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的长轮询</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>long一polling)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方式，服务器</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Hold</span>—<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">段时间后再返回信息；</span></p>
<p>2)&nbsp;HTTP&nbsp;Streaming,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>iframe<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〈</span>script<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〉</span>#<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">签完成数据的传输；</span></p>
<p>3)&nbsp;TCP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">长连接</span></p>
<p>4)&nbsp;HTML5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">新引入的</span>WebSocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以实现服务器主动发送数据至网页端，它和</span>HTTP— <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">样，是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个基于</span>HTTP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的应用层协议，跑的是</span>TCP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所以本质上还是个长连接，双向通信，</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">意味着服务器端和客户端可以同时发送并响应请求，而不再像</span>HTTP<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的请求和响应。</span></p>
<p>5)&nbsp;nodejs<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>http://socket.io<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">它是</span>websocket<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>一^^<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">开源实现，对不支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">websocket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的浏 览器降级成</span>comet&nbsp;/ ajax<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">轮询，</span>http://socket.io<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的良好封装使代码编写非常容易。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上述的</span> 1 <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">统称为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">comet</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">comet</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参考：</span><a href="http://www.ibm.com/developerworks/cn/"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ibm</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">developerworks</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span></a>&nbsp;web/wa一lo一comet/</p>
<p class="46">一百四十五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">简述</span></strong><strong>Node</strong><strong>.</strong><strong>js</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的适用场景？</span></strong></p>
<p>IIO <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">密集而非计算密集的情景；高并发微数据（比如账号系统）的情景。特别是高并发，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Node.js </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的性能随并发数量的提高而衰减的现象相比其他 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">server </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">都有很明显的优势。</span></p>
<p><strong>Bad Use Cases</strong></p>
<p>1．CPU heavy apps <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（高</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CPU</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">消耗的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">app</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>2．Simple CRUD / HTML apps <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（简单的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">CRUD / HTML apps</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>3．NoSQL + Node.js + Buzzword Bullshit <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">NoSQL + Node.js + </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">各种扯淡的时髦词汇）</span></p>
<p><strong>Good Use Cases</strong></p>
<p>1．JSON API</p>
<p>2．Single page apps <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（单页面</span><span style="font-family: Arial">app</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span></p>
<p>3．Shelling out to unix tools <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">unix</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">工具的脚本化调用）</span></p>
<p>4．Streaming data <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（流数据）</span></p>
<p>5．Soft Realtime Applications <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（软件实时程序）</span></p>
<p class="46">一百四十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">什么是</span></strong>HTTPS<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，做什么用的呢？如何开启</span></strong>HTTPS<strong>?</strong></p>
<p>1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">什么是</span>HTTPS</p>
<p>https<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span>http<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的加密版本，是在</span>http<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求的基础上，采用</span>ssl<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行加密传输。</span></p>
<p>2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">做什么用</span></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section9">
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加密数据，反劫持，</span>SEO </p>
<p>3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如何开启</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">生成私钥与证书，配置</span>nginx,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">重启</span>nginx<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">看效果</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000006199237"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">segmentfault</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">c</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">om</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1190000006199237</span></a>?utm_source=tuicool&amp;utm_medium=referral</p>
<p class="46">一百四十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你们原来公司如何发送的新消息推送</span>?</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（参考：）一般的服务器</span>Push<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术包括：</span></p>
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">基于</span> AJAX <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的长轮询（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">long</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">polling</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）方式，服务器</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Hold</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一段时间后再返回信息；</span></p>
<p>2．HTTP Streaming<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">iframe</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">&lt;script&gt;</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">标签完成数据的传输；</span></p>
<p>3．TCP <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">长连接</span></p>
<p>4．HTML5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">新引入的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">WebSocket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，可以实现服务器主动发送数据至网页端，它和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一样，是一个基于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的应用层协议，跑的是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">TCP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，所以本质上还是个长连接，双向通信，意味着服务器端和客户端可以同时发送并响应请求，而不再像</span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的请求和响应</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上述的</span>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">统称为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">comet</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">技术，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Comet</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：基于 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">HTTP </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">长连接的“服务器推”技术前些日子给项目网站加了后台通知的实时推送到前端显示，用的是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">nodejs</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http://socket.io</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，它是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">websocket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的一个开源实现，对不支持</span><span style="font-family: Arial">websocket</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的浏览器降级成</span><span style="font-family: Arial">comet / ajax </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">轮询，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">http://socket.io</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的良好封装使代码编写非常容易。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百四十八、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何用</span></strong>NodeJS<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">搭建中间层？</span></strong></p>
<p>（如下图）&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">最上端是服务端，就是我们常说的后端。后端对于我们来说，就是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个接口的集合，服务端提供各种各样的接口供我们使用。因为有</span>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">层，也不用局限是什么形式的服务。对于后端开发来说，他们只用关心业务代码的接口实现。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务端下面是</span>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用。</span></p>
<p>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用中有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">层</span>Model&nbsp;Proxy<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与服务端进行通讯。这</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">层主要目前是抹平我们对不同接口</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的调用方式，封装</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些</span>view<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">层需要的</span>Model<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">层还能轻松实现原来</span>vmcommon,tms&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">引用淘宝内容管理系统）等需求。</span></p>
<p>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">层要使用什么框架由开发者自己决定。不过推荐使用</span>express&nbsp;+&nbsp;xTemplate<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的组合，</span> xTemplate<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">能做到前后端公用。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">怎么用</span>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">大家自己决定，但是令人兴奋的是，我们终于可以使用</span>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">轻松实现我们想要的输出方式</span> JSON/JSONP/RESTful/HTML/BigPipe/Comet/Socket/<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同步、异步，想怎么整就怎么整</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">完全根据你的场景决定。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器层在我们这个架构中没有变化，也不希望因为引入</span>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">改变你以前在浏览器中开发的认知。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">引入</span>Node<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只是把本该就前端控制的部分交由前端掌控。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="http://blog.csdn.net/u011413061/article/details/50294263"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://blog.csdn.net/u011413061/article/details/50294263</span></a></p>
<p class="51"><strong><em>组件设计</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百四十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">设计</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个弹框组件，组件宽度为屏幕高度的</span>50%<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">， 宽度为屏幕宽度的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">80%</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，水平垂直居中。</span></strong><strong>弹窗</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">组件有</span> </strong>header<strong>, </strong>body<strong>, </strong>footer<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">三部分，</span></strong>header<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中有标题，可定制，</span></strong>body<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">区域，</span></strong>footer<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">区域有确定和取消按钮，可定制两个按钮的文字内容，组件外的内容有遮罩，点击遮罩和取消按钮时关闭弹框，参照下图。</span></strong><strong>（类似于</strong><strong>layer<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的弹出层插件</span></strong><strong>）</strong></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section10">
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用面向对象封装插件较为合适</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">构造函数的参数有</span>header<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的标题及</span>body<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">内容和按钮文字内容</span> </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">封装的方法应该有</span>show, hide,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在点击遮罩和取消按钮时调用</span>hide<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法</span> </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">并且</span>hide<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>show<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法应该有返回值以供判断。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百五十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">实现</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个手势滑动轮播图组件。效果参考：</span></strong><strong>https</strong><strong>://</strong><strong>static</strong><strong>.</strong><strong>xiaohongchun</strong><strong>.</strong><strong>com</strong><strong>/</strong><strong>goods</strong><strong>/4514</strong><strong>&nbsp;</strong><strong>(</strong><strong>请在手机里打开）</strong></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>详细参考：<a href="http://www.jb51.net/article/65177.htm"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://www.jb51.net/article/65177.htm</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百五十一、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">设计基于观察者模式的事件绑定机制</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">观察者模式</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（发布</span>-订阅模式）<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的定义：</span>Observer<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的意图是定义对象之间的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（被观察者）对多（观察者）</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的关系，当</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个对象的状态发生改变时，所有依赖它的对象得到通知，并且会自动更新自己</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>JavaScript中，一般使用事件模型来替代传统的观察者模式。 </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">好处：</span> </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>1）可广泛应用于异步编程中，是一种替代传递回调函数的方案。 </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>2）可取代对象之间硬编码的通知机制，一个对象不用再显示地调用另外一个对象的某个接口。两对象轻松解耦。</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码</span>参考<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span><a href="http://blog.csdn.net/phker/article/details/6880371"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://blog.csdn.net/phker/article/details/6880371</span></a></p>
<p><a href="http://www.cnblogs.com/LuckyWinty/p/5796190.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://www.cnblogs.com/LuckyWi nty/p/5796190.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百五十二、&nbsp;jq<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">自己扩展过什么插件？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">弹出层插件、</span>pagination<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">插件、瀑布流插件、模态框插件等</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考：</span>Jquery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">插件库</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;jquery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之家</span></p>
<p class="46">一百五十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">侧滑菜单如何实现？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">主要依靠两个大的容器来模拟侧滑菜单界面和主界面，把侧滑菜单放到页面右侧看不</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">到的地方，在操作的同时，使用</span>css3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">过渡、动画或者</span>jq<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来使两个容器相对运动，实现侧滑菜单效果</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考：</span><a href="http://www.111cn.net/wy/js-ajax/99687.htm"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.111</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">net</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">wy</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">js</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ajax</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/99687</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.htm</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百五十四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">权限管理如何实现？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）前端控制：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　前端的控制比较简单，从后台获取到用户的权限之后，可以存在</span>session<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中，然后在页面加载的时候，通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">session</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cookie</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中存的权限来选择让该功能展现或者禁用。</span></p>
<p>前端实现代码<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="http://blog.csdn.net/liuweidagege/article/details/42497731"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://blog.csdn.net/liuweidagege/article/details/42497731</span></a></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）后台控制：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　仅仅依靠前端的控制是无法完美解决权限控制的问题，因为前端页面的加载过程是在浏览器中完成的，用户可以自行篡改页面；或者用户可以直接通过</span>URI<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求来获取非法权限功能。所以需要在后台实现权限控制。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　后台的控制方法也很多，比如</span>filter<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">spring</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">AOP</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等。在此选用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">springMVC</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">interceptor</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来控制。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）全局异常管理：</span></p>
<p>　　思路是在拦截器中权限校验失败时，抛出一个权限校验失败的异常，然后通过全局异常管理类来捕获并返回前端特定的格式。具体如下。</p>
<p class="46">一百五十五、&nbsp;<strong>—<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个大数组，可能存了 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">100</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">万个数字，要从其中取出 来第二大的数的下标，有什么快速的方法？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用两个变量</span>max<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">max2</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">其中</span>max<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">储存最大值，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">max2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">储存第二大值</span>；<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">初始化的时候，将数组中的第</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个元素中较大的存进</span>max<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中，较小的存进</span><span style="font-family: Arial">max2</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">然后从第三个元素</span>(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下标为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的元素开始，如果遇到的数比</span><span style="font-family: Arial">max</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">大，就让</span><span style="font-family: Arial">max2=max;max</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等于遇到的数</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">直循环，直到数组尾部</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">最后输出</span>max2</p>
<p class="43"><strong><em>单元测试</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百五十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">单个组件怎么测试性能</span></strong></p>
<p>React<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件测试框架用</span>mocha,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">测试库用官方的测试工具库，也可使用第三方库</span>Enzyme,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">建议使用第三方的。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="http://www.ruanyifeng.com/blog/2016/02/react-testing-tutorial.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ruanyifeng</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/2016/02/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">react</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">testing</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">tutorial.html</span></a>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Vue<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Unit</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">e</span>2e<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">测试工具：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="http://www.tuicool.com/articles/6vulNvR"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">tuicool</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">articles</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/6</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">vulNvR</span></a></p>
<p class="42"><strong><em>React</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百五十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">有了解过</span>React.js<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">吗？</span></strong></p>
<p>React.js <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只是一个视图库</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　（</span>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）声明式设计</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　（</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）高效：通过对</span><span style="font-family: Arial">DOM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的模拟，最大限度的减少与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">DOM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的交互。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　（</span>3<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）灵活：可以与已知的框架或库很好的配合。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　（</span>4<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）</span><span style="font-family: Arial">JSX</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">语法的扩展，不一定使用，但建议用。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　（</span>5<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）组件：构建组件，使代码更容易得到复用，能够很好地应用在大项目的开发中。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">　　（</span>6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）单向响应的数据流：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">React</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实现了单向响应的数据流，从而减少了重复代码，这也是解释了它为什么比传统数据绑定更简单。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百五十八、&nbsp;<strong>redux</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中间件</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中间件提供第三方插件的模式，自定义拦截</span>action一&gt; reducer<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的过程。变为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">action</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〉</span> middlewares 一&gt; reducer<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。这种机制可以让我们改变数据流，实现如异步</span><span style="font-family: Arial">action</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">， </span><span style="font-family: Arial">action</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">过滤，日志输出，异常报告等功能。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">常见的中间件：</span> </p>
<p>redux一logger:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供日志输出 </span></p>
<p>redux一thunk:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">处理异步操作</span></p>
<p>redux一promise:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">处理异步操作</span>，actionCreator<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的返回值是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">promise</span></p>
<p class="46">一百五十九、&nbsp;redux<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">有什么缺点</span></strong></p>
<p>1．一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个组件所需要的数据，必须甶父组件传过来，而不能像</span>flux<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中直接从</span>store<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">取。</span></p>
<p>2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个组件相关数据更新吋，即使父组件不需要用到这个组件，父组件还是会重新</span>render,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可能会 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有效率影响，或者需要写复杂的</span>shouldComponentUpdate<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行判断。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百六十、&nbsp;react<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">组件的划分业务组件技术组件？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">根据组件的职责通常把组件分为</span>UI<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件和容器组件。</span></p>
<p>UI<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件负责</span>UI<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的呈现，容器组件负责管理数据和逻辑。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">两者通过</span>React一Redux<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供</span><span style="font-family: Arial">connect</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法联系起来。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">具体使用可以参照如下链接：</span></p>
<p><a href="http://www.ruanyifeng.com/blog/2016/09/redux_tutorial_part_three_react-redux.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ruanyifeng</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/2016/09/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">redux</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">_</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">tutorial</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">_</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">part</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">_</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">three</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">_</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">react</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">redux.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百六十一、&nbsp;react<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">生命周期函数</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这个问题要考察的是组件的生命周期</span></p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">初始化阶段：</span></p>
<p>getDefaultProps:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">获取实例的默认属性</span> </p>
<p>getInitialState:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">获取每个实例的初始化状态</span> </p>
<p>componentWillMount:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件即将被装载、渲染到页面上</span> </p>
<p>render:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件在这里生成虚拟的</span>DOM<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节点 </span></p>
<p>componentDidMount:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件真正在被装载之后</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">二、</span>	<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">运行中状态：</span></p>
<p>componentWillReceiveProps:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件将要接收到属性的时候调用</span></p>
<p>shouldComponentUpdate:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件接受到新属性或者新状态的时候（可以返回</span>false,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">接收数据后不更新，阻止</span>render<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">调用，后面的函数不会被继续执行了）</span></p>
<p>componentWillUpdate:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件即将更新不能修改属性和状态</span> </p>
<p>render:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件重新描绘</span> </p>
<p>componentDidUpdate:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件已经更新</span></p>
<p>三、&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">销毁阶段：</span></p>
<p>compcomponentWillUnmount:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件即将销毁</span></p>
<p class="46">一百六十二、&nbsp;react<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">性能优化是哪个周期函数？</span></strong></p>
<p>shouldComponentUpdate<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这个方法用来判断是否需要调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">render</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法重新描绘</span><span style="font-family: Arial">dom</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。因为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">dom</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的描绘非常消耗性能，如果我们能在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">shouldComponentUpdate</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法中能够写出更优化的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">dom</span>&nbsp;diff<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">算法，可</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以极大的提高性能。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参考：</span><a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000006254212"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000006254212</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百六十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">为什么虚拟</span></strong>dom<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">会提高性能？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">虚拟</span>dom<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相当于在</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和真实</span>dom<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中间加了</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个缓存，利用</span>dom&nbsp;diff<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">算法避免了没有必要的</span>dom<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">操作，从而提髙性能。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">具体实现步骤如下：</span></p>
<p>1．&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用</span>JavaScript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象结构表示</span>DOM<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">树的结构；然后用这个树构建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个真正的</span>DOM<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">树，插到文档当中</span></p>
<p>2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">当状态变更的时候，重新构造</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">棵新的对象树。然后用新的树和旧的树进行比较，记录两棵树差异</span></p>
<p>3．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所记录的差异应用到步骤</span>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所构建的真正的</span>DOM<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">树上，视图就更新了。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考链接：</span><a href="https://www.zhihu.com/question/29504639?sort=created"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhihu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">question</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/29504639?</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">sort=created</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百六十四、&nbsp;diff<strong>&nbsp;</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">算法？</span></strong></p>
<p>1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">把树形结构按照层级分解，只比较同级元素。</span></p>
<p>2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">给列表结构的每个单元添加唯</span>_<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">key</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性，方便比较。</span></p>
<p>3)&nbsp;React<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只会匹配相同</span><span style="font-family: Arial">class</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">component (</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这里面的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">class</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">指的是组件的名字）</span></p>
<p>4)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">合并操作，调用</span>component<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">setState</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法的时候</span>,React<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将其标记为</span><span style="font-family: Arial">dirty.</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">到每</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个事件循环</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">结束</span>,React<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">检查所有标记</span><span style="font-family: Arial">dirty</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">component</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">重新绘制</span><span style="font-family: Arial">.</span></p>
<p>5)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">选择性子树渲染。开发人员可以重写</span>shouldComponentUpdate<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提高</span><span style="font-family: Arial">diff</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的性能。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考链接：</span><a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000000606216"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">segmentfault</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">19000000060621</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">6</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百六十五、&nbsp;react<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">性能优化方案</span></strong></p>
<p>1)&nbsp;重写shouldComponentUpdate来避免不必要的dom操作0</p>
<p>2)&nbsp;使用&nbsp;production 版本的react.js0</p>
<p>3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span>key<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来帮助</span>React<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">识别列表中所有子组件的最小变化。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考链接：</span></p>
<p><a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000006254212"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https://segmentfault.com/a/1</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">190000006254212</span></a>&nbsp;<a href="http://blog.csdn.net/limm33/article/details/50948869"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://blog.csdn.net/limm33/article/details/50948869</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百六十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">简述</span></strong>flux<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">思想</span></strong></p>
<p>Flux<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的最大特点，就是数据的</span>"<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">单向流动</span><span style="font-family: Arial">"</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section11">
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用户访问</span>View</p>
<p>2．View<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">发出用户的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Action</span></p>
<p>3．Dispatcher<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">收到</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Action</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">要求</span>Store<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行相应的更新 </span></p>
<p>4．Store<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">更新后，发出</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>"change"<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件</span></p>
<p>5．View<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">收到</span>"change"<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件后，更新页面</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考链接：</span><a href="http://www.ruanyifeng.com/blog/2016/01/flux.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ruanyifeng</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/2016/01/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">flux.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百六十七、&nbsp;React<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">项目用过什么脚手架？</span> </strong>Mern<strong>? </strong>Yeoman<strong>?</strong></p>
<p>Mern: MERN<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是脚手架的工具，它可以很容易地使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Mongo</span>, Express, React&nbsp;and&nbsp;NodeJS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">生成</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同构</span>JS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">应用。它最大限度地减少安装时间，并得到您使用的成熟技术来加速开发。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参考链接：</span><a href="http://www.open-open.com/lib/view/open1455953055292.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">open</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">open</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">lib</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">view</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">open</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">1455953055292</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.html</span></a></p>
<p class="42"><strong><em>Vue.js</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百六十八、&nbsp;vue<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">与</span></strong>react<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的对比，如何选型？从性能，生态圈，数据量，数据的传递上，作比较</span></strong></p>
<p>1)&nbsp;React<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>Vue<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有许多相似之处，它们都有：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span> Virtual&nbsp;DOM</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供了响应式</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>Reactive)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和组件化（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Composable)</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的视图组件。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将注意力集中保持在核心库，伴随于此，有配套的路由和负责处理全局状态管理的库。</span></p>
<p>2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">性能：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">到目前为止，针对现实情况的测试中，</span>Vue<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的性能是优于</span>React<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的。</span></p>
<p>3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">生态圈</span></p>
<p>Vue.js: ES6+Webpack+unit/e2e+Vue+vue一router+<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">单文件组件</span>+vuex+iVew </p>
<p>React: ES6+Webpack+Enzyme+React+React一router+Redux</p>
<p>4)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">什么时候选择</span>Vue.js</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果你喜欢用（或希望能够用）模板搭建应用，请使用</span>Vue </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果你喜欢简单和</span>”<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">能用就行</span>”<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的东西，请使用</span>Vue </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果你的应用需要尽可能的小和快，请使用</span>Vue </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果你计划构建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个大型应用程序，请使用</span>React </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果你想要</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个同时适用于</span>Web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">端和原生</span>App<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的框架，请选择</span>React </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果你想要最大的生态圈，请使用</span>React </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参考：</span></p>
<p><a href="http://cn.vuejs.org/v2/guide/comparison.html%23React"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">vuejs</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">org</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">v</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">2/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">guide</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">comparison</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">html#React</span></a></p>
<p><a href="http://blog.csdn.net/yzh_2017/article/details/54909166"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">csdn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">net</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">yzh</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">_2017/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">article</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">details</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/54909166</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百六十九、&nbsp;vue<strong>&nbsp;</strong>slot<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">是做什么的？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">简单来说，假如父组件需要在子组件内放</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">些</span>D<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">〇</span>M<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，那么这些</span><span style="font-family: Arial">DOM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是显示、不显示、在哪</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个地方显示、如何显示，就是</span>slot<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">分发负责的活。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参考：</span><a href="http://cn.vuejs.org/v2/guide/components.html%23%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8-Slot-%E5%88%86%E5%8F%91%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http://cn.vueis.orq/v2/quide/comp<span style="font-family: 宋体">〇</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">nents.html#</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">使用</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline">Slot</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline"><span style="font-family: 宋体">分发内容</span></span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百七十、&nbsp;vue<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span></strong>angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的优缺点以及适用场合？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参见：《在选择框架的时候要从哪方面入手》</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">题</span></p>
<p class="46">一百七十一、&nbsp;vue<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">路甶实现原理？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">以官方仓库下</span>examples/basic<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">基础例子来</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点点具体分析整个流程。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和流程相关的主要需要关注点的就是</span>components<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">history</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目录以及</span><span style="font-family: Arial">create</span>一matcher.js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">create</span>一route一map.js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span>index.js，install.js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">从入口，作为插件，实例化</span>VueRouter,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实例化</span>History,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实例化</span>Vue, defineReactive<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定 义</span>_route, router一link<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">router</span>一view<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件等几个方面展开分析</span></p>
