<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">必须参见：</span><a href="http://www.tuicool.com/articles/jQRnlrF"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">tuicool</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">articles/jQRnlrF</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百七十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你们</span></strong>vue<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">项目是打包了</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个</span></strong>js<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">文件，</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个</span></strong>css<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">文件，</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">还是有多个文件？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">根据</span>vue一cli<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">脚手架规范，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>CSS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文件。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span></p>
<p><a href="http://blog.csdn.net/lx376693576/article/details/54911340"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">csdn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">net</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">lx</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">376693576/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">article</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">details</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/54911340</span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/24322005"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhuanlan</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhihu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">p</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/24322005</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百七十三、&nbsp;vue<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">遇到的坑，如何解决的？</span></strong></p>
<p>Vue1.0<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">升级</span>2.0<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有很多坑</span>:<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">生命周期；路由中引入静态</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">全局组件，全局变量，全局</span> function; v一for<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">循环的</span>key, value<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">值互换了位置，还有</span>track一by; filter<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">过滤器；遍历数组时，</span> key<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">值不能做</span>model;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">父子通信等。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">其他坑详见：</span></p>
<p><a href="http://blog.csdn.net/lemon_zhao/article/details/55510589"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">blog</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">csdn</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">net</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">lemon</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">_</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhao</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">article</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">details</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/55510589</span></a>&nbsp;<a href="https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000008347498"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">segmentfault</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/1</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">190000008347498</span></a>&nbsp;<a href="http://www.tuicool.com/articles/aUrmumV"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">tuicool</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">articles/aUrmumV</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百七十四、&nbsp;vue<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的双向绑定的原理，和</span></strong>angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的对比</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在不同的</span>MWM<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">框架中，实现双向数据绑定的技术有所不同。</span></p>
<p>AngulaJS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">采用</span>‘‘<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">脏值检测</span><span style="font-family: Arial">”</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的方式，数据发生变更后，对于所有的数据和视图的绑定关系进 行</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次检测，识别是否有数据发生了改变，有变化进行处理，可能进</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">步引发其他数据的改</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">变，所以这个过程可能会循环几次，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">直到不再有数据变化发生后，将变更的数据发送到视</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">图，更新页面展现。如果是手动对</span>ViewModel<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的数据进行变更，为确保变更同步到视图，</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要手动触发</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次</span>‘‘<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">脏值检测</span><span style="font-family: Arial">”</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>VueJS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">则使用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ES5</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供的〇</span><span style="font-family: Arial">bject</span>.defineProperty()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法，监控对数据的操作，从而可以自</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">动触发数据同步。并且，由于是在不同的数据上触发同步，可以精确的将变更发送给绑定的</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">视图，而不是对所有的数据都执行</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次检测。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="http://www.jianshu.eom/p/d3a15a1f94a0"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">jianshu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">eom</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">p</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">d</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">3</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">15</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">1</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">f</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">94</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">a</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">0</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百七十五、&nbsp;vue<strong>一</strong>cli<span style="font-family: MingLiU">，</span><span style="font-family: MingLiU">脚手架</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">安装：</span>$ npm&nbsp;instaH&nbsp;一g&nbsp;vue一cli</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span>$ vue&nbsp;init&nbsp;&lt;template一name&gt; &lt;project一name&gt;</p>
<p>webpack<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">配置详解：</span><a href="https://zhuanlan.zhihu.eom/p/24322005"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhuanlan</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">zhihu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">eom</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">p</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/24322005</span></a></p>
<p class="46">一百七十六、&nbsp;Vue<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">里面</span></strong>router<strong>一</strong>link<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">在电脑上有用，在安卓上没反应</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">怎么解决？</span></strong></p>
<p>Vue<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">路由在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Android</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">机上有问题，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">babel</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">问题，安装</span><span style="font-family: Arial">babel</span>&nbsp;polypill<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">插件解决。</span></p>
<p class="43"><strong><em>框架底层</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百七十七、&nbsp;j<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">〇</span></strong>uery<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">源码中值得借鉴的？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用模块化思想，模块间保持独立，不会导致多个开发人员合作时产生的冲突。</span></p>
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在设计程序时，要结构清晰，髙内聚，低耦合。</span></p>
<p>2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">利用多态的方式，实现方法的重载，提髙代码的复用率</span></p>
<p>3．jQuery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的链式调用以及回溯</span></p>
<p>4．jQuery.fn.extend<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">;jQuery</span>.extend<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法来实现扩展静态方法或实例</span>方法</p>
<p class="46">一百七十八、&nbsp;<strong>$.</strong>ready<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">是怎么实现的？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原生</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中</span>window.onload<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件是在页面所有的资源都加载完毕后触发的</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果页面上有大图片等资源响应缓慢，会导致</span>window.onload<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件迟迟无法触发</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所以出现了 </span>DOM Ready<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件</span>.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">此事件在</span>D0M<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">文档结构准备完毕后触发，即在资源加载前触发</span>.</p>
<p>jQuery<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的</span>ready<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法实现了当页面加载完成后才执行的效果，但他并不是</span>window.onload<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者</span>doucment.onload<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的封装，而是使用标准</span>W3C<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器</span>DOM<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">隐藏</span>api<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和旧</span>浏<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">览器缺陷来完成的。</span>可以通过阅读jq<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">源码来理解：</span></p>
<p class="50">DOMContentLoaded = function(){</p>
<p class="50">	&nbsp;//<span style="font-family: 宋体">取消事件监听，执行</span>ready<span style="font-family: 宋体">方法</span></p>
<p class="50">	if ( document.addEventListener ){ &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p class="50">		document.removeEventListener( "DOMContentLoaded", </p>
<p class="50">	DOMContentLoaded, false );	</p>
<p class="50">		jQuery.ready();</p>
<p class="50">	}else if ( document.readyState === "complete" ) {</p>
<p class="50">		document.detachEvent( "onreadystatechange", DOMContentLoaded );</p>
<p class="50">		jQuery.ready();</p>
<p class="50">	}</p>
<p class="50">};</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span> jQuery <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中完整的代码如下所示。</span></p>
<p class="50">jQuery.ready.promise = function( obj ) {</p>
<p class="50">	if ( !readyList ) {</p>
<p class="50">		readyList = jQuery.Deferred();</p>
<p class="50">			//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">表示页面已经加载完成，直接调用 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">ready</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法</span></p>
<p class="50">		if ( document.readyState === "complete" ) { </p>
<p class="50">			//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">jQuery.ready</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">压入异步消息队列，设置延迟时间</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">1</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">毫秒（注意，有些浏览器延迟不能小于</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">4</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">毫秒）</span></p>
<p class="50">			setTimeout( jQuery.ready); </p>
<p class="50">		} </p>
<p class="50">		else if ( document.addEventListener ) //</p>
<p class="50">		{</p>
<p class="50">			&nbsp;//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">监听</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">DOM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">加载完成</span></p>
<p class="50">			document.addEventListener( "DOMContentLoaded", DOMContentLoaded, false );</p>
<p class="50">			&nbsp;//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这里是为了确保所有</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">ready</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">执行结束，如果</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">DOMContentLoaded</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法执行了，将有一个状态值 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">isReady</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">被设置为</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">true,</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因此，</span></p>
<p class="50">			&nbsp;//ready<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法一旦执行，那么将只执行一次，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">window.addEventListener</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">ready </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将被 </span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">return </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中断</span></p>
<p class="50">			window.addEventListener( "load", jQuery.ready, false );</p>
<p class="50">		} else {</p>
<p class="50">			//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">低版本的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">IE</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器</span></p>
<p class="50">			document.attachEvent( "onreadystatechange", DOMContentLoaded );</p>
<p class="50">			window.attachEvent( "onload", jQuery.ready );</p>
<p class="50">			var top = false;</p>
<p class="50">			try {</p>
<p class="50">				top = window.frameElement == null &amp;&amp; document.documentElement;</p>
<p class="50">			} catch(e) {</p>
<p class="50">			}</p>
<p class="50">			if ( top &amp;&amp; top.doScroll ) &nbsp;//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">剔除</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">iframe</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的成分</span></p>
<p class="50">			{</p>
<p class="50">				(function doScrollCheck() {</p>
<p class="50">					if ( !jQuery.isReady ) {</p>
<p class="50">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="50">						try {</p>
<p class="50">							//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">根据</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">bug</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来兼容低版本的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">IE http://javascript.nwbox.com/IEContentLoaded/</span></p>
<p class="50">							top.doScroll("left");</p>
<p class="50">						} catch(e) {</p>
<p class="50">							//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">由于低版本的</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">IE </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浏览器，</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">onreadystatechange</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件不可靠，因此需要根据各个</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">bug</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来判断页面是否已加载完成</span></p>
<p class="50">							return setTimeout( doScrollCheck, 50 ); </p>
<p class="50">						}</p>
<p class="50">						jQuery.ready();</p>
<p class="50">					}</p>
<p class="50">				})();</p>
<p class="50">			}</p>
<p class="50">		}</p>
<p class="50">	}</p>
<p class="50">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="50">return readyList.promise( obj );</p>
<p class="50">};</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要的时候，在我们调用</span> ready <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数的时候，才需要注册这些判断页面是否完全加载的处理，如下所示：</span></p>
<p class="50">ready: function( wait ){</p>
<p class="50">	if ( wait === true ? <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">jQuery.readyWait : jQuery.isReady ) { </span></p>
<p class="50">		//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">判断页面是否已完成加载并且是否已经执行</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">ready</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法</span></p>
<p class="50">		return;</p>
<p class="50">	}</p>
<p class="50">	if ( !document.body ) {</p>
<p class="50">		return setTimeout( jQuery.ready );</p>
<p class="50">	}	</p>
<p class="50">	jQuery.isReady = true; //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">指示</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">ready</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法已被执行</span>	</p>
<p class="50">	if ( wait !== true &amp;&amp; <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一一</span><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;">jQuery.readyWait &gt; 0 ) {</span></p>
<p class="50">		return;</p>
<p class="50">	}	</p>
<p class="50">	readyList.resolveWith( document, [ jQuery ] );	</p>
<p class="50">	if ( jQuery.fn.trigger ) {</p>
<p class="50">		jQuery( document ).trigger("ready").off("ready"); </p>
<p class="50">	}</p>
<p class="50">}</p>
<p>总结：</p>
<p>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">页面加载完成有两种事件，一是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ready</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，表示文档结构已经加载完成（不包含图片等非文字媒体文件），二是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">onload</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，指示页 面包含图片等文件在内的所有元素都加载完成。</span><span style="font-family: Arial">(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以说：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ready </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">onload </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">前加载！！！</span><span style="font-family: Arial">)</span><br><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一般样式控制的，比如图片大小控制放在</span>onload <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里面加载</span><span style="font-family: Arial">;</span><br>jS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">事件触发的方法，可以在</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ready </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里面加载</span><span style="font-family: Arial">;</span></p>
<p class="46">一百七十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">懒加载的实现原理</span>?</strong></p>
<p>意义：懒加载的主要目的是作为服务器前端的优化，减少请求数或延迟请求数。</p>
<p>实现原理：先加载一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">部分数据，当触发某个条件时利用异步加载剩余的数据，新得到的数据</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不会影响原有数据的显示，同时最大程度上减少服务器端的资源耗用。</span></p>
<p>实现方式：</p>
<ol>
<li>第一种是纯粹的延迟加载，使用<span style="text-decoration: underline">setTimeOut</span>或<span style="text-decoration: underline">setlnterval</span>进行加载延迟.</li>
<li>第二种是条件加载，符合某些条件，或触发了某些事件才开始异步下载。</li>
<li>第三种是可视区加载，即仅加载用户可以看到的区域，这个主要由监控滚动条来实现<span style="font-family: 微软雅黑">，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体">一</span>般会在距用户看到某图片前一定距离便开始加载，这样能保证用户拉下时正好能看到图片。</li>

</ol>
<p class="46">一百八十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">双向数据绑定和单向数据的区别？</span></strong></p>
<p>1．单向数据流中，父组件给子组件传递数据，但反过来不可以传递，也就是说单向数据流是从最外层节点传递到子节点，他们只需从最外层节点获取props<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">渲染即可，如果顶层组件的</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">某个</span>prop<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">改变了，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">React</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会递归的向下便利整棵组件树，重新渲染所有使用这个属性的组件，</span> React<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件内部还具有自己的状态，这些状态只能在组件内修改；双向数据绑定是数据与视图</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">双向绑定，数据发生改变时，视图也改变，视图发生改变时，数据也会发生改变。</span></p>
<p>2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">双向数据绑定的各种数据相互依赖相互绑定，导致数据问题的源头难以被跟踪到；单向</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">数据流的数据流动方向可以跟踪，流动单</span>一，追查问题的时候可以更快捷，缺点是写起来不太方便，要使视图发生改变就得创建各种action来维护state。</p>
<p>3．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">双向绑定把数据变更的操作隐藏在框架内部，调用者并不会直接感知。而在践行单向数</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">据流的</span>flux系的实现中，其实不过是在全局搞了一个单例的事件分发器（dispatcher)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，开发者 </span>必须显式地通过这个统一的事件机制做数据变更通知。</p>
<p class="46">一百八十一、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">怎么实现</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个类似于</span></strong>const<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">功能的方法？</span></strong></p>
<p>es6<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中</span>const<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相当于声明常量不可更改，我们利用</span>defineProperty<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以模拟实现；我们把</span> writable<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置为</span>false<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的时候，该属性就成了只读，也就满足了常量了性质，我们把常量封装</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在</span>CONST<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">命名空间里面，但是因为我们依然可以通过修改属性</span>writable<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为</span>true<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">修改属性值，所以 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">configurable</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">设置为</span>false,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不能修改属性；</span></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<div class="Section12">
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">模拟：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如下代码</span>CONST.a<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相当于</span><span style="font-family: Arial">es6</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中</span><span style="font-family: Arial">cont a=2; CONST.a</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是不可以更改</span>的<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">常量；</span> </p>
<table>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top" width="349">
<p><strong>var CONST = { };</strong></p>
<p><strong>Object.defineProperty(CONST, ‘a’, { </strong></p>
<p><strong>value: 2,</strong></p>
<p><strong>writable: false, </strong></p>
<p><strong>configurable: false,</strong></p>
<p><strong>enumerable: true //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可枚举 </span></strong></p>
<p><strong>});</strong></p>
<p><strong>console.log(CONST.a);</strong><strong>//2</strong></p>
<p><strong>CONST.a = 3;</strong></p>
<p><strong>console.log(CONST.a);</strong><strong>//2</strong></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="46">一百八十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">使用原生</span></strong><strong>js</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">模拟</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个</span></strong><strong>apply</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">方法</span></strong></p>
<p>apply<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">语法：</span>apply([thisObj[,argArray]])</p>
<p>定义：应用某一对象的一个方法，用另一个对象替换当前对象。</p>
<p>说明：</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果</span> argArray <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不是一个有效的数组或者不是 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">arguments </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象，那么将导致一个 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">TypeError</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果没有提供</span> argArray <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">thisObj </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">任何一个参数，那么 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">Global </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象将被用作 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">thisObj</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">， 并且无法被传递任何参数。</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>Function.prototype.apply = function (context, arr) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var context = Object(context) || window;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;context.fn = this;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var result;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;if (!arr) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;result = context.fn();</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;else {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var args = [];</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for (var i = 0, len = arr.length; i &lt; len; i++) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;args.push('arr[' + i + ']');</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;result = eval('context.fn(' + args + ')')</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;delete context.fn</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return result;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="46">一百八十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">使用原生</span></strong><strong>js</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">模拟</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个</span></strong><strong>call</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">方法</span></strong></p>
<p>call()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法在使用一个指定的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">this</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">值和若干个指定的参数值的前提下调用某个函数或方法。</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>Function.prototype.call = function (context) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var context = context || window;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;context.fn = this;</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var args = [];</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;for(var i = 1, len = arguments.length; i &lt; len; i++) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;args.push('arguments[' + i + ']');</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;}</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;var result = eval('context.fn(' + args +')');</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;delete context.fn</strong></p>
<p><strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;return result;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p>以上两个方法的具体实现原理可以参考：<a href="https://juejin.im/post/5907eb99570c3500582ca23c"><span style="text-decoration: underline">https://juejin.im/post/5907eb99570c3500582ca23c</span></a>&nbsp;	</p>
<p class="46">一百八十四、&nbsp;<strong>O</strong>bject<strong>.</strong>create<strong>()</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和直接创建对象有什么区别？</span></strong></p>
<p>Object.create()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法创建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个拥有指定原型和若干个指定属性的对象</span> //Object.create(proto,[propertiesObject])</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">该方法创建</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个对象，其接受两个参数，第</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个参数是这个对象的原型对象</span>proto,</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">第二个是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个可选参数，用以对对象的属性做进</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">步描述</span> </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果</span>proto<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参数不是</span>null<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个对象值，则抛出</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>TypeError<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">异常</span> </p>
<p>var objl = Object.create({</p>
<p>&nbsp;x: 1, </p>
<p>&nbsp;y: 2</p>
<p>}); //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象</span>obj1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">继承了属性</span>x<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>y</p>
<p>var&nbsp;obj2 = Object.create(null);//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">obj2 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">没有原型</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象字面量是创建对象最简单的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">种形式，</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目的是在于简化创建包含大量属性的对象的过程。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象字面量由若干属性名</span>(keys)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和属性值</span>(values)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">成对组成的映射表，</span></p>
<p>key<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和</span>value<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中间使用冒号</span>(:)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">分隔，</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">每对</span>key/value<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之间使用逗号</span>(,)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">分隔，</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">整个映射表用花括号</span>({})<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">括起来。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在用字面量来创建对象的时候，对象中的</span>property<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">定义可以用单引号或双引号来包括，也可以忽略引号。不过，当</span>property<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中出现空格、斜杠等特殊字符，或者使用的</span>property<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span>JS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">关键词冲突时，则必须使用引号。</span></p>
<p>var obj = {</p>
<p>property_1: value_1,// property—# <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可能是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个标识符</span>...</p>
<p>2: value_2, //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个数字</span> "property n": value_n // <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个字符串</span> </p>
<p>}</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过对象字面量创建的对象复用性较差，</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span>Object.create()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">创建对象时不需要定义</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个构造函数就允许你在对象中选择其原型对象。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百八十五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">使用</span></strong>for<strong>&nbsp;</strong>in<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">遍历对象和使用</span></strong>Object<strong>.</strong>keys<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">来遍历对象</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">有什么区别？</span></strong></p>
<p>1．for&nbsp;in<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">主要用于遍历对象的可枚举属性，包括自有属性、继承自原型的属性</span></p>
<p>2．Object.keys<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">返回</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个数组，元素均为对象自有的可枚举属性</span></p>
<p>3．Object.getOwnProperty&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用于返回对象的自有属性，包括可枚举的和不可枚举的</span> </p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="604">
<p><strong>var obj = {</strong></p>
<p><strong>"name":"xiaosan",</strong></p>
<p><strong>"age":2</strong><strong>3</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>Object.defineProperty(obj,"height",{value:178,enumerable:false})</strong></p>
<p><strong>Object.prototype.prototypel = function(){</strong></p>
<p><strong>console.log('aaa')</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>Object.prototype.prototype2 = 'bbb';</strong></p>
<p><strong>//for in</strong></p>
<p><strong>for(var i in obj){</strong></p>
<p><strong>console.log(i); //name age prototypel prototype2 </strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>//Object.keys</strong></p>
<p><strong>console.log(Object.keys(obj)) //name age</strong></p>
<p><strong>//Object.getOwnProperty</strong></p>
<p><strong>console.log(Object.getOwnPropertyNames(obj)) //name age height</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="46">一百八十六、&nbsp;<strong>深</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">拷贝和浅拷贝以及应用场景</span></strong></p>
<p>i.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浅拷贝</span></p>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">拷贝就是把父对</span>象<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的属性，全部拷贝给子对象。</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>var Chinese = { </strong></p>
<p><strong>nation:'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中国’</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>Var Doctor={</strong></p>
<p><strong>career:'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">医生</span><span style="font-family: Arial">'</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>function extendCopy(p) { </strong></p>
<p><strong>var c = {}; </strong></p>
<p><strong>for (var i in p) { </strong></p>
<p><strong>c[i] = p[i];</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>c.uber = p; return c;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用的时候，这样写：</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>Doctor = extendCopy(Chinese);</strong></p>
<p><strong>Doctor.career ='<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">医生</span><span style="font-family: Arial">'</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">； </span></strong></p>
<p><strong>alert(Doctor.nation); // <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中国</span></strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">但是，这样的拷贝有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个问题。那就是，如果父对象的属性等于数组或另</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个对象，那么实际上，子对象获得的只是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个内存地址，而不是真正拷贝，因此存在父对象被篡改的可能。</span></p>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请看，现在给</span>Chinese<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">添加</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>"<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">出生地</span><span style="font-family: Arial">"</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性，它的值是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个数组。</span></p>
<p>Chinese.birthPlaces&nbsp;=['<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">北京</span><span style="font-family: Arial">','</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上海</span><span style="font-family: Arial">','</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">香港</span><span style="font-family: Arial">'];</span></p>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span><span style="font-family: Arial">extendCopy</span>()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">函数，</span>Doctor<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">继承了</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Chinese</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>
<p>Doctor&nbsp;= extendCopy(Chinese);</p>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">然后，我们为</span>Doctor<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>"<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">出生地</span><span style="font-family: Arial">"</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">添加</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个城市：</span></p>
<p>Doctor.birthPlaces.push('<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">厦门</span><span style="font-family: Arial">')</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">；</span></p>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">看</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下输入结果</span></p>
<p>alert(Doctor.birthPlaces); //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">北京，上海，香港，厦门 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">alert(Chinese.birthPlaces); //</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">北京，上海，香港，厦门</span></p>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">结果是两个的出生地都被改了。</span></p>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所以，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">extendCopy</span>()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">只是拷贝了基本类型的数据，我们把这种拷贝叫做</span>''<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浅拷贝〃。</span></p>
<p>2.<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">深拷贝</span></p>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">所谓</span><span style="font-family: Arial">"</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">深拷贝</span><span style="font-family: Arial">"</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，就是能够实现真正意义上的数组和对象的拷贝。它的实现并不难， 只要递归调用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">"</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浅拷贝</span><span style="font-family: Arial">"</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就行了。</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>var Chinese = {</strong></p>
<p><strong>nation:'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中国’</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>var Doctor = { </strong></p>
<p><strong>career:'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">医生</span><span style="font-family: Arial">'</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>function deepCopy(p, c) { </strong></p>
<p><strong>var c = c || {}; </strong></p>
<p><strong>for (var i in p) {</strong></p>
<p><strong>if (typeof p[i] === 'object') {</strong></p>
<p><strong>c[i] = (p[i].constructor === Array) ? [] : {}; deepCopy(p[i], c[i]);</strong></p>
<p><strong>} else {</strong></p>
<p><strong>c[i] = p[i];</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>return c;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">看一下使用方法：</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>Doctor = deepCopy(Chinese);</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p>//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">现在，给父对象加</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个属性，值为数组。然后，在子对象上修改这个属性：</span></p>
<p>Chinese.birthPlaces&nbsp;=['<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">北京</span><span style="font-family: Arial">','</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上海</span><span style="font-family: Arial">','</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">香港</span><span style="font-family: Arial">'];</span></p>
<p>Doctor.birthPlaces.push('<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">厦门</span><span style="font-family: Arial">')</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">； </span></p>
<p>alert(Doctor.birthPlaces); //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">北京，上海，香港，厦门</span></p>
<p>alert(Chinese.birthPlaces); //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">北京，上海，香港</span></p>
<p>JavaScript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中的对象</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般是可变的</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（</span>Mutable),<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为使用了引用赋值，新的对象简单的引用了原始对象，改变新的对象将影响到原始对象。如</span>'foo={a: 1}; bar=foo; bar.a=2'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">你会发现此时</span> 'foo.a'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也被改成了</span> '2'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。</span></p>

</div>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">虽然这样做可以节约内存，但当应用复杂后，这就造成了非常大的隐患，</span>Mutable<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">带来的优点变得得不偿失。为了解决这个问题，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">般的做法是使用</span>shallowCopy&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">浅拷贝）或</span>deepCopy&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">深拷贝）来避免被修改，但这样做造成了</span>CPU<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和内存的浪费。</span></p>
<p>Immutable<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以很好地解决这些问题。</span>	</p>
<p class="46">一百八十七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">原型链，闭包与继承</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">闭包的好处：</span></p>
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不会污染全局环境；</span></p>
<p>2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以进行形参的记忆，减少形参的个数</span>,<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">延长形参生命周期； </span></p>
<p>function&nbsp;add(x) {</p>
<p>return&nbsp;function(y) { </p>
<p>return&nbsp;(x+y);</p>
<p>}</p>
<p>}</p>
<p>var&nbsp;sum&nbsp;= add(2); </p>
<p>sum(5);//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">结果为</span>&nbsp;7</p>
<p>3．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方便进行模块化开发；</span> </p>
<p>var&nbsp;module&nbsp;= (function() { </p>
<p>var&nbsp;name&nbsp;= '123'; </p>
<p>function&nbsp;init() {</p>
<p>console.log(name);</p>
<p>}</p>
<p>return&nbsp;{</p>
<p>getname:init</p>
<p>}</p>
<p>})()</p>
<p>module.getname();//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">结果为</span>&nbsp;123;</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">继承：</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个构造函数继承另</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个构造函数中的方法</span>;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以省去大量的重复。</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>function Man(name,age) { </strong></p>
<p><strong>this.name = name; this.age = age;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>var person = new Man('tom',19); </strong></p>
<p><strong>function Woman(name,age) { </strong></p>
<p><strong>this.sex = 'woman';</strong></p>
<p><strong>Man.call(this,name,age);</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>Woman.prototype = Man.prototype; </strong></p>
<p><strong>var person1 = new Woman('july',20); </strong></p>
<p><strong>person1.name//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">结果为 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">july </span></strong></p>
<p><strong>person1.age //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">结果为 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">20 </span></strong></p>
<p><strong>person1.sex //<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">结果为 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">woman</span></strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原型链查找：进行方法调用的时候，会</span>先<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在实例自身上找，如果没有就去该实例的原型上找。</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>function People() { </strong></p>
<p><strong>this.name = 'a People';</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>People.prototype.say = function() { </strong></p>
<p><strong>this.age = '10';</strong></p>
<p><strong>console.log(this.name,this.age);</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>var person = new People(); </strong></p>
<p><strong>person.say();</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p class="42"><strong><em>AngularJS</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">一百八十八、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">说说你对</span>MVC<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span><span style="font-family: Arial">MVVM</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的理解</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>mvc:</strong></p>
<p>View <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">传送指令到 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">Controller</span></p>
<p>Controller <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">完成业务逻辑后，要求 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">Model </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">改变状态</span></p>
<p>Model <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将新的数据发送到 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">View</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，用户得到反馈</span></p>
<p><strong>所有通信都是单向的。</strong></p>
<p>Angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">它采用双向绑定（</span><span style="font-family: Arial">data-binding</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">）：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">View</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的变动，自动反映在 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">ViewModel</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，反之亦然。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组成部分</span>Model<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">View</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ViewModel</span></p>
<p>View<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">UI</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">界面</span></p>
<p>ViewModel<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：它是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">View</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的抽象，负责</span><span style="font-family: Arial">View</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Model</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之间信息转换，将</span><span style="font-family: Arial">View</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Command</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">传送到</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Model</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">；</span></p>
<p>Model<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：数据访问层</span></p>
<p class="46">一百八十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">对</span> bootstrap <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的掌握</span></strong><strong>？</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">为什么用</span> angular+bootstrap <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">搭</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">建后台管理系统</span></strong></p>
<p>bootstrap<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个快速开发的响应式框架，主要是为了快速搭建</span>ui<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">界面</span>，bootstrap <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>web<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件和</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">插件对</span>pc<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">端开发比较友好，尤其是栅格化系统可以良好兼容浏览器，</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">低版本浏览器可以使用</span>bootstrap一responsive<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的插件兼容，</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">插件有各种回调机制，可以满足自己的多样开发需求，而且</span>bootstrap<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span>css<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">属性来操作样式，免去了手写原生代码的痛苦</span>，<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行数据绑定，</span>bootstrap<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来搭建界面，提升开发效率</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个人心得：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">我在实际开发中使用</span>ace&nbsp;admin<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这套基于</span>boostrap<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的框架，可以更快速的开发，数据项通过</span>json<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">结构进行配置，几乎不用手写代码，提升开发效率</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十、&nbsp;<strong>angular</strong><span style="font-family: MingLiU">中</span><strong>ng</strong><strong>一</strong><strong>if</strong><span style="font-family: MingLiU">和</span><strong>ng</strong>-<strong>show/hide</strong>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: MingLiU">有什么区别？</span></p>
<p>1．ng<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">if </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在后面表达式为 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">true </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的时候才创建这个 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">dom </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节点，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ng</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">show </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是初始时就创建了，用 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">display:block </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">display:none </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来控制显示和不显示。</span></p>
<p>2．ng<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">if </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会（隐式地）产生新作用域，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">ng</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">switch </span>.ng<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">include </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等会动态创建一块界面的也是如此。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个人心得：</span></p>
<p>ng一if<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">添加删除节点，那么肯定回创建作用域，而</span>ng一show/hide<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">则不会</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十一、&nbsp;Angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中</span></strong>ng<strong>一</strong>click<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中写的表达式，可以用</span></strong>js<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">原生上</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的方法吗？为什么？</span></strong></p>
<p>&nbsp;ng一click<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">和原生事件完成的功能是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">样的，但是</span>ng一click<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">做了优化，而且</span>ng一click<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里面可以写表达式，运算过程，</span>click<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">则要单独处理，手写功能。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个人心得：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">如果不在作用域里添加函数，可以配合</span>ng一init<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">初始化属性值，在</span>ng一click<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里添加算</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">法或者某</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">功能，虽然</span>ng一inK<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不推荐使用，但是侧面说明</span>ng一click<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的优势</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">内置</span></strong>filter<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">都有哪些？</span></strong></p>
<p>ng <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">内置的 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">filter </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有九种：</span></p>
<p>date<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（日期）</span></p>
<p>currency<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（货币）</span></p>
<p>limitTo<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（限制数组或字符串长度）</span></p>
<p>orderBy<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（排序）</span></p>
<p>lowercase<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（小写）</span></p>
<p>uppercase<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（大写）</span></p>
<p>number<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（格式化数字，加上千位分隔符，并接收参数限定小数点位数）</span></p>
<p>json<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（格式化 </span><span style="font-family: Arial">json </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对象）</span></p>
<p>filter<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">（处理一个数组，过滤出含有某个子串的元素）</span></p>
<p>filter<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有两种使用方法，一种是直接在页面里：</span></p>
<p>&lt;p&gt;{{now | date : 'yyyy<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">MM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">dd'}}&lt;/p&gt;</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">另一种是在</span> js <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里面用：</span></p>
<p>// $filter('<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">过滤器名称</span><span style="font-family: Arial">')(</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要过滤的对象</span><span style="font-family: Arial">, </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参数</span><span style="font-family: Arial">1, </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">参数</span><span style="font-family: Arial">2,...)</span></p>
<p>$filter('date')(now, 'yyyy<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">MM</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span><span style="font-family: Arial">dd hh:mm:ss');</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何自定义</span></strong>filter<strong>?</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在模块下挂在</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>filter()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">方法，第</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个参数传入过滤器的名字，第二个参数是回调函数，处理过滤方法的详细内容，最后返回结果，这样外部就可以根据过滤器的名字调用了</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">例如</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>
<p><strong>myAppModule.filter("reverse"<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">function(){ </span></strong></p>
<p><strong>return &nbsp;function(input,uppercase){ </strong></p>
<p><strong>var out ="";</strong></p>
<p><strong>for(var i=0 ; i&lt;input.length; i++){ </strong></p>
<p><strong>out = input.charAt(i)+out;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>if(uppercase){ </strong></p>
<p><strong>out = out.toUpperCase();</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>return out;</strong></p>
<p><strong>}</strong></p>
<p><strong>});</strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">使用：</span>name<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">丨</span>reverse<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过管道符调用</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十四、&nbsp;<strong>factory</strong><strong>、</strong><strong>service</strong>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: MingLiU">和</span> <strong>provider</strong>&nbsp;<span style="font-family: MingLiU">是什么</span><span style="font-family: 宋体">关系</span><span style="font-family: MingLiU">？</span></p>
<p>factory&nbsp;, service&nbsp;, provider都<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是</span>angular&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供的服务</span> </p>
<p>factory<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是原生</span><span style="font-family: Arial">js</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里的方法，</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个简单的函数</span></p>
<p>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">类似原生里构造函数的过程，拥有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个构造器</span>constructor<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也就是说有</span> new<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的过程，追加属性和方法都是在</span>this<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上追加的</span></p>
<p>provider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是服务商当</span>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">需要配置的时候，需要使用</span>provider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供服务，例如当使用</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行跨域访问，需要配置</span>jsonp<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">信息的时候，就可以使用</span>provider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行</span>config<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的配置，简单理解是</span>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的高级版本，</span>provider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>$get<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的属性来返回</span> $provider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的实例</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">他们都是单例模式，只实例化</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个人理解</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span></p>
<p>provider&nbsp;&gt; service&nbsp;&gt; factory</p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;factory<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">用来配置简单的服务</span></p>
<p>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是在</span>factory<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的基础之上加入了面向对象的思想，提供更多功能的服务</span></p>
<p>provider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是在</span>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的基础上进</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">步改进配置信息</span> </p>
<p>factory<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在底层代码上都来源于</span>provider </p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">例子介绍：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">我可以在</span>factory<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里写</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>$http( )<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求，不做任何配置，参数写死</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">我可以在</span>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里写</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>$http( )<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">请求，传入请求的参数可以先配置在</span>this<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的属性上传入方法</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">我可以在</span>provider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里写</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个请求，然后在</span>config<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">上传入要配置的参数，</span>URL<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span> method<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>data<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等信息，通过</span>config<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来修改</span>provider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的参数，再将服务商提供的服务注入控制器</span>controller</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">注意事项：</span></p>
<p>config<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里传入的参数是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">nameProvider</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而不是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">name</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也就是说你的叫做</span> myProvider, config&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">里传入的参数就是</span>myProviderProvider<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">而不是</span><span style="font-family: Arial">myProvider</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十五、&nbsp;angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的数据绑定采用什么机制？详述原理</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>$watch<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来监听每</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次</span>dom<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的变化，然后</span>$digest<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来遍历循环所有的</span>$watch <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">队列，发现与原来不同的值，也就是脏值则进行修改，最后通知</span>$apply&nbsp;, $apply<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会进入</span>angular&nbsp;context<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的执行环境，通知浏览器拿回控制权，修改相应的</span>dom<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">节点</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个人心得：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">每</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>ng<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">指令的触发都在内部触发了</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>$Watch<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的队列，加入</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组标签</span> </p>
<p>&lt;li&nbsp;ng一repeat="item&nbsp;in&nbsp;items"&gt;</p>
<p>{{ item&nbsp;}}</p>
<p>&lt;/li&gt;</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">循环了</span> 10<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">次，那么就触发了</span>10<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>item<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">与</span>1<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>ng一repeat<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的</span>11<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span><span style="font-family: Arial">$watch</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的队列，</span></p>
<p>$digest<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会遍历循环这些队列，比较值</span>的<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">变化，有变化的即为脏值过程叫做</span>dirty一checking<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>$digest<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">修改完对应的值就会通知</span>$apply()<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">准备进入</span>angular&nbsp;context<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的执行阶段修改</span>dom<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">没有变化则不修改。也就是说我们在页面每次触发的操作，每次输入</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个文字都会触发</span>$watch<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，可见于</span>react<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相比</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的劣势出现了</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十六、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">两个平级界面块</span></strong>a<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">和</span></strong>b<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如果</span></strong>a<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中触发</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个事件，</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">有哪些方式能让</span></strong>b<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">知道？详述原理</span></strong></p>
<p>1．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>a<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的子</span><span style="font-family: Arial">controller</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">将事件使用</span>$emit<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">传递给父</span><span style="font-family: Arial">controller</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">再将事件用 </span>$broadcast<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">传递给</span><span style="font-family: Arial">b</span>&nbsp;controller<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">实现数据传递</span></p>
<p>2．<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">也可以通过</span>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">服务，将数据保存在</span>service<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之内，然后在</span>b<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中调用</span>service</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个人心得：</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">像这种数据传递的方式其实有很多种，本质是不同作用于之间的数据传递，只要</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">掌握住这</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">点思想有很多方式解决，比如我可以尝试挂在</span>$rootScope<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">之上进行共</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">享，也可以用本地存储来存储数据，实现数据共享。方法不重要，关键是如何解决</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的思路。</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十七、&nbsp;<strong>—</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">个</span></strong>angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">应用应当如何良好地分层？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目录结构的划分</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对于小型项目，可以按照文件类型组织，比如：</span> </p>
<p>css</p>
<p>js</p>
<p>controllers</p>
<p>models</p>
<p>services</p>
<p>filters</p>
<p>templates</p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">但是对于规模较大的项目，最好按业务模块划分，比如</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span> </p>
<p>css</p>
<p>modules</p>
<p>account</p>
<p>controllers</p>
<p>models</p>
<p>services</p>
<p>filters</p>
<p>templates</p>
<p>disk</p>
<p>controllers</p>
<p>models</p>
<p>services</p>
<p>filters</p>
<p>templates</p>
<p>modules<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下最好再有</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个</span>common<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">目录来存放公共的东西</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十八、&nbsp;angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">应用常用哪些路甶库，各自的区别是什</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">么？</span></strong></p>
<p>ng一router<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>ui一touter<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>ui一router<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以嵌套子视图</span></p>
<p class="46">一百九十九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如果通过</span></strong>angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的</span></strong>directive<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">规划</span></strong><strong>一</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">套全组件化体</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">系，可能遇到哪些挑战？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">隔离作用域，</span>ng一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">指令的作用域传递</span></p>
<p class="46">二百、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">分属不同团队进行开发的</span></strong>angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">应用，如果要做整合，可能会遇到哪些问题，如何解决？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可能会遇到不同模块之间的冲突。比如</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个团队所有的开发在</span>moduleA<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下进行，</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">另</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">团队开发的代码在</span>moduleB<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下</span></p>
<table class="55">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="center" width="636">
<p><strong>angular.module('myApp.moduleA'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">[ ])</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>.factory('serviceA', function(){</strong></p>
<p><strong>.......</strong></p>
<p><strong>})</strong></p>
<p><strong>angular.module('myApp.moduleB'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">[ ])</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>.factory('serviceA'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">function(){</span></strong></p>
<p><strong>......</strong></p>
<p><strong>})</strong></p>
<p><strong>angular.module('myApp'<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">['myApp.moduleA'</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: Arial">'myApp.moduleB'])</span></strong></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">会导致两个</span>module<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下面的</span>serviceA<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">发生了覆盖。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个人心得：没有太好的解决方案，只能约定命名规范</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇一、&nbsp;angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的缺点有哪些？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不适合做交互过多的项目，因为没有选择器的存在，</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">导致学习成本较高，对前端不友好。但遵守</span>AngularJS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的约定时，生产力会很高，对</span>Java<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">程序员友好</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为所有内容都是动态获取并渲染生成的，搜索引擎没法爬取</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇二、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何看待</span>angularl.2<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中引入的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">controller as</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">语 法？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">为</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">添加</span>this<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">作用域链，使得</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">更加</span>像<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">原声写法</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">详述</span></strong><strong>angular<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的</span><span style="font-family: Arial">“</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">依赖注入</span><span style="font-family: Arial">”</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">。</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">依赖注入是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个在组件中给出的替代了硬的组件内的编码它们的依赖关系的软件设计模式。这减轻</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个组成部分，从定位的依赖，依赖配置。这有助于使组件可重用，维护和测试。</span></p>
<p>AngularJS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">提供了</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个至高无上的依赖注入机制。它提供了</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个可注入彼此依赖</span> constant&nbsp;value&nbsp;factory&nbsp;service&nbsp;provide&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">核心组件。</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">当你简单的动态给页面插入</span></strong><strong>html<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">时</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，此时</span></strong><strong>ht</strong><strong>ml<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">带</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">有</span> </strong><strong>angular</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的语法不会执行的，为什么？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">通过</span>$compile<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行处理，任何指令的生效都需要</span>compile<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">步在</span>app<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">启动的时候</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">先帮你做了，但你插入的</span>html<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">是没有经过</span>compile<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这个步骤的，所以你手动</span> compile<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">下即可。</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">使用</span>ng</strong><strong>一</strong><strong>repeat<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">出错：</span><span style="font-family: Arial">Error: [ngRepeat:dupes]</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">，怎么回事？</span></strong></p>
<p>Error: [ngRepeat:dupes]<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">这个出错提示具体意思是指数组中有</span>2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个以上的相同数字。 </span>ngRepeat<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不允许</span>collection<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">中存在两个相同</span>Id<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的对象</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">对于数字对象来说，它的</span>id<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">就是它自身的值，因此，数组中是不允许存在两个相同的数字的。为了规避这个错误，需要定义自己的</span>track&nbsp;by<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">表达式。 </span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">例如</span>：在ng一repeat="itme&nbsp;in&nbsp;items&nbsp;"中加入rack&nbsp;by&nbsp;item.id&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者</span>track&nbsp;by&nbsp;fnCustomld(item)<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">。 </span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">嫌麻烦的话，直接拿循环的索引变量</span>$index<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">来用</span><span style="font-family: Arial">item</span>&nbsp;in&nbsp;items&nbsp;track&nbsp;by&nbsp;$index——<span style="font-family: Arial">&gt;</span>ng一repeat="itme&nbsp;in&nbsp;items&nbsp;track&nbsp;by&nbsp;$index"</p>
<p>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">句话总结：因为</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">不允许数组中出现重复的值，所以会报错</span>dupes<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">错误，意思是重复的参数错误</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇六、&nbsp;<strong>Ng<span style="font-family: 华文黑体">一</span></strong><strong>repeat</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">迭代数组的时候，如果数组中有相同值，会有什么问题，如何解决？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">见上题</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇七、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">使用第三方插件或者原生的</span></strong>js<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">修改</span></strong>angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中的</span> </strong>model<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">或者</span></strong>view<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的值时，相应的</span></strong>model<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">或者</span></strong>view<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的值</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">不会变化，也就是</span></strong>angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">的双向数据绑定失效，怎么回事？</span></strong></p>
<p>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有自己的</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个上下文，所有与</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">有关的代码执行（如双向数据绑定）都在这个上下文中进行，因此如果你用第三方插件或者原生的</span>js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行操作时，此时代码是在</span>javascript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的上下文中执行，</span>angular<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">无法知道你是否修改</span>model<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者</span>view<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的值，自然也就无法进行双向数据绑定。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">解决方案</span>是<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">在操作之后执行</span>$scope.$apply( )<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">或者将操作的代码放在</span>$scope.$apply(function( ){//<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">操作的代码</span><span style="font-family: Arial">...})</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇八、&nbsp;angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中注入方式有推断式注入、</span></strong>$inject<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">注入、内联式注入，当然这三种方式在</span></strong>angular<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">中是等效的，</span><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">但推断式注入对于压缩的</span></strong>JavaScript<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">代码来说是不起作用的，为什么？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">因为压缩过后的</span> JavaScript <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码重命名了函数的参数名。</span>在压缩js<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">代码的时候</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">尽量不要用推断式注入，最佳是用内联式注入的方式。</span></p>
<p class="46">二百〇九、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何看待</span> </strong>angular<strong>2?</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">相比</span>Angularl.x<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>Angular2<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的改动很大，几乎算是</span>一<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">个全新的框架。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">基于</span>TypeScript&nbsp;(<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以使用</span>TypeScript<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">进行开发），在大型项目团队协作时，强语言类型更有利。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">组件化，提升开发和维护的效率。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">还有</span>module<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">支持动态加载</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>new&nbsp;router<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">，</span>promise<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">的原生支持等等。</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">迎合未来标准，吸纳其他框架的优点，值得期待，不过同时要学习的东西也更多了</span> (ES&nbsp;next<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span>TS<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span>Rx<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">等）</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参考：</span></p>
<p><a href="http://www.tuicool.com/articles/ymmq2mf"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">tuicool</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">articles</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ymmq</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">2</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">mf</span></a></p>
<p><a href="http://www.cnblogs.eom/laixiangran/p/4938732.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">cnblogs</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">eom</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">laixiangran</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">p</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/4938732</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.html</span></a></p>
<p class="43"><strong><em>综合问题</em></strong></p>
<p class="46">二百一十、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">请列举你知道的前端框架？常用的前端开发工具？</span> <span style="font-family: 华文黑体">开发过哪些应用和组件？</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;前端框架</p>
<p>bootstrap/jQuery/zepto/backbone/AngularJS/vue.js/React/</p>
<p>React&nbsp;Native/小程序</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 微软雅黑">前端开发工具</span> gulp/webpack/git/svn/npm/linux </p>
<p class="45">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">架构工具</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">：</span>bower<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">npm</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">yeoman</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">gulp</span><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">、</span><span style="font-family: Arial">webpack</span></p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;应用和组件</p>
<p>根据自己做的项目对答</p>
<p class="46">二百一十一、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">项目测试没问题。但是放到线上就有问题了，你是怎么分析解决的？</span></strong></p>
<p>可能的原因：</p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;后端原因：后端接口，后端服务器</p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;域名、<span style="text-decoration: underline">IP</span>和路径问题</p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;网络环境问题</p>
<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;线上库、框架、工具的版本和本地不一致问题</p>
<p class="45">(5)&nbsp;线上和本地数据资源不一致问题</p>
<p class="45">(6)&nbsp;程序<span style="text-decoration: underline">bug</span></p>
<p class="46">二百一十二、&nbsp;ES<strong>6</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">里面你用过什么？</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">1)&nbsp;块作用域<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span>let</p>
<p class="45">2)&nbsp;衡量<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span>const</p>
<p class="45">3)&nbsp;解构数组<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span>Array&nbsp;Destructuring</p>
<p class="45">4)&nbsp;解构对象<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span>Object&nbsp;Destructuring</p>
<p class="45">5)&nbsp;模板字符串<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">一</span>Template&nbsp;Strings</p>
<p class="45">6)&nbsp;展开操作符</p>
<p class="45">7)&nbsp;剩余操作符</p>
<p class="45">8)&nbsp;解构参数</p>
<p class="45">9)&nbsp;箭头函数</p>
<p class="45">10)&nbsp;对象表达式</p>
<p class="45">11)&nbsp;对象属性名</p>
<p class="45">12)&nbsp;对比两个值是否相等</p>
<p class="45">13)&nbsp;把对象的值复制到另一个对象里</p>
<p class="45">14)&nbsp;设置对象的prototype</p>
<p class="45">15)&nbsp;__<span style="text-decoration: underline">proto</span>__</p>
<p class="45">16)&nbsp;supper</p>
<p class="45">17)&nbsp;迭代器</p>
<p class="45">18)&nbsp;<span style="text-decoration: underline">class</span>&nbsp;类</p>
<p class="45">19)&nbsp;get&nbsp;set</p>
<p class="45">20)&nbsp;静态方法</p>
<p class="45">21)&nbsp;继承</p>
<p class="45">22)&nbsp;模块化</p>
<p>细节参见：<a href="http://es6.ruanyifeng.com/"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">es</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">6.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">ruanyifeng</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span></a></p>
<p class="46">二百一十三、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">如何管理团队？</span></strong></p>
<p class="45">(1)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">区分技术和管理角色在意识上的差异</span></p>
<p class="45">(2)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">时间管理</span></p>
<p class="45">(3)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">同时管理自己和其他人的代码</span></p>
<p class="45">(4)&nbsp;<span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">赢得团队的尊敬</span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">详细参见：</span><a href="http://www.t262.com/read/187780.html"><span style="text-decoration: underline">http</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">://</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">www</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">t</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">262.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">com</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">read</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">/187780</span><span style="text-decoration: underline">.html</span></a></p>
<p class="46">二百一十四、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你做过的你负责的最难的数据交互模块是</span>?</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">根据自己做的项目对答。</span></p>
<p class="46">二百一十五、&nbsp;<strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你平时写过什么业务逻辑？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">根据自己做的项目对答。</span></p>
<p class="46">二百一十六、&nbsp;<strong>在项目开发过程中</strong><strong><span style="font-family: 华文黑体">你负责的具体是什么模块？</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">根据自己做的项目对答。</span></p>
<p class="46">二百一十七、&nbsp;<strong>如果需要你加班，你会加吗，抵触吗？</strong></p>
<p>其实你肯定抵触，但你肯定要回答如果项目需要肯定会加</p>
<p class="46">二百一十八、&nbsp;<strong>一个小项目让你自己负责搭建底层一些架构，你能胜任吗？</strong></p>
<p>例：我肯定愿意尝试，并做到最优的选择方案出来</p>
<p class="46">二百一十九、&nbsp;<strong>如果项目拖太久，你情绪低落或者厌烦了怎么调节？</strong></p>
<p>例：你结合自身挑着好听的说就行，就像聊天</p>
<p class="46">二百二十、&nbsp;<strong>你建议自己造轮子，还是利用开源的轮子？</strong></p>
<p><span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">例：根据实际情况而定，如果开源完全满足</span> <span style="font-family: 方正宋黑简体">可以自己二次开发就好，大大缩短开发周期如果实在没有契合度很高的，可以花费几个工作日尝试造轮。</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p class="46"><strong>注：</strong></p>
<p>开放性问题（一般面试中我们都避免不了），这些问题往往决定你是否最终被录用或者等到终轮面试，技术点回答错了不要紧，人脑不是机器，是可以恶补的。但如果你没有思想和独到的思路，基础挖的再深，可能也打动不了面试官，因为比你基础好的一大堆，但每个人的个性思想却是不同的，因此我们除了在学会知识点的基础上，还要懂得一些为人处事，注意我们平时的言行举止，不要因小失大；</p></div>

### border-width为什么不支持百分比？
因为border没有继承性,如果使用百分比,那么就没有参考对象,浏览器解析就不知道百分数乘以谁来确定边框的宽度,所以只能用指定的值得大小来确定.
